# hep-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Dynamical Causal Horizons and the Quarkonium Flow Paradox](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24623)
*Yi Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种新的几何机制来解释重夸克偶素（heavy quarkonia）在相对论性核-核碰撞中的逐级压制现象，认为压制由初始碎裂阶段产生的极端时空几何决定，而非传统的热化夸克-胶子等离子体（Quark-Gluon Plasma）连续散射过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，重夸克偶素在超相对论性核-核碰撞中的逐级压制被解释为热化夸克-胶子等离子体（Quark-Gluon Plasma）存在的证据。然而，底偶素（bottomonium）同时观测到的消失椭圆流（elliptic flow, v₂ ≈ 0）与宏观输运模型固有的路径长度依赖性相矛盾，这促使研究者寻找新的解释框架。

Method: 研究者提出了一种几何解决方案：夸克偶素压制由初始碎裂阶段产生的极端时空几何决定。通过将底偶素（Υ）家族作为原始量子标尺，证明解离是在最早时刻（τ ≲ 0.1 fm/c）确定的因果事件。该框架利用动态霍金-安鲁（Hawking-Unruh）因果视界，当内禀束缚态半径超过局部安鲁视界（r_{nS} > r_H）时，重夸克对发生因果解耦。

Result: 该框架产生了一个单尺度解析核修正因子（nuclear modification factor）R_{AA} = exp[-κr_{nS} (N_{part}^{1/3} - N_{pp}^{1/3})]，无需逐态调参即可自然地重现Pb+Pb碰撞中观测到的压制层次。由于瞬时标量解耦保留了原始动量各向同性，运动学独立性和v₂ ≈ 0成为稳健的几何预期。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一个可检验的机制，将亚原子碎裂与因果事件视界联系起来。夸克偶素压制由初始碎裂阶段的极端时空几何决定，而非连续的部分子散射过程，这解释了同时观测到的压制层次和消失椭圆流现象。

Abstract: The sequential suppression of heavy quarkonia in ultra-relativistic $A+A$ collisions is conventionally interpreted as evidence of a thermalized Quark-Gluon Plasma. However, the simultaneous observation of vanishing elliptic flow ($v_2 \approx 0$) for bottomonium contradicts the path-length dependence inherent in macroscopic transport models. We propose a geometric resolution: quarkonium suppression is governed by the extreme spacetime geometry generated during initial fragmentation, rather than continuous late-stage partonic scattering. The intense color string tension induces extreme local deceleration, giving rise to a dynamical Hawking-Unruh causal horizon. By employing the bottomonium ($Υ$) family as pristine quantum rulers, we demonstrate that dissociation is a causal event determined at the earliest moments ($τ\lesssim 0.1$ fm/$c$). The dynamical horizon restricts the maximum causal range over which the evolving wave packet can maintain quantum coherence. When the intrinsic bound-state radius exceeds the local Unruh horizon ($r_{nS} > r_H$), the heavy quark pair is causally decoupled. This framework yields a single-scale analytical nuclear modification factor $R_{AA} = \exp[-κr_{nS} (N_{\text{part}}^{1/3} - N_{pp}^{1/3})]$, which naturally reproduces the suppression hierarchy observed in Pb+Pb collisions without state-by-state tuning. Crucially, because this instantaneous scalar decoupling preserves primordial momentum isotropy, kinematic independence and $v_2 \approx 0$ emerge as robust geometric expectations, providing a testable mechanism that bridges subatomic fragmentation and causal event horizons.

</details>


### [2] [Cogenesis of visible and dark matter in type-I Dirac seesaw](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24693)
*Debasish Borah,Partha Kumar Paul,Narendra Sahu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于I型狄拉克跷跷板机制的新型共生成框架，通过矢量费米子的非平衡衰变同时产生可见和暗物质区的不对称性，实现了重子不对称和暗物质遗迹的共生成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在通过扩展最小I型狄拉克跷跷板机制，建立一个统一框架同时解释宇宙中的重子不对称性和暗物质（DM）遗迹。传统模型通常分别处理这两个问题，而该框架试图在单一机制下实现二者的共生成（cogenesis）。

Method: 方法基于扩展的I型狄拉克跷跷板（Dirac seesaw）机制，在原有三个重矢量费米子（N）、单态标量（η）和标准模型（SM）中微子右旋分量（ν_R）的基础上，引入了狄拉克费米子暗物质（χ）及其较重的标量伴子（φ）。通过矢量费米子的非平衡衰变（out-of-equilibrium decays）同时产生可见区和暗物质区的不对称性。

Result: 研究发现成功的共生成可以在暗物质质量范围100 MeV ≲ m_χ ≲ 39 TeV内实现。下界源于对称暗物质组分在大爆炸核合成（BBN）时期前有效湮灭的要求，上界则由不对称暗物质的幺正性约束（unitarity constraints）设定。该模型可通过暗物质、中微子、宇宙微波背景（CMB）和引力波（GW）等多种观测手段进行检验。

Conclusion: 该框架成功实现了重子不对称和暗物质遗迹的共生成，为统一解释宇宙中物质-反物质不对称性和暗物质起源提供了可行方案。多区不对称性生成及其相互洗脱过程提供了丰富的动力学，同时保持了模型在不同观测领域的可检验性。

Abstract: We propose a novel cogenesis framework based on the type-I Dirac seesaw mechanism. The minimal type-I Dirac seesaw with three heavy vector like fermions $(N)$, one singlet scalar $(η)$ and the right-handed counterparts $(ν_R)$ of the Standard Model (SM) neutrinos is extended to include a Dirac fermion dark matter (DM) $(χ)$ and its heavier scalar companion ($φ$). The out-of-equilibrium decays of the vector-like fermion generate asymmetries simultaneously in the visible sector, through decay channels involving $(ν_R,η)$ or lepton, Higgs doublets in the SM, and in the dark sector via decaying into $(χ,φ)$. The resulting lepton asymmetry is partially converted into the observed baryon asymmetry by electroweak sphaleron processes, while the dark-sector asymmetry survives to constitute the present-day asymmetric DM relic. The generation of asymmetries in multiple sectors and their mutual washouts provide rich dynamics while also keeping the model testable at different observations involving DM, neutrinos, cosmic microwave background (CMB), as well as gravitational waves (GW). We find that successful cogenesis can be realized for DM masses in the range $100~\mathrm{MeV} \lesssim m_χ\lesssim 39~\mathrm{TeV}$. The lower bound arises from the requirement that the symmetric component of DM annihilates efficiently before the big bang nucleosynthesis (BBN) epoch, while the upper bound is set by unitarity constraints on the asymmetric DM.

</details>


### [3] [$DD^*$ correlation functions in deciphering the nature of $T_{cc}(3875)^+$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24980)
*Duo-Lun Ge,Zhi-Wei Liu,Li-Sheng Geng*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究评估了Tcc(3875)+作为分子态与分子-紧致混合态两种假设下的D*-D散射长度和femtoscopic关联函数，发现虽然两种场景产生相似的质谱线形，但其关联函数存在显著差异，表明femtoscopy可作为区分近阈强相互作用机制的有效探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解近阈强相互作用对于区分重味谱学中的强子分子态和紧致多夸克态至关重要。Tcc(3875)+作为双重粲四夸克候选者，因其非常接近D*-D阈值而成为关键基准。近期研究报道的相互作用模糊性进一步推动了本研究的开展。

Method: 研究评估了Tcc(3875)+作为分子态和分子-紧致混合态两种假设下的D*-D散射长度和femtoscopic关联函数。分析基于典型LHC产生的粒子发射源条件，比较了两种场景的理论预测。

Result: 虽然两种场景产生相似的质谱线形，但其对应的femtoscopic关联函数存在显著差异，在典型LHC粒子发射源条件下仍保持明显可区分性。这表明femtoscopy能够敏感地探测Tcc(3875)+的近阈动力学。

Conclusion: femtoscopy可作为敏感且互补的探针，用于研究Tcc(3875)+的近阈动力学，为未来LHC的femtoscopy测量提供重要的理论参考。该方法有助于澄清该双重粲四夸克候选者的内部结构本质。

Abstract: Understanding near-threshold strong interactions is essential for disentangling hadronic molecules and compact multiquark states in heavy-flavor spectroscopy. In this context, the doubly charmed tetraquark candidate $T_{cc}(3875)^+$ serves as a critical benchmark because it lies very close to the $D^*$-$D$ thresholds. Motivated by the interaction ambiguity reported recently [\href{https://doi.org/10.1103/kd4s-9rzr}{Phys.Rev.D 113, L031505 (2026)}], we evaluate the $D^*$-$D$ scattering lengths and femtoscopic correlation functions for the molecular and molecule-compact admixture assignments of the $T_{cc}(3875)^+$. We show that, although these scenarios yield similar invariant-mass line shapes, their corresponding femtoscopic correlation functions differ markedly and remain clearly distinguishable for typical particle-emitting sources created at the LHC. Our results indicate that femtoscopy can serve as a sensitive and complementary probe of the near-threshold dynamics of $T_{cc}(3875)^+$, providing vital theoretical references for future LHC femtoscopy measurements.

</details>


### [4] [$2^{++}$ Light Tensor Hybrid Meson from QCD Laplace Sum Rules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25059)
*Jason Ho,Robin Kleiv,Siyuan Li,Stephan Narison,Tom Steele,Davidson Rabetiarivony*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过QCD拉普拉斯求和规则（Laplace Sum Rules）分析了轻张量（J^PC=2^{++}）混杂介子的质量和耦合常数，包含了次领头阶（NLO）微扰修正和高达六维（D=6）的非微扰凝聚贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于利用改进的QCD求和规则方法精确计算轻张量混杂介子的质量和耦合常数，以探索实验观测到的f_2(1950)和f'_2(2010)粒子中可能的混杂介子（\bar qqg）成分。

Method: 采用QCD拉普拉斯求和规则方法，包含了次领头阶（NLO）微扰修正和高达六维（D=6）的非微扰凝聚贡献，同时考虑了手征极限下凝聚项带来的NLO领头对数修正。

Result: 获得轻张量混杂介子质量M_{2^+} = (2038±190) MeV，相对较小的耦合常数f_{2^+} = (10.5±2.9) MeV（以f_π=93 MeV归一化），并首次在NLO精度下计算出张量混杂拓扑荷Π_{qg}(0) = (2.41±0.43)×10^{-4} GeV^6。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明f_2(1950)和/或f'_2(2010)可能具有显著的\bar qqg混杂成分，同时计算出的张量混杂拓扑荷为格点QCD或低能定理（LET）提供了可检验的理论预言。

Abstract: We present an analysis of the light tensor ($J^{PC}=2^{++}$) hybrid meson mass and coupling from QCD Laplace Sum Rules where the next-to-leading order (NLO) perturbative (PT) corrections and the contributions of the non-perturbative (NP) condensates up to dimension-six ($D=6$) are included. NLO leading-logarithms corrections due to the condensates which contribute in the chiral limit are considered. We obtain the mass $M_{2^+}= (2038\pm 190)$ MeV and a relatively small coupling $f_{2^+}=(10.5\pm 2.9)$ MeV normalized as $f_π=93$ MeV. Our results suggest that the $f_2(1950)$ or/and the $f'_2(2010)$ may have a sizeable $\bar qqg$ hybrid component. We also compute the tensor hybrid topological charge (value of the two-point function at zero momentum) and find (for the first time) at NLO: $Π_{qg}(0)=(2.41\pm 0.43) \times 10^{-4}{\rm GeV}^6$ which could be checked from some lattice QCD or/and low energy theorems (LET).

</details>


### [5] [Deeply virtual meson production at HERA and at the EIC within the Color Glass Condensate EFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25363)
*Renaud Boussarie,Luigi Delle Rose,Michael Fucilla,Alessandro Papa,Lech Szymanowski,Samuel Wallon*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究在色玻璃凝聚体（Color Glass Condensate）框架下，推导了深度虚介子产生（DVMP）过程在扭度-3（twist-3）精度下的所有螺旋度振幅的紧凑表达式，并进行了唯象分析。研究结合了次领头阶（NLO）修正，提供了迄今最精确的理论描述，并与HERA数据对比，预测了未来电子-离子对撞机（EIC）的电子-铅碰撞结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究延续先前对扭度-3精度下深度虚介子产生（Deeply Virtual Meson Production, DVMP）的工作，旨在推导所有螺旋度振幅（helicity amplitudes）的紧凑表达式。研究动机在于通过纳入小x演化（small-x evolution）和次领头阶（next-to-leading order）修正，提供对这些可观测量最精确的理论描述。

Method: 在色玻璃凝聚体（Color Glass Condensate, CGC）框架下，研究推导了所有螺旋度振幅的紧凑表达式。小x演化通过数值求解跑动耦合与共线改进的Balitsky-Kovchegov（BK）和Balitsky-Fadin-Kuraev-Lipatov（BFKL）方程实现，并以McLerran-Venugopalan（MV）模型作为初始条件。研究还捕捉了相关的次领头阶（NLO）修正子集。

Result: 研究对螺旋度振幅比$\mathcal{A}^{11}/\mathcal{A}^{00}$和自旋密度矩阵元$r_{00}^{04}$进行了唯象分析。结果与HERA实验数据进行了对比，并预测了未来电子-离子对撞机（Electron-Ion Collider, EIC）中电子-铅碰撞的结果。研究还讨论了低光子虚度下的非线性效应以及与轻矢量介子分布振幅（distribution amplitudes）相关的真正高扭度（higher-twist）贡献的作用。

Conclusion: 该研究通过纳入次领头阶修正，提供了对深度虚介子产生过程可观测量迄今最精确的理论描述。研究不仅验证了理论框架与HERA数据的一致性，还为未来电子-离子对撞机实验提供了预测。分析揭示了低光子虚度下非线性效应的重要性，以及高福克态（higher-Fock-state）组分对真正高扭度贡献的关键作用。

Abstract: Continuing our previous study of Deeply Virtual Meson Production (DVMP) at twist-3 accuracy, we derive compact expressions for all helicity amplitudes. We perform a phenomenological analysis of the helicity-amplitude ratio $\mathcal{A}^{11}/\mathcal{A}^{00}$ and of the spin-density matrix element $r_{00}^{04}$ within the Color Glass Condensate framework. Small-$x$ evolution is incorporated by numerically solving the running-coupling-and-collinearly-improved Balitsky-Kovchegov and Balitsky-Fadin-Kuraev-Lipatov equations with the McLerran-Venugopalan model as the initial condition. By capturing a relevant subset of next-to-leading order corrections, we provide the most theoretically accurate description of these observables to date. Our results are compared to HERA data, and predictions are presented for electron-lead collisions at the future Electron-Ion Collider. We discuss the impact of non-linear effects at low photon virtuality and the role of genuine higher-twist contributions associated with light vector meson distribution amplitudes, corresponding to higher-Fock-state components of the projectile.

</details>


### [6] [Constraining the heavy leptophilic neutral gauge bosons through the $Z\to\ell^+\ell^-$, $W^\pm\to\ell^\pmν_\ell$, and $h\to\ell^+\ell^-$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25589)
*Bibhabasu De,Amitabha Dey*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有味道特异性轻子亲和耦合（flavor-specific leptophilic couplings）的中性规范玻色子Z'，发现现有实验约束在重质量区域（≥1 TeV）较为宽松，但通过电弱规范玻色子和希格斯粒子的轻子衰变模式的圈图修正，可以施加更强的排除限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有味道特异性轻子亲和耦合（flavor-specific leptophilic couplings）的中性规范玻色子Z'的假设可能性，这类新物理（New Physics）相互作用在重质量区域（特别是≥1 TeV）的实验约束相对宽松，需要寻找新的探测方法。

Method: 利用轻子亲和Z'存在时，电弱规范玻色子和希格斯粒子的轻子衰变模式在圈图水平（loop level）上的修正，基于现有相应衰变宽度的上限约束进行分析。

Result: 研究发现，通过分析轻子衰变模式的圈图修正，可以对重质量Z'的相互作用施加比直接探测更强的排除限制（stronger exclusion limits），未来相关衰变通道的更新数据可与提议的轻子对撞机互补使用。

Conclusion: 轻子衰变宽度的圈图修正为探测重质量轻子亲和Z'提供了有效方法，未来衰变通道数据与轻子对撞机实验的互补可以探测TeV尺度及更高能标的更弱轻子亲和新物理相互作用。

Abstract: We consider the hypothetical possibility of neutral gauge bosons~($Z^\prime$) with flavor-specific leptophilic couplings. For such {\it New Physics}~(NP) interactions, the current experimental constraints are much relaxed in the heavy mass regime, particularly for masses $\geq \mathcal{O}(1)$ TeV. However, in the presence of a leptophilic $Z^\prime$, leptonic decay modes of the electroweak gauge bosons and Higgs can be corrected at the loop level. Using the existing upper bounds on the corresponding decay widths, we find that one can impose stronger exclusion limits on the interactions of a heavy $Z^\prime$. Future updates on the aforesaid decay channels can be used in complementarity with the proposed lepton colliders to probe even weaker leptophilic NP interactions at the TeV scale and beyond.

</details>


### [7] [UV-complete and stable Quintom Dark Energy models in the light of DESI DR2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24685)
*Fotis Koutroulis*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出将Quintom暗能量模型嵌入5D非微扰规范-希格斯统一框架，通过高维规范场在4D边界投影产生物理和幽灵标量场，自然实现暗能量状态方程穿越宇宙常数边界，且无需精细调节即可拟合DESI观测数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准Quintom暗能量模型通常需要精细调节才能实现状态方程穿越宇宙常数边界。本文旨在为Quintom暗能量提供一个自然的紫外完备（UV completion）框架，避免基本理论中的不稳定性问题。

Method: 采用5D各向异性轨道格点（anisotropic orbifold lattice）上的非微扰规范-希格斯统一（NPGHU）模型，其中5D SU(2)规范场在4D边界投影为复标量场和U(1)规范场，构成动力学暗能量部分，而标准模型和暗物质保持四维局域化。

Result: 该构造产生的4D有效作用量是一个修正的Quintom模型，其背景状态方程可自然实现Quintom-B行为。来自大质量规范幽灵（massive gauge ghost）的关键贡献使得模型无需精细调节即可极好地拟合DESI数据，且在低能截断Λ≈O(10)H₀的最自然参数区域下，模型在线性扰动和真空衰变方面保持稳健。

Conclusion: NPGHU框架为Quintom暗能量提供了一个自然且可预测的基本理论嵌入方案，该方案避免了基本幽灵不稳定性，无势能项，并具有与近似洛伦兹不变性相关的有限低能截断，确保了有效理论的一致性。

Abstract: We propose that Quintom dark energy, the simplest framework allowing crossing of the cosmological-constant boundary, admits a natural UV completion in a 5D anisotropic orbifold lattice: the Non-Perturbative Gauge-Higgs Unification (NPGHU) model. In this setup, a bulk 5D SU(2) gauge field projects on the 4D boundary to a complex scalar and a U(1) gauge field, identified with the dynamical dark-energy sector, while the Standard Model and dark matter remain localized in four dimensions. At late times, bulk-induced dimension-6 higher-derivative operators generate both physical and phantom scalar and gauge degrees of freedom. We show that the resulting 4D effective action is a modified Quintom model whose background equation of state can naturally realize Quintom-B behavior. A crucial contribution arises from the massive gauge ghost, allowing an excellent fit to DESI data with negligible fine-tuning, unlike standard Quintom scenarios. We further show that the inherited properties of the NPGHU construction e.g. absence of fundamental ghost instabilities, absence of potential terms and a finite low-energy cutoff $Λ$ associated with approximate Lorentz invariance, play a central role in the consistency of the effective theory under linear perturbations and vacuum decay. For the most natural regime, $Λ\approx {\cal O}(10)H_0$, the model remains robust despite the presence of IR phantom modes. Our results provide a natural and predictive framework in which Quintom dark energy can be consistently embedded in a fundamental theory.

</details>


### [8] [Quantum field-theoretic framework for neutrino decoherence from scattering in a medium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25344)
*Konstantin Stankevich,Alexander Studenikin,Maksim Vyalkov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文建立了一个用于描述中微子在介质中演化的量子场论框架，重点研究中微子与费米子散射诱导的量子退相干效应。该模型超越了假定固定中微子动量的标准处理方法，将退相干参数与散射截面明确关联，为中微子量子退相干的理论预测与实验约束提供了桥梁。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于发展中微子在介质中演化的量子场论描述，特别关注中微子与费米子散射诱导的量子退相干效应。现有标准处理方法通常假定中微子动量固定，需要超越这一限制以更精确描述动量变化过程。

Method: 方法包括推导一个广义林德布拉德主方程（generalized Lindblad master equation），该方程考虑了中微子动量变化的跃迁过程。理论框架将退相干参数与散射截面明确关联，并将该形式体系应用于三种情景：中微子与电子散射、通过非标准相互作用（NSI）与质子和中子散射、以及与暗物质费米子散射。

Result: 研究结果表明，退相干效应能够显著改变中微子振荡模式。该框架为超出标准模型（Standard Model）的物理提供了新的探测手段，特别是在非标准相互作用和暗物质费米子散射等情景中。

Conclusion: 结论是所发展的理论框架成功连接了中微子退相干参数与散射截面，为中微子量子退相干的理论预测与实验约束建立了桥梁。该模型超越了固定动量的标准处理方法，为探测超出标准模型的物理提供了新途径。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework for quantum field description of neutrino evolution in a medium, with a focus on quantum decoherence induced by neutrino scattering on fermions. By deriving a generalized Lindblad master equation that accounts for neutrino momentum-changing transitions, we go beyond the standard treatment that assumes fixed neutrino momentum. Our model explicitly connects decoherence parameters to scattering cross sections, offering a bridge between theoretical predictions and experimental constraints on neutrino quantum decoherence. We apply the developed formalism to several scenarios: 1) neutrino scattering on electrons, 2) neutrino scattering on protons and neutrons through non-standard interactions (NSI), 3) neutrino scattering on dark matter fermions. The obtained results demonstrate that decoherence effects can significantly alter neutrino oscillation patterns and provide a new probe for physics beyond the Standard Model.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扭度-3横向自旋依赖核子结构函数g₂在高能过程中出现，其与夸克-胶子关联的联系可解释为横向极化核子内非极化夸克所受的平均横向色洛伦兹力。

Method: 采用基矢光前量子化方法，用量子色动力学输入对角化光前哈密顿量获得光前波函数，将结果演化到共同尺度5 GeV²，并在动量空间和冲击参数空间分别给出相应形状因子和横向力分量。

Result: 在向前极限下提取了扭度-3约化矩阵元d₂，其结果与其他理论计算和实验测定具有可比性，为横向极化深度非弹性散射中的西弗斯不对称性提供了补充视角。

Abstract: The twist-3 transverse spin--dependent nucleon structure function $g_2$ arises in high-energy processes involving a transversely polarized nucleon. Its connection to quark--gluon correlations allows for an interpretation in terms of the average transverse color Lorentz force acting on unpolarized quarks inside a transversely polarized nucleon. In this work, we investigate this force using light-front wave functions obtained by diagonalizing the light-front Hamiltonian with quantum chromodynamics inputs within the Basis Light-front Quantization approach. We evolve our results to a common scale of $5~\mathrm{GeV}^2$ and present the corresponding form factors in momentum space as well as the transverse force components in impact-parameter space. These distributions provide a complementary perspective on the Sivers asymmetry in transversely polarized deep-inelastic scattering. In the forward limit, we extract the twist-3 reduced matrix element $d_2$, and our results are found to be comparable with those from other theoretical calculations and experimental determinations.

### [10] [$θ$ Angle and Axial Anomaly in Holographic QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25729)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从全息对偶（holographic duality）的底层构建角度，几何化地描述QCD中的θ-真空结构和U(1)_A轴反常现象，为理解η'介子质量与反常的关系提供新的理论框架。

Method: 采用五维全息描述方法，通过高维规范场（higher-dimensional gauge field）几何化地呈现多分支θ-真空结构，利用Stückelberg耦合实现轴反常，该耦合与Chern-Simons项（Chern-Simons term）对偶。

Result: 在该框架中，η'介子作为体涨落（bulk fluctuations）的零模（zero mode）出现，其质量来源于反常诱导的Stückelberg项，自然地再现了η'质量与杨-米尔斯拓扑敏感性（Yang-Mills topological susceptibility）之间的Witten-Veneziano关系。

Conclusion: 该构建为反常对η'质量的贡献提供了透明的全息推导，成功地将θ-真空结构和U(1)_A反常纳入统一的五维全息框架，验证了Witten-Veneziano关系在全息对偶中的自然实现。

Abstract: We present a bottom-up holographic description of the QCD $θ$-vacuum and the $U(1)_A$ anomaly in five dimensions. The multi-branched $θ$-vacuum structure emerges geometrically from a higher-dimensional gauge field, while the axial anomaly is realized through a Stückelberg coupling that is dual to a Chern-Simons term. In this framework, the $η'$ meson appears as a zero mode of bulk fluctuations, and its mass arises from the anomaly-induced Stückelberg term. The construction provides a transparent holographic derivation of the anomaly contribution to the $η'$ mass and naturally reproduces the Witten-Veneziano relation between the $η'$ mass and the Yang-Mills topological susceptibility.

### [11] [Bound states of anyons: a geometric quantization approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24701)
*Qingchen Li,Pavel A. Nosov,Taige Wang,Eslam Khalaf*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种在任意子希尔伯特空间内研究任意子束缚的可控、可扩展方法，应用于ν=1/3 Laughlin态的准空穴，发现纯排斥相互作用下仍能形成束缚态，这是由Berry相位效应驱动的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 任意子相互作用及其可能的束缚问题在分数量子霍尔态物理中至关重要。需要一种在任意子希尔伯特空间内研究任意子束缚的可控、可扩展方法。

Method: 引入了一种完全在任意子希尔伯特空间内工作的理论框架，其特征是有效势（捕获经典任意子构型的静电能量）和Kähler势（同时编码任意子Berry相位及其希尔伯特空间结构）。通过Kähler流形上的几何量子化（geometric quantization）形式构建任意子哈密顿量，可在少任意子希尔伯特空间中精确对角化。

Result: 应用于ν=1/3 Laughlin态准空穴时发现：当屏蔽长度与磁长度相当或更小时，Laughlin准空穴形成束缚态，尽管电子-电子相互作用和准空穴静电势都是纯排斥的。束缚态形成是Berry相位效应驱动的，由准空穴密度分布在ℓ_B尺度上的振荡引起。随着屏蔽长度减小，观察到多个准空穴的相序列：自由e/3任意子、配对2e/3束缚态、三任意子电荷-e团簇及更大的复合物。

Conclusion: 该方法为研究任意子束缚提供了可靠框架，揭示了Berry相位在任意子束缚中的关键作用。研究结果对量子霍尔系统的电荷成像实验和分数量子反常霍尔材料中巡游任意子相的相图具有重要启示。

Abstract: The question of anyon interactions and their possible binding plays a key role in the physics of fractional quantum Hall states. Here, we introduce a controlled and scalable approach to study anyon binding by working entirely within the Hilbert space of anyons. The resulting theory is characterized by an effective potential, which captures the electrostatic energy of classical anyon configurations, and a Kähler potential, which simultaneously encodes the anyon Berry phase and the structure of their Hilbert space; both quantities are readily computed using Monte Carlo methods for large systems, enabling reliable extrapolation to the thermodynamic limit. By applying the formalism of geometric quantization on Kähler manifolds, we construct the anyon Hamiltonian, which can be exactly diagonalized in the few-anyon Hilbert space. Applying our approach to the quasiholes of the $ν=1/3$ Laughlin state with screened Coulomb interaction, we find that Laughlin quasiholes form bound states for screening lengths comparable or smaller than the magnetic length. Remarkably, binding occurs despite both the bare electron-electron interaction and the quasihole electrostatic potential being purely repulsive. The bound-state formation is a Berry phase effect, driven by oscillations in the quasihole density profile on the $\ell_B$ scale that are invisible in the quasihole electrostatic potential alone. For multiple quasiholes, we identify a sequence of phases as the screening length is reduced: free $e/3$ anyons, paired $2e/3$ bound states, three-anyon charge-$e$ clusters, and larger composite objects. Finally, we discuss possible signatures in charge imaging experiments on quantum Hall systems and the relevance to the phase diagram of itinerant anyon phases in fractional quantum anomalous Hall materials.

</details>


### [12] [Topological properties of gapless phases in an interacting spinful wire](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24831)
*Polina Matveeva,Dmitri Gutman,Sam T. Carr*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究在具有自旋-电荷分离的相互作用自旋模型中探索无能隙相（gapless phases）的拓扑性质，重点关注ℤ₂对称性破缺相之间的边界，发现了两种拓扑非平庸的无能隙态：拓扑Luther-Emery液体和拓扑Mott绝缘体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索相互作用系统中无能隙相的拓扑性质，特别关注具有自旋-电荷分离的模型在ℤ₂对称性破缺相边界处的拓扑特征。传统上，无能隙相缺乏局域序参量，难以用平均场理论描述，但其拓扑性质值得深入研究。

Method: 研究方法聚焦于分析相互作用自旋模型在ℤ₂对称性破缺相之间的无能隙边界。通过研究拓扑非平庸绝缘体与平庸绝缘体边界处的物理，识别出两种不同的拓扑无能隙态，并将其与无相互作用的拓扑金属相建立绝热连接。

Result: 研究发现两种拓扑非平庸的无能隙态：拓扑Luther-Emery液体（topological Luther-Emery liquid）和拓扑Mott绝缘体（topological Mott insulator）。前者具有无能隙电荷激发和携带分数自旋的拓扑边缘模，后者具有无能隙自旋激发和携带分数电荷的边缘态。这些相互作用无能隙相可绝热连接到无相互作用的拓扑金属相。

Conclusion: 结论表明，即使缺乏局域序参量和平均场描述，相互作用无能隙相仍可展现丰富的拓扑结构。拓扑Luther-Emery液体和拓扑Mott绝缘体分别通过分数自旋和分数电荷的边缘态体现其拓扑性质，且与无相互作用的拓扑金属相存在绝热连接，揭示了相互作用系统中拓扑相的新颖特征。

Abstract: We study topology in gapless phases of an interacting spinful model with spin-charge separation. We focus on the gapless boundaries between $\mathbb{Z}_2$ symmetry-breaking phases. We find two topologically non-trivial gapless states that occur at the boundary between a non-trivial and a trivial insulator. They correspond to topological Luther-Emery liquid and topological Mott insulator. The Luther-Emery liquid is characterized by gapless charge excitations and features topological edge modes that carry fractional spin, while the topological Mott insulator has gapless spin sector and features edge states that carry fractional charge. Surprisingly, even though there is no mean-field description of the interacting gapless phases, as there is no local order parameter, we show that they can be adiabatically connected to a non-interacting topological metal. This non-interacting state is a phase boundary between decoupled Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chains with the winding number $ν=2$ and chains with $ν=1$.

</details>


### [13] [Dynamical Response of the Kitaev Spin Liquid under Third-Nearest-Neighbor Heisenberg Interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24918)
*Chuan Chen,Jiucai Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了第三近邻海森堡相互作用（$J_3$）对Kitaev自旋液体（KSL）动力学性质的影响，发现$J_3$会诱导出类顺磁子集体模，并在临界值处引发量子相变，同时揭示了拉曼散射中物质马约拉纳费米子与visons激发的不同特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于越来越多的证据表明第三近邻海森堡相互作用（$J_3$）在候选Kitaev材料中的重要性。本文旨在探究$J_3$微扰下Kitaev自旋液体（KSL）的动力学性质，特别是其自旋动力学结构因子（DSF）和拉曼散射响应。

Method: 采用自洽的部分子平均场加随机相位近似（self-consistent parton mean-field plus random-phase approximation）框架，研究了$J_3$微扰对Kitaev自旋液体的影响。通过分析自旋动力学结构因子和进行微扰性拉曼计算，探索了系统的动力学特征。

Result: 研究发现$J_3$会在自旋动力学结构因子中诱导出相干、类顺磁子（paramagnon-like）的集体模，这些模与高能马约拉纳连续谱共存。随着$|J_3|$增大，这些模的软化预示着向磁有序的量子相变。拉曼计算显示，类Kitaev顶点仅探测巡游物质马约拉纳费米子，而类$J_3$顶点则同时包含物质马约拉纳和visons激发。

Conclusion: 该研究为$J_3$微扰Kitaev自旋液体的动力学特征提供了统一视角，有助于解释具有显著$J_3$相互作用的候选Kitaev材料的实验谱。研究发现磁有序在铁磁和反铁磁Kitaev模型中具有共同的临界$J_3$值，且有序态在四子格对偶变换下形成精确的对偶对。

Abstract: Motivated by growing evidence for the significance of the third-nearest-neighbor Heisenberg ($J_3$) interaction in candidate Kitaev materials, we investigate the dynamical properties of the Kitaev spin liquid (KSL) under a $J_3$ perturbation, focusing on its spin dynamical structure factor (DSF) and Raman scattering. Within a self-consistent parton mean-field plus random-phase approximation framework, we find that $J_3$ induces coherent, paramagnon-like collective modes that coexist with a high-energy Majorana continuum in the spin DSF. The softening of these modes with increasing $|J_3|$ signals a quantum phase transition to magnetic order. Remarkably, magnetic ordering sets in at a common critical $J_3$ for both ferromagnetic ($K<0$) and antiferromagnetic ($K>0$) Kitaev models, with the resulting ordered states forming exact dual pairs under a four-sublattice duality transformation that maps $(K,J_3) \rightarrow (-K,J_3)$. An external magnetic field further softens the preexisting paramagnon modes, thereby enhancing magnetic order. Perturbative Raman calculations show that while the Kitaev-like Raman vertex probes only itinerant matter Majorana fermions, the response from the $J_3$-like vertex features both matter Majoranas and visons. Four-vison excitations produce a sharp peak accompanied by a two-fermion continuum, whereas two-vison excitations yield a continuum closely resembling the single-matter-fermion density of states. These results provide a unified perspective on the dynamical signatures of $J_3$-perturbed KSL and are helpful for interpreting experimental spectra in candidate Kitaev materials with sizable $J_3$ interactions.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究采用量子色弦模型（quantum color string model）框架进行分析，通过比较理论计算结果与铜酸盐实验LDOS数据，识别了粒子-空穴对称性破缺（PHSB）效应。

Abstract: Scanning tunneling microscopy (STM) serves as a powerful pictorial tool for visualizing the local density of states (LDOS) of an individual stripe, which strongly intertwines with superconductivity in the underdoped cuprates. The exotic LDOS map patterns thus appear as the key to uncovering the mystery of the underlying microscopic mechanisms. With the quantum color string model framework, we reveal that the microscopic origin of the ubiquitous $4a_0\times4a_0$ plaquettes is closely related to spinon singlet pairs. Moreover, by comparing our data with LDOS of cuprates, we identify an effect of particle-hole symmetry breaking (PHSB): a $2a_0$ shift, which is confirmed in a longer stripe ($L=18$).Our work offers a fresh wavefunction-based perspective for interpreting STM signals in experiments and may advance the microscopic comprehension of high-$T_c$ cuprates.

### [15] [Structural and magnetic phases of topological kagome metal Fe$_3$Sn$_2$ under pressure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25271)
*S. Chattopadhyay,L. Thomarat,C. S. Ong,K. Kargeti,Lipika,J. -P. Rueff,L. Nataf,K. Manna,S. K. Panda,C. Shekhar,V. Balédent*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过高压实验与理论计算相结合，揭示了Kagome铁磁体Fe₃Sn₂在压力诱导下的结构相变与磁性演化，包括高自旋到低自旋转变以及丰富的压力-温度磁相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索压力对Kagome铁磁体Fe₃Sn₂晶体结构和磁性的影响，特别是压力如何通过耦合晶格、自旋态和相对论性磁相互作用来重塑磁性能量景观。

Method: 采用X射线衍射（X-ray diffraction）、X射线发射光谱（X-ray Emission Spectroscopy）、X射线磁圆二色性（X-ray Magnetic Circular Dichroism）等实验技术，并结合自旋极化密度泛函理论（spin-polarized density functional theory）计算。

Result: 在约20 GPa以上观察到结构相变，同时XES显示局域Fe磁矩显著减小，表明高自旋到低自旋转变。XMCD揭示了丰富的压力-温度磁相图：室温下共线铁磁相持续到结构相变，低温下倾斜磁构型在更高压力下保持稳定。理论计算表明压力增强了自旋-轨道驱动的磁各向异性和Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya相互作用。

Conclusion: 压力通过耦合晶格、自旋态和相对论性磁相互作用，重塑了Fe₃Sn₂的磁性能量景观，确立了静水压力作为调控Kagome材料磁各向异性和潜在拓扑相的有效控制参数。

Abstract: We investigate the pressure-induced evolution of crystal structure and magnetism in the kagome ferromagnet Fe$_3$Sn$_2$ by combining X-ray diffraction, X-ray Emission Spectroscopy, X-ray Magnetic Circular Dichroism, and spin-polarized density functional theory calculations. X-ray diffraction reveals a structural phase transition above $\sim$20~GPa, which coincides with a pronounced reduction of the local Fe magnetic moment evidenced by X-ray emission spectroscopy, indicating a high-spin to low-spin transition. While XES probes the amplitude of the local moment, XMCD provides direct information on the orientation of the ordered magnetic moments and uncovers a rich pressure--temperature magnetic phase diagram. At room temperature, a collinear ferromagnetic phase with moments aligned along the $c$ axis persists up to the structural transition. At low temperature, a tilted magnetic configuration remains stable to significantly higher pressures, while at intermediate temperatures pressure stabilizes the low-temperature magnetic phase at the expense of the high-temperature one. Spin-polarized first-principles calculations show that, although isotropic ferromagnetic exchange interactions remain robust under compression, pressure enhances spin--orbit--driven magnetic anisotropy and Dzyaloshinskii--Moriya interactions, favoring non-collinear magnetic configurations. Our results demonstrate that pressure reshapes the magnetic energy landscape of Fe$_3$Sn$_2$ by coupling lattice, spin state, and relativistic magnetic interactions, establishing hydrostatic pressure as an effective control parameter to engineer magnetic anisotropy and potentially topological phases in kagome materials.

</details>


### [16] [Flat band driven competing charge and spin instabilities in the altermagnet CrSb](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25317)
*A. Korshunov,M. Alkorta,C. -Y. Lim,F. Ballester,Cong Li,Zhilin Li,D. Chernyshov,A. Bosak,M. G. Vergniory,Ion Errea,S. Blanco-Canosa*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了铬化锑（CrSb）中动量空间电子局域化导致的平带物理，通过实验观测到电荷序与自旋序的强烈竞争，并发现了迄今为止最大的自旋-声子耦合效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动量空间电子波函数局域化（confinement of electronic wavefunctions in momentum space）可产生平电子带（flat electronic bands），其中动能淬灭（quenching of kinetic energy）增强态密度并放大相互作用效应，为涌现量子相（emergent quantum phases）提供理想条件。研究旨在探索平带物理如何介导自旋、电荷和晶格自由度之间的强纠缠。

Method: 研究通过实验观测铬化锑（CrSb）的布里渊区M点短程电荷序涨落（short-range charge-order fluctuations），分析其在尼尔温度（Neel temperature, TN）以上的行为。结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）解释电子态与声子支（phonon branch）的强耦合机制。

Result: 在TN以上观测到布里渊区M点q*=(1/2 0)的短程电荷序涨落，进入磁有序相后这些涨落消失，表明电荷序与自旋序的直接竞争。在TN处q*点的声子色散（phonon dispersion）出现显著的科恩类反常（Kohn-like anomaly），显示强电子-声子耦合（electron-phonon coupling）。TN以下交换伸缩（exchange striction）使相关软声子模（soft phonon mode）重整化约6 meV，这是迄今报道的最大自旋-声子耦合（spin-phonon coupling）。

Conclusion: 铬化锑（CrSb）凭借其化学简单结构和对称性保护的交替磁态（altermagnetic state），成为探索平电子带如何介导巨大自旋-声子耦合和竞争破缺对称性（competing broken symmetries）的理想模型平台。电荷序与自旋序参数之间的竞争，通过平带物理放大，驱动了观测到的声子反常及其在TN处的突变重构。

Abstract: The confinement of electronic wavefunctions in momentum space can give rise to flat electronic bands, where the quenching of kinetic energy enhances the density of states and amplifies interaction effects. Such conditions are fertile ground for emergent quantum phases, as spin, charge and lattice degrees of freedom become strongly entangled. In these regimes, subtle competitions between intertwined order parameters often dictate the macroscopic ground state, producing complex and sometimes unexpected collective behavior. Here we show that the altermagnet CrSb provides a realization of this scenario, and uncover short-range charge-order fluctuations at the M point of the Brillouin zone, q*=(1/2 0), persisting above the Neel temperature (TN). Remarkably, these fluctuations collapse upon entering the magnetically ordered phase, revealing a direct and robust competition between charge and spin order. At TN, the phonon dispersion at q* develops a pronounced Kohn-like anomaly, signaling strong electron-phonon coupling in the vicinity of the magnetic transition. Below TN, exchange striction dramatically renormalizes the associated soft phonon mode by approximately ~6 meV, the largest spin-phonon coupling ever reported. First-principles calculations attribute this behavior to a strong coupling between nearly dispersionless electronic states and a phonon branch that appears unstable at the harmonic level only when no magnetic order is considered, revealing the large sensitivity of the lattice to magnetic symmetry breaking. The competition between charge and spin order parameters, amplified by flat-band physics, drives the observed phonon anomaly and its abrupt reconstruction at TN. With its chemically simple structure and symmetry-protected altermagnetic state, CrSb emerges as a model platform to explore how flat electronic bands mediate giant spin-phonon coupling and competing broken symmetries.

### [17] [Stabilization of zigzag order in NiPS$_3$ via positive biquadratic interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25475)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已有广泛研究，但范德华反铁磁体NiPS₃的自旋哈密顿量（spin Hamiltonian）仍存在争议。虽然最近邻铁磁相互作用（J₁）和第三近邻反铁磁海森堡相互作用（J₃）已达成共识，但双二次交换项（biquadratic exchange term, B）的作用及其强度仍不确定。

Method: 采用密度泛函理论（density functional theory）计算，并提取双二次相互作用参数。在最小J₁-J₃-B模型中，使用最小增强自旋波理论（minimally augmented spin-wave theory）分析，并通过密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group）计算进一步验证参数。

Result: 计算得到正的双二次相互作用，其强度比B/J₃ ≈ 0.44。在J₁-J₃-B模型中，这些参数能自然地稳定锯齿形有序（zigzag ordering）。密度矩阵重整化群计算进一步证实提取的参数能合理描述基态。

Conclusion: 虽然完全确定NiPS₃的自旋哈密顿量仍需进一步研究，但本研究为其双二次相互作用提供了新的见解，表明该相互作用在稳定锯齿形基态有序中具有重要作用。

Abstract: Despite extensive research, the precise spin Hamiltonian of the van der Waals antiferromagnet NiPS$_3$ -- which hosts a zigzag-ordered ground state -- remains debated. While consensus has emerged on ferromagnetic nearest-neighbor ($J_1$) and antiferromagnetic third-nearest-neighbor ($J_3$) Heisenberg interactions, recent studies suggest a biquadratic ($B$) exchange term may also play a role, though its estimated magnitude varies widely. To address this controversy, we perform density functional theory calculations and extract a positive biquadratic interaction with $B/J_3 \approx 0.44$. Within the minimal $J_1$-$J_3$-$B$ model, we show that these parameters naturally stabilize zigzag ordering using minimally augmented spin-wave theory. Density-matrix renormalization group calculations further validate our extracted parameters as a reasonable description of the ground state. Although fully resolving the spin Hamiltonian of NiPS$_3$ requires further investigation, our findings provide new insights into its biquadratic interaction.

### [18] [Neural network as low-cost surrogates for impurity solvers in quantum embedding methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25557)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究训练神经网络作为动力学平均场理论（DMFT）模拟中的杂质求解器（impurity solver），使用比先前工作少1-2个数量级的训练样本。将神经网络求解器与连续时间量子蒙特卡洛（CTQMC）杂质求解器进行比较分析。

Result: 神经网络求解器在训练集内插值时达到与流行CTQMC杂质求解器相当的精度。当外推到训练分布外的较低温度时，其性能显著下降，但输出仍能为更精确的CTQMC杂质求解器提供优质初始猜测，加速求解时间达5倍。

Conclusion: 研究表明神经网络在低数据量条件下可作为DMFT模拟的有效杂质求解器替代方案，特别是在快速相空间探索（rapid phase-space exploration）背景下，能够显著加速计算过程。

Abstract: A promising application of ML is in creating low-cost surrogate models to replace computational bottlenecks in quantum many-body simulations. Here, we explore whether a NN can be trained in the low-data regime, with one to two orders of magnitude fewer training examples than previous works, as an efficient substitute for the impurity solver in DMFT simulations of correlated electron models. We show that the NN solver achieves accuracy comparable to popular CTQMC impurity solvers when interpolating between samples within the training set. While the NN's performance decreases notably when extrapolating to lower temperatures outside the training distribution, its output still provides an excellent initial guess for input to more accurate CTQMC impurity solvers, thus accelerating the time to solution up to a factor of five. We discuss our results in the context of rapid phase-space exploration.

### [19] [Majorana-assisted nonlocal spin correlation in quasi-one-dimensional Kitaev spin liquids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25647)
*Yuki Yamazaki,Shingo Kobayashi,Akira Furusaki*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文提出马约拉纳辅助的非局域自旋关联作为准一维Kitaev自旋液体中马约拉纳非局域性的表现，揭示了有限尺寸诱导拓扑保护的末端马约拉纳零模与端到端自旋关联之间的映射关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索准一维Kitaev自旋液体中马约拉纳非局域性的具体表现形式，为量子自旋液体中的本征马约拉纳非局域性建立可观测的实验特征。

Method: 聚焦于准一维几何结构中Kitaev蜂窝模型的零通量（flux-free）扇区，分析其拓扑性质并证明存在由有限尺寸诱导拓扑（finite-size-induced topology）稳定的末端马约拉纳零模（Majorana zero modes）。通过将非局域马约拉纳费米子宇称算符映射到非局域自旋弦算符，研究局部扰动下的自旋关联行为，并辅以数值计算验证。

Result: 发现非局域马约拉纳费米子宇称算符$P_{\text{MF}}=iγ_{\text{L}}γ_{\text{R}}$映射为自旋弦算符，产生与$P_{\text{MF}}$和总费米子宇称算符乘积成正比的端到端自旋关联。数值计算证实了由马约拉纳零模产生的有限非局域自旋关联，且无任何局域磁化。

Conclusion: 该研究为量子自旋液体中的本征马约拉纳非局域性建立了具体特征，表明马约拉纳辅助的非局域自旋关联可作为马约拉纳非局域性在准一维Kitaev自旋液体中的明确表现。

Abstract: We propose Majorana-assisted nonlocal spin correlation as a manifestation of Majorana nonlocality in quasi-one-dimensional (1D) Kitaev spin liquids. Focusing on the flux-free sector of the Kitaev honeycomb model in a quasi-1D geometry, we uncover its topological nature and show that it hosts Majorana zero modes localized at both ends, which are stabilized by finite-size-induced topology. We further show that the nonlocal Majorana fermion parity operator, $P_{\text{MF}}=iγ_{\text{L}}γ_{\text{R}}$, is mapped to a nonlocal spin-string operator, producing an end-to-end spin correlation proportional to the product of $P_{\text{MF}}$ and total fermion parity operators when local perturbations remove redundant ground-state degeneracies while preserving the Majorana and total fermion parities in the flux-free sector. Numerical calculations confirm a finite nonlocal spin correlation generated by these Majorana zero modes without any local magnetization. Our results establish a concrete signature of intrinsic Majorana nonlocality in quantum spin liquids.

### [20] [Pseudogap and Non-Fermi-liquid criticality in double Kondo model for bilayer nickelates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25742)
*Jing-Yu Zhao,Ya-Hui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过单点动力学平均场理论（DMFT）分析双层镍酸盐高温超导正常态相图，发现无层间隧穿时存在非费米液体（NFL）临界点，区分了过掺杂区的标准费米液体和欠掺杂区的赝隙（PG）金属（称为"第二费米液体"）。研究将该框架应用于双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇，提出当前实验样品处于过掺杂费米液体区，赝隙相和非费米液体临界性可能通过电子掺杂实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于双层镍酸盐高温超导性的最新实验进展，旨在通过双层Kondo晶格模型探究正常态的相图结构，特别关注层间耦合和掺杂对电子态的影响。

Method: 采用单点动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）分析双层Kondo晶格模型，并在辅助费米子（ancilla-fermion）框架下提供赝隙和基态波函数的解析描述。通过DMFT直接计算复合费米子的谱函数，展示类Kondo共振峰。

Result: 当层间隧穿t⊥为零时，发现由层间自旋耦合J⊥或空穴掺杂x调谐的非费米液体（NFL）临界点，区分了过掺杂区的标准费米液体和欠掺杂区的赝隙（pseudogap, PG）金属。该PG相（称为"第二费米液体"）表现出小空穴口袋，违反微扰Luttinger定理但无对称性破缺或分数化。PG金属表现为重费米液体，具有小准粒子残差和大有效质量。

Conclusion: 将分析扩展到有限t⊥并应用于双层镍酸盐La₃Ni₂O₇，提出当前实验样品（x≈0.5）处于过掺杂费米液体区，表明赝隙相和非费米液体临界性可能通过电子掺杂实现。在PG相内，辅助费米子可解释为自旋极化子，DMFT计算直接展示了该复合费米子的类Kondo共振峰。

Abstract: Motivated by recent experimental progress on high-temperature superconductivity in bilayer nickelates, we investigate the phase diagram of the normal state in a bilayer Kondo lattice model using single-site dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT). When the interlayer tunneling $t_\perp$ is absent, we identify a non-Fermi-liquid (NFL) critical point tuned by the interlayer spin coupling $J_\perp$ or hole doping $x$, which separates a standard Fermi liquid in the overdoped region from a distinct pseudogap (PG) metal in the underdoped regime. This PG phase, which we term the `second Fermi liquid' (sFL), exhibits small hole pockets and violates the perturbative Luttinger theorem despite the absence of symmetry breaking or fractionalization. The PG metal behaves like a heavy Fermi liquid, with small quasi-particle residue and large effective mass. We also provide an intuitive analytical description of the pseudogap and the ground-state wave function based on an ancilla-fermion framework. Inside the PG phase, we interpret the ancilla fermion as a spin-polaron and demonstrate a Kondo-like resonance peak in the spectral function of this composite fermion directly in DMFT calculation. Extending the analysis to finite $t_\perp$, we apply this framework to the bilayer nickelate $\mathrm{La}_3\mathrm{Ni}_2\mathrm{O}_7$. We propose that current experimental samples ($x \approx 0.5$) reside in the overdoped FL regime, suggesting that the pseudogap phase and the NFL criticality may be accessed via electron doping.

### [21] [The Rules-and-Facts Model for Simultaneous Generalization and Memorization in Neural Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25579)
*Gabriele Farné,Fabrizio Boncoraglio,Lenka Zdeborová*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文提出了规则与事实（RAF）模型，为理解神经网络同时学习规则和记忆事实的能力提供了理论框架。该模型量化了过参数化如何支持记忆，以及正则化和核选择如何控制容量分配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代神经网络具有同时学习底层规则和记忆特定事实或例外的能力，但对此双重能力的理论理解仍然有限。需要建立一个最小可解模型来精确描述这一现象。

Method: 引入了规则与事实（Rules-and-Facts, RAF）模型，该模型结合了统计物理学习中的两个经典研究方向：用于泛化的师生框架（teacher-student framework）和用于记忆的Gardner式容量分析（Gardner-style capacity analysis）。在RAF模型中，训练标签的一部分（1-ε）由结构化教师规则生成，另一部分（ε）由随机标签的非结构化事实组成。

Result: 研究量化了学习者何时能同时恢复底层规则（允许对新数据泛化）并记忆非结构化示例。结果表明，过参数化（overparameterization）能够同时实现这两个目标：足够的超额容量支持记忆，而正则化（regularization）和核或非线性选择控制容量在规则学习和记忆之间的分配。

Conclusion: RAF模型为理解现代神经网络如何推断结构同时存储稀有或不可压缩信息提供了理论基础。该模型架起了泛化和记忆两个经典研究方向的桥梁，为神经网络的双重能力提供了精确的理论描述框架。

Abstract: A key capability of modern neural networks is their capacity to simultaneously learn underlying rules and memorize specific facts or exceptions. Yet, theoretical understanding of this dual capability remains limited. We introduce the Rules-and-Facts (RAF) model, a minimal solvable setting that enables precise characterization of this phenomenon by bridging two classical lines of work in the statistical physics of learning: the teacher-student framework for generalization and Gardner-style capacity analysis for memorization. In the RAF model, a fraction $1 - \varepsilon$ of training labels is generated by a structured teacher rule, while a fraction $\varepsilon$ consists of unstructured facts with random labels. We characterize when the learner can simultaneously recover the underlying rule - allowing generalization to new data - and memorize the unstructured examples. Our results quantify how overparameterization enables the simultaneous realization of these two objectives: sufficient excess capacity supports memorization, while regularization and the choice of kernel or nonlinearity control the allocation of capacity between rule learning and memorization. The RAF model provides a theoretical foundation for understanding how modern neural networks can infer structure while storing rare or non-compressible information.

# nlin.SI [[Back]](#toc)

### [22] [Deautonomising the Lyness mapping](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24871)
*Basil Grammaticos,Alfred Ramani,Ralph Willox*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文研究了Lyness映射（一种可积的N阶离散系统）的去自治化（deautonomisation）问题。研究发现，标准形式的映射只有N=2时可去自治化，而导数形式对任意N都可行。N=2情况的导数去自治化产生了包含两个指数项的新颖结果，并揭示了"晚期"奇点限制（late singularity confinement）中动力学度的非传统计算方式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在从去自治化（deautonomisation）角度研究Lyness映射，这是一种从Hirota-Miwa方程的一维约化生成的可积N阶离散系统。研究动机在于探索该映射在不同形式下的去自治化可能性及其产生的数学特性。

Method: 研究方法包括分析Lyness映射的标准形式和导数形式（derivative form）的去自治化条件。特别关注N=2情况，通过奇点限制（singularity confinement）技术分析其"晚期"行为，并应用完全去自治化原理（full-deautonomisation principle）。

Result: 结果表明，标准Lyness映射仅N=2时可去自治化，而导数形式对任意N都可行。N=2导数形式的去自治化产生了新颖现象：系数中的长期依赖（secular dependence）通过两个不同指数项而非单一指数项体现。此外，实现了从乘法依赖到加法依赖的极限转换而不改变因变量。

Conclusion: N=2情况的"晚期"奇点限制分析揭示了完全去自治化原理的新实现：动力学度（dynamical degree）并非通过线性或乘法方程简单给出，而是体现在非线性（且不可积）的晚期限制条件的增长中。这为离散系统的去自治化研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We examine the Lyness mapping (an integrable $N$th-order discrete system which can be generated from a one-dimensional reduction of the Hirota-Miwa equation) from the point of view of deautonomisation. We show that only the $N=2$ case can be deautonomised when one works with the standard form of the mapping. However it turns out that deautonomisation is possible for arbitrary $N$ when one considers the derivative form of the Lyness mapping. The deautonomisation of the derivative of the $N=2$ case leads to a result we have never met before: the secular dependence in the coefficients of the mapping enters through two different exponential terms instead of just a single one. As a consequence, it turns out that a limit of this multiplicative dependence towards an additive one is possible without modifying the dependent variable. Finally, the analysis of the `late' singularity confinement of the $N=2$ case leads to a novel realisation of the full-deautonomisation principle: the dynamical degree is not given (as is customary) simply by the solution of some linear or multiplicative equation, but is present in the growth of the non-linear (and non-integrable) late-confinement conditions.

</details>


### [23] [From pencils of Novikov algebras of Stäckel type to soliton hierarchies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25352)
*Maciej Błaszak,Krzysztof Marciniak,Błażej M. Szablikowski*

Main category: nlin.SI

TL;DR: 本文从Stäckel型Novikov代数的铅笔构造演化孤子层次结构，通过中心扩展Dubrovin-Novikov哈密顿算子得到相容泊松算子对，进而推导出耦合KdV和耦合Harry Dym层次结构及其三角形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于从Stäckel型Novikov代数的特殊类别出发，构建演化孤子层次结构。这类代数与Viète坐标中的经典Stäckel度量相关，为构造可积系统提供了代数基础。

Method: 方法包括：定义Stäckel型Novikov代数这一特殊关联代数类别；建立这些代数铅笔的充分条件，使得相应的Dubrovin-Novikov哈密顿算子能够进行中心扩展；通过中心扩展产生成对相容的泊松算子集合。

Result: 研究结果获得了耦合Korteweg-de Vries（cKdV）层次结构和耦合Harry Dym（cHD）层次结构，以及三角cKdV层次结构和三角cHD层次结构。这些层次结构由相容泊松算子对生成。

Conclusion: 结论表明，从Stäckel型Novikov代数的铅笔出发，通过中心扩展Dubrovin-Novikov哈密顿算子并产生相容泊松算子，能够系统性地构造多种演化孤子层次结构，包括耦合KdV和耦合Harry Dym系统及其三角变体。

Abstract: In this article we construct evolutionary soliton hierarchies from pencils of Novikov algebras of Stäckel type. We start by defining a special class of associative Novikov algebras, which we call Novikov algebras of Stäckel type, as they are associated with classical Stäckel metrics in Viète coordinates. We obtain sufficient conditions for pencils of these algebras so that the corresponding Dubrovin-Novikov Hamiltonian operators can be centrally extended, producing sets of pairwise compatible Poisson operators. These operators lead to coupled Korteweg-de~Vries (cKdV) and coupled Harry Dym (cHD) hierarchies, as well as to a triangular cKdV hierarchy and a triangular cHD hierarchy.

</details>

### [24] [The Dynamic Doppler Spectrum Induced by Nonlinear Sensor Motion: Relativistic Kinematics and 4D Frenet-Serret Spacetime Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24870)
*Bryce M. Barclay,Alex Mahalov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了非线性相对论运动中的动态多普勒效应，通过两种框架分析非惯性接收器观测的电磁信号：高阶运动学四维向量（相对论加速度和急动度）以及四维Frenet-Serret框架（曲率和挠率），推导了紧凑的频谱变换表达式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性相对论运动分析的核心在于精确描述诱导的动态多普勒效应。研究旨在为非惯性接收器观测的电磁信号提供理论框架，为雷达、传感和通信系统等工程应用提供诊断和预测工具。

Method: 采用两种框架描述相对论运动：首先使用高阶运动学四维向量（相对论加速度和急动度），推导频谱变换的紧凑表达式；其次使用四维Frenet-Serret框架和观测路径的曲率（curvature）与挠率（torsion），从几何参数角度描述信号特性。

Result: 相对论加速度和急动度分别导致指数频谱展宽和指数幅度增长/衰减。急动度在观测信号中诱导非线性偏斜啁啾。基于曲率和挠率的几何参数，获得了信号幅度和相位波动的描述，提供了简洁可解释的非惯性动态多普勒效应表征。

Conclusion: 简洁可解释的非惯性动态多普勒效应描述为雷达、传感和通信系统等工程应用提供了有用的诊断和预测工具，实现了对非线性相对论运动诱导效应的精确表征。

Abstract: Fundamental to the analysis of nonlinear relativistic motion is the precise characterization of the induced dynamic Doppler effects. In this work, we analyze the electromagnetic signals observed by non-inertial receivers using two frameworks to describe the relativistic motion. We first consider observer paths described by higher-order kinematic 4 vectors: relativistic acceleration and jolt. The dynamic Doppler effects of relativistic acceleration and jolt are exponential spectral broadening and exponential amplitude growth or decay. We derive compact expressions for the spectrum transformation resulting from relativistic acceleration and jolt. The jolt induces nonlinear skewed chirps in observed signals. Next we consider observer paths described by the 4D Frenet-Serret frame and the curvature and torsion of the observer path. We obtain descriptions of the amplitude and phase fluctuations of the signal in terms of the geometric parameters of curvature and torsion. Concise, interpretable descriptions of non-inertial dynamic Doppler effects provide a useful diagnostic and predictive tool for engineering applications including radar, sensing, and communications systems.

Abstract: Various applications of Chern-Simons theory in algebraic topology, in particular knot theory, condensed matter physics and cosmology are reviewed. Special attention is paid to appearances of Chern-Simons actions in the theory of the (integer and fractional) quantum Hall effect. ### [28] [On the integrability structure of the deformed rule-54 reversible cellular automaton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25424)
*Chiara Paletta,Tomaž Prosen*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了规则54可逆元胞自动机（RCA54）在1+1维时空晶格上的量子与随机变形，重点分析其在两种不同设置下的可积性结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索RCA54模型的量子与随机变形，并分析这些变形模型的可积性结构，特别是在量子电路和马尔可夫链电路两种不同设置下的表现。

Method: 对于量子变形，通过构造六格点支撑的Lax算子，证明守恒荷属于由转移矩阵高阶对数导数生成的无穷塔；对于随机变形，采用交错补丁矩阵拟设（staggered patch matrix ansatz）构造非平衡稳态，结合未变形RCA54的交换补丁态拟设与矩阵乘积拟设。

Result: 量子变形中，最短范围非平凡守恒荷密度支撑在六个连续格点上，属于由转移矩阵生成的无穷守恒荷塔；随机变形中，通过交错补丁矩阵拟设显式构造了非平衡稳态；此外提出了基于数字复杂性（digit complexity）的经验判据来检测模型的可积性或精确可解性。

Conclusion: 研究成功分析了RCA54量子与随机变形的可积性结构，建立了相应的数学框架，并提出了检测模型可积性的新判据，为理解这类离散时空模型的可积性质提供了系统方法。

Abstract: We study quantum and stochastic deformations of the rule-54 reversible cellular automaton (RCA54) on a 1+1-dimensional spatiotemporal lattice, focusing on their integrability structures in two distinct settings. First, for the quantum deformation, which turns the model into an interaction-round-a-face brickwork quantum circuit (either on an infinite lattice or with periodic boundary conditions), we show that the shortest-range nontrivial conserved charge commuting with the discrete-time evolution operator has a density supported on six consecutive sites. By constructing the corresponding range-6 Lax operator, we prove that this charge belongs to an infinite tower of mutually commuting conserved charges generated by higher-order logarithmic derivatives of the transfer matrix. With the aid of an intertwining operator, we further prove that the transfer matrix commutes with the discrete-time evolution operator.
  Second, for the stochastic deformation, which renders the model into a Markov-chain circuit, we investigate open boundary conditions that couple the system at its edges to stochastic reservoirs. In this setting, we explicitly construct the non-equilibrium steady state (NESS) by means of a staggered patch matrix ansatz, a hybrid construction combining the previously used commutative patch-state ansatz for the undeformed RCA54 with the matrix-product ansatz. Finally, we propose a simple empirical criterion for detecting integrability or exact solvability in a given model setup, introducing the notion of digit complexity.

</details>

### [32] [The Spatial Hydrodynamic Attractor: Resurgence of the Gradient Expansion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24611)
*Mahdi Kooshkbaghi*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了远离平衡态（far-from-equilibrium）动力学系统的流体力学吸引子（hydrodynamic attractor），证明了非相对论空间梯度展开（spatial gradient expansion）虽发散但严格可Borel求和（Borel summable），而相对论因果性（relativistic causality）约束下的空间梯度展开则具有有限收敛半径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，远离平衡态动力学系统坍塌到流体力学吸引子通常用梯度展开（gradient expansion）近似。时间梯度级数（temporal gradient series）不可Borel求和且需要transseries补全，而空间梯度展开的解析结构（analytic structure）一直未被阐明。

Method: 通过拉格朗日反演（Lagrange inversion）推导了所有阶数的精确封闭形式Chapman-Enskog系数，并分析了非相对论和相对论情形下空间梯度级数的收敛性质。

Result: 证明了非相对论空间梯度级数虽阶乘发散（factorially divergent）但严格可Borel求和。进一步发现这种发散源于无界的伽利略速度（unbounded Galilean velocities）；施加相对论因果性约束后，空间流体力学展开具有有限收敛半径（finite radius）。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了空间梯度展开的解析结构：非相对论情形下可Borel求和，而相对论因果性确保了空间流体力学展开的收敛性，为远离平衡态系统的流体力学描述提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Far-from-equilibrium kinetic systems collapse onto a hydrodynamic attractor, traditionally approximated by a gradient expansion. While temporal gradient series are non-Borel summable and require transseries completions, the analytic structure of the spatial expansion has remained elusive. Here, we derive exact closed-form Chapman--Enskog coefficients at all orders via Lagrange inversion and prove that the non-relativistic spatial gradient series, though factorially divergent, is strictly Borel summable. Furthermore, we show that this divergence originates from unbounded Galilean velocities; enforcing relativistic causality yields a convergent spatial hydrodynamic expansion with finite radius.

</details>

### [33] [Photoacoustic tomography with time-dependent damping: Theoretical and a convolutional neural network-guided numerical inversion procedure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24610)
*Sunghwan Moon,Anwesa Dey,Souvik Roy*

TL;DR: 该研究为光声层析成像（PAT）提出了一种考虑声学衰减影响的图像重建方法，通过阻尼波动方程建模，证明了初始压力的唯一确定性，并开发了基于庞特里亚金极大值原理的无梯度数值重建算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光声层析成像（photoacoustic tomography, PAT）中，生物组织内的声学衰减会导致显著的信号失真，需要开发能够准确建模这种衰减效应并实现稳健图像重建的理论框架和数值方法。

Method: 采用具有空间变化声速和时变阻尼项的阻尼波动方程（damped wave equation）对异质介质中的PAT进行建模；通过边界数据的谐波延拓（harmonic extension）证明初始压力的唯一确定性；对于恒定阻尼情况，利用$-c^2(\xx)Δ$的Dirichlet本征函数展开获得显式级数重建公式；最后基于庞特里亚金极大值原理（Pontryagin's maximum principle）开发无梯度数值方法。

Result: 在自然假设下，证明了初始压力可通过边界测量唯一确定；对于恒定阻尼情况，推导出基于Dirichlet本征函数展开的显式级数重建公式；开发了稳健且计算可行的无梯度数值重建方法。

Conclusion: 该研究为衰减PAT提供了一套完整的理论框架和数值实现方案，通过阻尼波动方程准确建模声学衰减效应，证明了重建的唯一性，并开发了基于庞特里亚金极大值原理的实用重建算法，为生物医学成像应用提供了重要工具。

Abstract: In photoacoustic tomography (PAT), a hybrid imaging modality that is based on the acoustic detection of optical absorption from biological tissue exposed to a pulsed laser, a short pulse laser generates an initial pressure proportional to the absorbed optical energy, which then propagates acoustically and is measured on the boundary. To account for the significant signal distortion caused by acoustic attenuation in biological tissue, we model PAT in heterogeneous media using a damped wave equation featuring spatially varying sound speed and a time-dependent damping term. Under natural assumptions, we show that the initial pressure is uniquely determined by the boundary measurements using a harmonic extension of the boundary data with energy decay. For constant damping, an expansion in Dirichlet eigenfunctions of $-c^2(\xx)Δ$ leads to an explicit series reconstruction formula for the initial pressure. Finally, we develop a gradient free numerical method based on the Pontryagin's maximum principle to provide a robust and computationally viable approach to image reconstruction in attenuating PAT.

</details>


### [34] [Structure-Preserving Integration for Magnetic Gaussian Wave Packet Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25596)
*Sebastian Merk,Caroline Lasser*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 该文开发了用于磁薛定谔方程（magnetic Schrödinger equation）高斯波包动力学的结构保持时间积分方案，通过变分Dirac-Frenkel公式得到波包参数的哈密顿系统，构建了Boris型积分器和显式高阶辛格式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于为磁薛定谔方程的高斯波包动力学开发结构保持时间积分方案。由于磁矢量势（magnetic vector potential）的存在导致非可分离结构和修正的辛几何，需要设计能够保持系统固有几何特性的数值方法。

Method: 采用变分Dirac-Frenkel公式获得波包参数的有限维哈密顿系统。通过最小替换引入动力学动量，将平均动力学重构为泊松系统（Poisson system）。基于此表示构建了适应变分设置的Boris型积分器，以及基于分裂方法（splitting methods）和分区Runge-Kutta积分器的显式高阶辛格式。

Result: 所提方法能够保持表征Hagedorn参数化的二次不变量，在对称假设下保持线性和角动量，并在长时间区间内近乎守恒平均哈密顿量。获得了波包参数和可观测量的一致误差估计，数值实验验证了积分器良好的长时间行为和结构保持特性。

Conclusion: 该研究成功开发了适用于磁薛定谔方程高斯波包动力学的结构保持积分方案，这些方法在保持系统几何特性方面表现优异，为相关量子动力学模拟提供了有效的数值工具。

Abstract: We develop structure-preserving time integration schemes for Gaussian wave packet dynamics associated with the magnetic Schrödinger equation. The variational Dirac--Frenkel formulation yields a finite-dimensional Hamiltonian system for the wave packet parameters, where the presence of a magnetic vector potential leads to a non-separable structure and a modified symplectic geometry. By introducing kinetic momenta through a minimal substitution, we reformulate the averaged dynamics as a Poisson system that closely parallels the classical equations of charged particle motion. This representation enables the construction of Boris-type integrators adapted to the variational setting. In addition, we propose explicit high-order symplectic schemes based on splitting methods and partitioned Runge--Kutta integrators. The proposed methods conserve the quadratic invariants characterizing the Hagedorn parametrization, preserve linear and angular momentum under symmetry assumptions, and exhibit near-conservation of the averaged Hamiltonian over long time intervals. Rigorous error estimates are derived for both the wave packet parameters and observable quantities, with bounds uniform in the semiclassical parameter. Numerical experiments demonstrate the favorable long-time behavior and structure preservation of the integrators.

</details>


### [35] [An efficient compact splitting Fourier spectral methods for computing the dynamics of rotating spin-orbit coupled spin-2 Bose-Einstein condenstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25282)
*Xin Liu,Ziqing Xie,Yongjun Yuan,Yong Zhang,Xinyi Zhao*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高效的高阶紧致分裂傅里叶谱方法，用于研究具有旋转和自旋轨道耦合（SOC）的自旋-2玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（BECs）的动力学。该方法将哈密顿量分裂为线性部分（包含拉普拉斯、旋转和SOC项）和非线性部分，通过傅里叶谱方法近似波函数，并利用离散快速傅里叶变换（FFT）进行数值计算。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究具有旋转和自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）的自旋-2玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates, BECs）的动力学行为。为了更好地模拟这些复杂系统的动力学特性，需要开发高效且精确的数值方法。

Method: 提出了一种高效的高阶紧致分裂傅里叶谱方法（high-order compact splitting Fourier spectral method）。该方法将哈密顿量分裂为线性部分（包含拉普拉斯、旋转和SOC项）和非线性部分。通过基于旋转的函数映射，精确且显式地积分线性子问题，同时消除旋转项并防止SOC项演化为时间依赖形式。非线性子问题在物理空间中解析积分。

Result: 该方法在空间上具有谱精度，在时间上具有高阶精度。该方法高效、显式、无条件稳定且易于实现。研究还推导了一些动力学性质，并进行了系统研究，包括精度和效率测试、动力学性质验证、SOC效应以及涡旋晶格动力学分析。

Conclusion: 所提出的紧致分裂方法仅涉及两个算子，便于设计高阶分裂方案。该方法为研究具有旋转和自旋轨道耦合的自旋-2玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体的动力学提供了有效的数值工具，能够处理旋转项和SOC项带来的主要挑战。

Abstract: This paper investigates the dynamics of spin-2 Bose-Einstein condensates (BECs) with rotation and spin-orbit coupling (SOC). In order to better simulate the dynamics, we present an efficient high-order compact splitting Fourier spectral method. This method splits the Hamiltonian into a linear part, which consists of the Laplace, rotation and SOC terms, and a nonlinear part that includes all the remaining terms. The wave function is well approximated by the Fourier spectral method and is numerically accessed with discrete Fast Fourier transform (FFT). For linear subproblem, the handling of rotation term and SOC term poses a major challenge. Using a function mapping based on rotation, we can integrate the linear subproblem exactly and explicitly. This mapping we propose not only helps eliminate the rotation term, but also prevents the SOC term from evolving into a time-dependent form. The nonlinear subproblem is integrated analytically in physical space. Such "compact" splitting involves only two operators and facilitates the design of high-order splitting schemes. Our method is spectrally accurate in space and high order in time. It is efficient, explicit, unconditionally stable and simple to implement. In addition, we derive some dynamical properties and carry out a systematic study, including accuracy and efficiency tests, dynamical property verification, the SOC effects and dynamics of vortex lattice.

### [36] [A Quasicontinuum Method with Optimized Local Maximum-Entropy Interpolation and Heaviside Enrichment for Heterogeneous Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25667)
*Benjamin Werner,Ondřej Rokoš,Jan Zeman*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 晶格系统（lattice systems）虽能有效模拟异质材料，但计算成本过高。准连续体方法通过粗网格插值降低计算量，但异质系统的材料界面仍需精细离散。扩展有限元法的富集策略可在非协调网格上表示界面，但需进一步改进。

Method: 在准连续体框架中，将Heaviside富集与无网格局部最大熵插值（Local Maximum Entropy interpolation）相结合，系统研究LME局部参数的作用及其优化。基于观察结果，推导出基于模式的简化规则，以较低计算成本保留优化的大部分优势。

Result: 优化后的LME插值在相同自由度下，比线性插值的准连续体方法提高了约一个数量级的位移精度。最优局部参数场在界面附近呈现非均匀分布，并表现出系统的空间结构特征。

Conclusion: 该方法在三个数值算例中得到验证。基于模式的简化规则能以较低计算成本实现大部分优化效果，为异质晶格系统的高效模拟提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Lattice systems are effective for modeling heterogeneous materials, but their computational cost is often prohibitive. The QuasiContinuum (QC) method reduces this cost by interpolating the lattice response over a coarse finite-element mesh, yet material interfaces in heterogeneous systems still require fine discretizations. Enrichment strategies from the eXtended Finite Element Method (XFEM) address this by representing interfaces on nonconforming meshes. In this work, we combine Heaviside enrichment with meshless Local Maximum Entropy (LME) interpolation in the QC framework for heterogeneous lattice systems. We systematically investigate the role of the LME locality parameter and its optimization. The results show that optimized LME interpolation improves displacement accuracy by about one order of magnitude over QC with linear interpolation at the same number of degrees of freedom. In addition, the optimal locality-parameter fields are nonuniform near interfaces and exhibit systematic spatial structure. Based on these observations, we derive simple pattern-based rules that retain much of the benefit of full optimization at a fraction of the computational cost. The approach is demonstrated on three numerical examples.

### [37] [Conventionalism in general relativity?: formal existence proofs and Reichenbach's theorem θ in context](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24608)
*Ruward Mulder*

Main category: physics.hist-ph

TL;DR: 该论文澄清了关于Reichenbach几何对偶性（geometric duality）证明的两个不同目标：存在性主张与普遍性主张，并证明不存在能够挽救"定理θ（theorem theta）"的丰富不可行定理（no-go theorem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Weatherall和Manchak（2014）的研究表明，在合理假设下，Reichenbach式普遍效应存在于非相对论引力中，但在相对论时空（relativistic spacetimes）中不存在，这导致广义相对论比牛顿理论更不易受欠定问题（underdetermination）影响。Dürr和Ben-Menahem（2022）认为这些假设可作为漏洞利用，实质上建立了一个丰富的不可行定理。

Method: 作者区分了证明的两个先前被混淆的目标：给定几何至少存在一个替代几何的存在性主张，以及Reichenbach著名的"定理θ"所代表的普遍性主张。通过明确打破其中一个假设并将证明推广到含挠时空（torsionful spacetimes），作者展示了不存在挽救定理θ的丰富不可行定理。

Result: 分析表明，不存在能够挽救Reichenbach"定理θ"普遍性主张的丰富不可行定理。通过打破假设并将证明推广到含挠时空，作者具体说明了如何规避原有证明的限制条件。

Conclusion: 作者建议采用纲领性态度：不应削弱证明本身，而是利用它来系统且严谨地阐述待证明的更强命题，从而系统探索替代时空理论（alternative spacetime theories）的空间。

Abstract: Weatherall and Manchak (2014) show that, under reasonable assumptions, Reichenbachean universal effects, constrained to a rank-2 tensor field representation in the geodesic equation, always exist in non-relativistic gravity but not so for relativistic spacetimes. Thus general relativity is less susceptible to underdetermination than its Newtonian predecessor. Dürr and Ben-Menahem (2022) argue these assumptions are exploitable as loopholes, effectively establishing a (rich) no-go theorem. I disambiguate between two targets of the proof, which have previously been conflated: the existence claim of at least one alternative geometry to a given one and Reichenbach's (in)famous ``theorem theta", which amounts to a universality claim that any geometry can function as an alternative to any other. I show there is no (rich) no-go theorem to save theorem theta. I illustrate this by explicitly breaking one of the assumptions and generalising the proof to torsionful spacetimes. Finally, I suggest a programmatic attitude: rather than undermining the proof one can use it to systematically and rigorously articulate stronger propositions to be proved, thereby systematically exploring the space of alternative spacetime theories.

</details>

### [38] [Modified log-Sobolev inequalities, concentration bounds and uniqueness of Gibbs measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25479)
*Yannic Steenbeck*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明，在满足特定浓度度量（concentration-of-measure）界限的条件下，对于给定相互作用只存在唯一的平移不变吉布斯点过程（translation-invariant Gibbsian point process）。这一界限在相应的修正对数索博列夫不等式（modified logarithmic Sobolev inequality）成立时得以满足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于理解吉布斯点过程的唯一性问题，特别是在非唯一性区域（non-uniqueness regimes）中修正对数索博列夫不等式是否成立。这关系到相关连续时间生灭动力学（continuous-time birth-and-death dynamics）中自由能耗散（free-energy dissipation）的速率特性。

Method: 采用概率论方法，通过证明在满足特定浓度度量界限的条件下，平移不变吉布斯点过程的唯一性。该方法的关键在于建立浓度度量界限与修正对数索博列夫不等式之间的关系。

Result: 主要结果是：对于自然例子中的非唯一性区域，修正对数索博列夫不等式无法被满足。因此，在这些情况下，相关连续时间生灭动力学中的自由能耗散不会以指数速度进行。

Conclusion: 结论表明，浓度度量界限或修正对数索博列夫不等式的存在保证了吉布斯点过程的唯一性。这一结果为理解非唯一性区域中动力学行为提供了理论依据，揭示了自由能耗散速率与相变现象之间的深刻联系。

Abstract: We prove that there is only one translation-invariant Gibbsian point process w.r.t. to a chosen interaction if any of them satisfies a certain bound related to concentration-of-measure. This concentration-of-measure bound is e.g. fulfilled if a corresponding modified logarithmic Sobolev inequality holds. In particular, for natural examples with non-uniqueness regimes, a modified logarithmic Sobolev inequality cannot be satisfied. Therefore, in these situations, the free-energy dissipation in related continuous-time birth-and-death dynamics in $\mathbb{R}^d$ is not exponentially fast.

</details>

### [42] [Origin of Giant Phonon Magnetic Moment in Orbital Seebeck Effect: a Heisenberg-type L-L Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25019)
*Hong Sun,Jinxin Zhong,Yimin Yao,Jun Zhou,Lifa Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文发现手性绝缘体中存在一种内在放大机制，可将热产生的声子角动量和声子磁矩放大近两个数量级。该机制源于声子角动量间的海森堡型长程耦合（L-L耦合），通过自洽反馈通道在线性响应范围内显著增强热响应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受最近在α-石英中观测到的轨道塞贝克效应（orbital Seebeck effect）启发，本文旨在识别手性绝缘体中热产生声子角动量和声子磁矩的内在放大机制。研究试图为α-石英中观测到的巨大声子磁矩提供微观起源解释。

Method: 本文提出了一种海森堡型长程耦合（Heisenberg-type long-range coupling），称为L-L耦合，它在声子角动量之间建立联系。该耦合开启了一个自洽反馈通道（self-consistent feedback channel），在线性响应（linear response）范围内强烈增强裸热响应（bare thermal response）。

Result: 计算显示存在显著的温度和尺寸依赖性放大效应，由非对角通道（off-diagonal channel）主导。当系统从下方接近阈值时，总声子角动量（total phonon angular momentum）可增强近两个数量级。这些发现表明L-L耦合可能为α-石英中观测到的巨大声子磁矩提供微观起源。

Conclusion: L-L耦合机制为手性绝缘体中热产生声子角动量和声子磁矩的显著增强提供了理论解释，并可能解释最近在α-石英中观测到的轨道塞贝克效应和巨大声子磁矩现象。

Abstract: Inspired by the recent observation of the orbital Seebeck effect in alpha-quartz, we identify an intrinsic amplification mechanism for thermally generated phonon angular momentum and phonon magnetic moment in chiral insulators. We propose a Heisenberg-type long-range coupling between phonon angular momenta, referred to here as L-L coupling, which opens a self-consistent feedback channel and strongly enhances the bare thermal response within linear response. Our calculations reveal a pronounced temperature- and size-dependent amplification, dominated by the off-diagonal channel, with the total phonon angular momentum enhanced by up to nearly two orders of magnitude as the system approaches the threshold from below. These findings suggest that L-L coupling may provide a microscopic origin of giant phonon magnetic moment the recently observed orbital Seebeck effect in alpha-quartz.

</details>

### [43] [The background gas humming and multi-messenger transients of stalled supermassive black hole binaries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24678)
*Pau Amaro Seoane,Alessandra Mastrobuono Battisti,Chingis Omarov,Denis Yurin,Maxim Makukov,Dana Kuvatova,Gulnara Omarova,Anton Gluchshenko*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究建立了超大质量黑洞双星在环双星盘内停滞时的多信使力学机制，揭示了通过激波形成产生的有界吸积爆发、谐波级联谱密度、双星质量比精确提取方法，以及作为最终真空旋进前兆的高频引力波侧带信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在理解停滞在环双星盘（circumbinary discs）内的超大质量黑洞双星（supermassive black hole binaries）的间歇性质量转移多信使力学机制，特别是探索吸积激波产生的观测信号及其对双星参数提取的潜力。

Method: 采用连续小波变换（continuous wavelet transforms）定位腔体边缘的气体团块并追踪其演化；通过非均匀艾里微分方程（inhomogeneous Airy differential equation）在Lindblad共振处正则化受迫流体方程，绕过线性奇点提取有限波幅以触发非线性激波形成。

Result: 激波产生有界吸积爆发（bounded accretion bursts），其热光度时间域模型导出形成谐波级联（harmonic cascade）的解析功率谱密度；吸积流叠加产生谱拍频（spectral beat frequency），可精确提取双星质量比；激波加速电子的辐射冷却产生从同步射电连续谱到逆康普顿伽马射线尾的多波长谱能量分布。

Conclusion: 研究识别出相对论性特征：一个不连续的高频引力波侧带信号，称为"背景气体嗡鸣"（background gas humming），源于吸积激波的高度不对称瞬态流体几何结构；该信号表现为离散高频爆发序列，其时间静止间隙随腔体收缩而系统压缩，最终在4.0 mHz附近的终端爆发作为最终真空旋进（vacuum inspiral）的多信使前兆。

Abstract: We establish the multi-messenger mechanics of episodic mass transfer in supermassive black hole binaries stalled within circumbinary discs. Utilizing continuous wavelet transforms, we isolate localized gas clumps at the cavity edge and track their evolution. By regularizing the forced fluid equations at Lindblad resonances via the inhomogeneous Airy differential equation, we bypass linear singularities to extract the finite wave amplitudes that trigger non-linear shock formation. These shocks produce bounded accretion bursts. We model the time-domain thermal luminosity, deriving an analytical power spectral density that forms a harmonic cascade. The superposition of the accretion streams generates a spectral beat frequency, providing an exact mathematical extraction of the binary mass ratio. The radiative cooling of shock-accelerated electrons produces a multi-wavelength spectral energy distribution from a synchrotron radio continuum to an inverse-Compton gamma-ray tail. We identify a relativistic signature: a discontinuous, high-frequency gravitational wave sideband termed the ``background gas humming''. This emission arises from the highly asymmetric, transient fluid geometry of the accretion shocks. Evaluating the asymptotic properties of the Airy regularization, we show that this humming manifests as a sequence of discrete high-frequency bursts with temporal quiescence gaps that systematically compress as the cavity shrinks. We show that the instantaneous mass of the gas actively trapped within the cavity violently amplifies prior to decoupling, culminating in a terminal burst near 4.0 mHz that serves as a multi-messenger precursor to the final vacuum inspiral.

### [44] [Photon Ring Astrometry I: A Simple Spin Measurement Technique for High-Resolution Images of M87*](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24722)
*Delilah E. A. Gates,Dominic O. Chang,Aaron Held,Daniel C. M. Palumbo*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种利用M87星系中心超大质量黑洞光子环（photon ring）亚像与直接像之间的相对位移进行黑洞自旋（spin）测量的新方法，该方法基于相对天体测量学（relative astrometry）原理，不依赖于对观测辐射的几何建模。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: M87星系中心的超大质量黑洞（supermassive black hole）目前是使用高分辨率视界尺度成像进行精确自旋测量的目标。现有观测旨在从更广泛的直接像中分辨出光子环的第一级透镜亚像（n=1 sub-image），但需要开发更有效的自旋测量技术。

Method: 本文识别了一个具体可观测物理量——光子环亚像与直接像中心之间的位移（displacement），并提出了基于此的简单自旋测量技术。该方法假设M87观测到的大尺度喷流（large-scale jet）与黑洞自旋轴对齐，将光子环的相对位置分解为平行和垂直于投影自旋轴的分量，并用n=1亚像的测量直径进行归一化。

Result: 研究显示，平行位移主要由倾角（inclination）和辐射半径（emission radius）决定，而横向位移与倾角和自旋紧密相关。通过简单几何模型和GRMHD模拟（general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic simulations）验证了这些效应。研究发现，相对天体测量分辨率达到≲0.1微角秒（μas）时，可对自旋进行有效约束。

Conclusion: 该方法将相对光子环天体测量学（relative photon ring astrometry）确立为约束基础时空几何的有前景方法，并引入了一种不依赖于观测辐射几何建模的自旋约束技术。对于顺行吸积流（prograde accretion flow）可将自旋约束到优于9%，逆行流（retrograde flow）为22%，流向未定时为26%。

Abstract: The central supermassive black hole of the galaxy M87 is currently a target for precision spin measurement using high-resolution, horizon-scale imaging. Such observations aim to resolve the first lensed (${n}~{=}~{1}$) sub-image of the photon ring from the broader direct image. In this work, we identify a concrete observable -- the displacement between the centers of the ${n}~{=}~{1}$ photon-ring sub-image and the direct image -- and propose its use in a simple spin-measurement technique. Leveraging the assumption that the observed large-scale jet of M87 is aligned with the black-hole spin axis, we separate the relative position of the photon ring into components parallel and transverse to the projected spin axis, normalizing both components with respect to the measured diameter of the ${n}~{=}~{1}$ sub-image. We show that the parallel shift is primarily determined by inclination and emission radius, while the transverse shift is tightly correlated with inclination and spin. We demonstrate these effects both in a simple geometric model (to explain the underlying physics) and in GRMHD simulations with magnetically arrested disks (to provide realistic instantiations of the effect). We find that a relative astrometric resolution of ${\lesssim}~{0.1\;μ\rm{as}}$ is sufficient to constrain the spin to better than 9% if the accretion flow is prograde or 22% if the flow is retrograde. If the direction of the accretion flow is undetermined, the spin can be constrained to within 26%. More generally, this identifies relative photon ring astrometry as a promising method to constrain the underlying spacetime geometry and introduces a spin-constraint technique that does not rely on geometric modeling of the observed emission.

</details>


### [45] [Binary neutron star mergers with a subsolar mass star](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25102)
*Maxence Corman,William E. East,Jocelyn S. Read*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过全广义相对论模拟，分析了包含亚太阳质量（0.8 M☉）中子星的双中子星并合系统，发现其具有高达10⁴量级的潮汐形变度，显著影响并合动力学、引力波信号和电磁信号，但当前引力波探测器仍能有效探测此类系统。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚太阳质量致密天体（包括原初黑洞或坍缩星盘中形成的中子星）的存在尚未得到确凿观测证实。研究动机在于探索此类天体若存在，其双星并合产生的引力波可能揭示其性质，并评估当前模型对包含亚太阳质量中子星的双中子星并合系统的描述能力。

Method: 采用全广义相对论模拟（fully general-relativistic simulations），研究1.7 M☉与0.8 M☉中子星的并合过程。量化亚太阳质量中子星高达10⁴量级的潮汐形变度（tidal deformabilities）对并合动力学、引力波和电磁信号的影响。

Result: 研究发现恒星间存在质量转移，且潮汐瓦解频率显著降低。虽然当前引力波波形模型未捕捉此特征，但这对当前引力波探测器灵敏度影响不大。在信噪比≲100时，LIGO和Virgo探测器设计灵敏度下恢复的本征参数无偏差。大形变度导致动力学喷射物质显著增加，超出当前唯象模型预测。

Conclusion: 包含亚太阳质量中子星的双中子星并合系统具有独特的动力学特征，特别是高形变度和增强的物质喷射。尽管当前引力波模型未完全描述这些特征，但现有探测器仍能有效探测此类系统，且参数恢复无显著偏差，为未来观测亚太阳质量致密天体提供了理论基础。

Abstract: While there are a number of proposed formation channels for subsolar mass compact objects, including black holes formed primordially, or neutron stars that form in collapsar disks, there have yet to be any conclusive observations of such objects. Motivated by the possibility that, if such objects exist, gravitational waves from binary mergers may reveal them, we study binary neutron star mergers where one star has a subsolar-mass in order to determine how well such systems are described by current models, and when they could be distinguished from a system with a subsolar-mass black hole. We perform fully general-relativistic simulations of a $1.7\ M_{\odot}$ star merging with a $0.8\ M_{\odot}$ star, leading to tidal deformabilities of up to $\mathcal{O}(10^4)$ for the latter, and quantify how this affects the merger dynamics and associated gravitation and electromagnetic signals. In this regime, we find mass transfer between the stars, as well as significantly lower disruption frequencies. Though this is not captured by current gravitational waveform models, we conclude that this does not significantly impact the sensitivity of current gravitational wave detectors to these sources. Assuming design sensitivity of the LIGO and Virgo detectors, we find no biases in the recovered intrinsic parameters for signal-to-noise ratios $\lesssim 100$. We also find that the large deformabilities lead to a significant increase in the amount of dynamically ejected matter compared to equal mass systems, exceeding the predictions of current phenomenological models.

### [46] [Landau Analysis in the Grassmannian](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25454)
*Benjamin Hollering,Elia Mazzucchelli,Matteo Parisi,Bernd Sturmfels*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 该论文将动量扭子（momentum twistors）应用于粒子物理散射振幅，发展了三空间中的朗道分析（Landau analysis），并将所得判别式与结果式识别为格拉斯曼流形积中关联簇的Hurwitz形式和Chow形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在将动量扭子（momentum twistors）这一粒子物理散射振幅的几何框架，与朗道分析（Landau analysis）这一研究费曼积分奇点的方法相结合，探索其几何结构。

Method: 方法包括在三空间（three-space）中发展费曼积分的朗道分析，将所得判别式（discriminants）和结果式（resultants）识别为格拉斯曼流形（Grassmannians）积中关联簇（incidence varieties）的Hurwitz形式和Chow形式。

Result: 研究结果包括分析了这些形式的次数和因子分解，以及朗道映射（Landau map）纤维在运动学区域（kinematic regimes）中的有理性或实性。通过将该映射识别为正位形簇（positroid varieties）上的amplituhedron映射，并将相关递归与提升映射（promotion maps）关联，揭示了正性（positivity）和簇结构（cluster structures）在平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论（planar N=4 super Yang-Mills theory）中出现的几何机制。

Conclusion: 论文建立了动量扭子框架下朗道分析的几何解释，揭示了该映射与amplituhedron映射的等价性，从而为平面N=4超杨-米尔斯理论中正性和簇结构的出现提供了统一的几何机制。

Abstract: Momentum twistors for scattering amplitudes in particle physics are lines in three-space. We develop Landau analysis for Feynman integrals in this setting. The resulting discriminants and resultants are identified with Hurwitz and Chow forms of incidence varieties in products of Grassmannians. We study their degrees and factorizations, and the kinematic regimes in which the fibers of the Landau map are rational or real. Identifying this map with the amplituhedron map on positroid varieties, and the associated recursions with promotion maps, yields a geometric mechanism for the emergence of positivity and cluster structures in planar N=4 super Yang-Mills theory.

### [47] [Bounds on the Mordell-Weil rank of elliptic fibrations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24666)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 论文提出了两种证明方法来推导椭圆纤维化Mordell-Weil群秩的上界，特别关注卡拉比-丘流形，并针对不同维度情况采用相应证明策略。

Result: 主要结果为：证明了卡拉比-丘三维流形（Calabi-Yau threefolds）的显式上界，这与物理预测一致；在温和假设下，为四维流形（fourfolds）给出了新的显式上界。

Conclusion: 这些结果促使作者提出了关于任意维度上界的猜想，为椭圆纤维化Mordell-Weil群秩的研究提供了新的理论框架和方向。

Abstract: We present two proofs for a bound on the rank of the Mordell-Weil group of some elliptic fibrations. The bounds apply to Calabi-Yau varieties, which are also of interest to the physics of string theory. We prove explicit bounds for Calabi-Yau threefolds, as predicted by physics, and give new explicit bounds for fourfolds under mild assumptions. These results motivate a conjecture for bounds in any dimensions.
