Method: 研究引入了五个基于聚并苯的紧束缚模型（tight-binding models），包括最常见的几何异构体顺式聚并苯（cis-polyacene）和反式聚并苯（trans-polyacene），以及三种经过修饰的聚并苯结构。通过分析这些结构的能带结构和拓扑特性，探究其拓扑性质差异。

Result: 尽管顺式和反式聚并苯的几何结构仅通过镜面对称性（mirror symmetry）区分，且具有相同的紧束缚能带结构，但它们的拓扑性质完全相反。反式聚并苯表现出非平凡拓扑相（nonzero winding number），而顺式聚并苯是拓扑平凡的。在三种修饰结构中，有两个观察到了奇异的拓扑行为。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了在满足相同对称性要求的条件下，几何结构的细微差异（如镜面对称性）可以导致完全相反的拓扑性质。这一发现扩展了对有机聚合物中拓扑现象的理解，并为通过结构修饰调控拓扑性质提供了新思路。

Abstract: The introduction of Su-Schrieffer-Heeger model has led to a major breakthrough in the area of one-dimensional topological insulators, even though this model was primarily formulated on an organic polymer called $trans$-polyacetylene in order to explain its anomalous conductivity. In this study, a group of five tight-binding models has been introduced which are formulated on another organic polymer called polyacene, where exotic topological behavior has been observed. Topological properties of the most common geometric isomers known as $cis$-polyacene, and $trans$-polyacene have been investigated along with three additional modified polyacene structures. Although their geometric structures differ by mirror symmetry, tight-binding band structures of $cis$-polyacene and $trans$-polyacene are found the same, where again their topological characters are found totally opposite. The $trans$-polyacene is nontrivial as it exhibits topological phase with nonzero winding number, while the $cis$-polyacene is topologically trivial, although both the structures adhere to the same set of symmetries required for the topological character. However, $cis$-polyacene possesses additional mirror symmetry in the real space. Three modified structures of polyacene have been considered in order to induce the nontrivial topology, where exotic topological behavior is noted in two of them.

### [110] [Micromotion area as proxy for anomalous Floquet topological systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25347)
*Luca Asteria,Klaus Sengstock,André Eckardt,Christof Weitenberg*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究为Floquet系统中的反常拓扑相（anomalous Floquet topology）提供了一种局域体态指标，通过测量初始局域粒子在驱动周期内扫过的面积来探测拓扑不变量（winding number）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 驱动Floquet系统可实现无静态对应物的拓扑相，但反常Floquet拓扑破坏了基于陈数（Chern number）的体边对应关系。目前缺乏类似于陈标记（Chern markers）的局域体态指标来表征Floquet系统的绕数（winding number）。

Method: 研究考虑两带模型（two-band models），分析初始局域粒子在Floquet周期内扫过的面积。在微运动（micromotion）中色散动力学被精细调节的点上，证明了面积的量子化特性。

Result: 当扫过的面积接近半晶胞面积时，信号指示反常相的存在。在色散动力学消失的精细调节点，面积被量子化且与绕数存在精确比例关系。研究还展示了实现任意高绕数的方法。

Conclusion: 该局域面积指标可在多种量子模拟平台中直接探测反常拓扑，适用于无序或相互作用系统。基于面积与绕数的关联，为实现高绕数拓扑相提供了新途径。

Abstract: Driven Floquet systems can realize topological phases with no static counterparts. These so-called anomalous Floquet topology breaks the bulk-boundary correspondence based on the Chern number. The number of edge modes in each band gap is instead determined by another integer index, a winding number, which is calculated from the time evolution operator of the bulk states within one driving period. While in the non-driven system, Chern markers provide a useful local proxy for the Chern number in the bulk, so far no such local bulk indicator is known for the winding number in Floquet systems. Here we consider two-band models and show that the area enclosed during a Floquet period by an initially localized particle signals the presence of an anomalous phase when it approaches half the unit cell area. In general, we show that at the fine-tuned point of dispersionless dynamics during the micromotion, the enclosed area is quantized and an exact proportionality relation exists between the area and the winding number. Direct detection of anomalous topology in real space could be realized in several quantum simulation platforms, and could be useful for systems with disorder or interactions. Building on the connection between area and winding number, we also show a way to realize arbitrarily high winding numbers.

### [111] [Correlation-Driven Orbital Order Realizes 2D Metallic Altermagnetism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25426)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究提出由电子关联（electronic correlations）和费米面嵌套（Fermi surface nesting）驱动的自发轨道有序（spontaneous orbital order）作为实现二维金属性交变磁体的通用路径。具体以单层YbMn₂Ge₂作为实例，通过反铁磁轨道有序（antiferro-orbital ordering）在dₓz和dᵧz轨道间打破相反自旋磁性子晶格的等价性，产生对称性强制的交变磁自旋纹理（symmetry-enforced altermagnetic spin texture）。

Conclusion: 研究确立了关联驱动轨道有序作为设计具有大自旋劈裂的关联交变磁体（correlated altermagnets）的稳健且通用机制，为二维自旋电子学材料设计提供了新途径。

Abstract: Two-dimensional metallic altermagnets are rare, and no correlated 2D material has been established to host large nonrelativistic spin splitting. Here we show that spontaneous orbital order, driven by electronic correlations and Fermi surface nesting, provides a general microscopic route to two-dimensional metallic altermagnetism. Antiferro-orbital ordering between the d$_{xz}$ and d$_{yz}$ orbitals breaks the equivalence of magnetic sublattices with opposite spins and generates a symmetry-enforced altermagnetic spin texture. As a concrete realization, we identify monolayer YbMn$_2$Ge$_2$ as a stable correlated metallic altermagnet exhibiting giant nonrelativistic spin splitting of order 1 eV. The resulting phase supports an exceptionally large and gate-tunable transverse spin conductivity. These results establish correlation-driven orbital order as a robust and general mechanism for designing correlated altermagnets with large spin splitting.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用张量网络（tensor networks）方法在实空间（real space）处理中间限域系统，以CdSe纳米片为例，该方法也适用于相关的二维系统（two-dimensional systems）。

Result: 计算了不同尺寸纳米片中激子（excitonic）和三子（trionic）的基态（ground states）及多个激发态（excited states），包括它们的能量和振子强度（oscillator strengths）。

Conclusion: 张量网络方法能够部分克服中间限域系统高维薛定谔方程的计算难题，更重要的是发展了在实空间使用张量网络处理中间限域系统的整体策略（overall strategies）。

Abstract: In semiconductor nanostructures, optical excitation typically creates bound electron-hole states, such as excitons, trions, and larger complexes. Their relative motion is described by the Wannier equation, which is valid only for spatially extended motion in the Coulomb-dominated, weak-confinement limit. Other small nanostructures, such as quantum dots, are in the confinement-dominated strong confinement regime, where the wavefunction factorizes into independent electron and hole parts. Nanoplatelets are in between the two regimes and require solving an unfactorized higher-dimensional Schrödinger equation, which is computationally expensive. This work demonstrates how tensor networks can partially overcome this problem, using CdSe nanoplatelets as an example. The method is also applicable to related two-dimensional systems. As a demonstration, we calculate the excitonic and trionic ground states, as well as several excited states, for nanoplatelets of varying sizes, including their energies and oscillator strengths. More importantly, overall strategies for using tensor networks in real space for systems under intermediate confinement have been developed.

### [113] [Topology of honeycomb nanoribbons revisited](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25497)
*Zebedeus F. Osseweijer,Lumen Eek,Harold J. W. Zandvliet,Pantelis Bampoulis,Cristiane Morais Smith*

Abstract: We present an in-depth study of end states in honeycomb nanoribbons, focusing on the interplay between nanoribbon termination, chiral symmetry, and complex next-nearest-neighbor hopping in the framework of the Haldane model. Although previous work has identified zero-dimensional end states in such systems, this analysis is incomplete. Here, we systematically investigate zigzag and armchair nanoribbons of various widths, using the multiband Zak phase to characterize the topological properties of the occupied bands. We show that the Zak phase is quantized only for certain ribbon terminations, and we elucidate how this termination dependence governs the existence and robustness of end states. Furthermore, we explore the effect of varying the complex next-nearest-neighbor hopping phase, demonstrating the breakdown of chiral symmetry, the evolution of the bulk gap, and the resulting depinning of end-state energies. Finally, we place our findings in the context of previous studies and discuss connections to the Kane-Mele model, including the role of Rashba spin-orbit coupling. Our work provides a more detailed analysis of topological end states in nanoribbons described by the Haldane and Kane-Mele models and offers a framework for their characterization in related systems.

### [114] [Puiseux series about exceptional singularities dictated by symmetry-allowed Hessenberg forms of perturbation matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25603)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米系统中高阶异常点的性质分析缺乏系统框架，需要建立统一的理论方法来理解不同对称性约束下异常点的奇异行为及其在传感器设计中的应用潜力。

Method: 在缺陷矩阵的约当标准基（Jordan-normal basis）中表达对称性保持扰动，分析扰动的上k-Hessenberg结构，通过Puiseux级数展开确定特征值和特征向量分裂的主导阶行为。

Result: 在宇称（P）和电荷共轭（C）对称的三带非厄米模型中，EP_3s最多表现为ε^{1/2}分支点；而宇称-时间反演（PT）对称系统通常支持最强奇异性的EP_3s（ε^{1/3}）。精细调谐的扰动可抑制主导阶分支点，实现更弱奇异性的分裂。

Conclusion: 该框架系统揭示了非厄米系统中异常点奇异性的结构决定机制，为设计基于异常点的方向依赖传感器提供了理论基础，并在四带模型中证实了EP_4s存在ε^{1/4}奇异性的可能性。

Abstract: We develop a systematic framework for determining the nature of exceptional points of $n^{\rm th}$ order (EP$_n$s) in non-Hermitian (NH) systems, represented by complex square matrices. By expressing symmetry-preserving perturbations in the Jordan-normal basis of the defective matrix at an EP$_n$, we show that the upper-$k$ Hessenberg structure of the perturbation directly dictates the leading-order eigenvalue- and eigenvector-splitting to be $\propto ε^{1/k}$, when expanded in a Puiseux series. Applying this to three-band NH models invariant under parity (P), charge-conjugation (C), or parity-time-reversal (PT), we find that EP$_3$s in P- and C-symmetric systems are restricted to at most $\sim ε^{1/2}$ branch points, while PT-symmetric systems generically support EP$_3$s with the strongest possible singularities (viz. $\sim ε^{1/3}$). We illustrate these results with concrete three-dimensional models in which exceptional curves and surfaces emerge. We further show that fine-tuned perturbations can suppress the leading-order branch point to a less-singular splitting, which have implications for designing direction-dependent EP-based sensors. The appendix extends the analysis to four-band C- and P-symmetric models, establishing the existence of EP$_4$s with $\sim ε^{1/4}$ singularities.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 安德森局域化（Anderson localization, AL）与非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect, NHSE）分别由无序（disorder）和非厄米性（non-Hermiticity）驱动。在一维非厄米系统中，这两种因素相互竞争，通过参数调节可实现AL到NHSE的平滑过渡。本研究旨在探索在自旋系统中，磁场作为额外自由度如何进一步丰富这种相互作用。

Method: 通过研究一维自旋非厄米无序链（disordered 1D spinful non-Hermitian chain），在自旋通道间采用适当关联的无序构型（correlated disorder configurations）下，分析磁场对局域行为的影响。采用逆参与率（inverse participation ratio）和平均质心（mean center of mass）作为分析工具。

Result: 研究发现，在自旋通道间存在关联无序构型时，磁场增强了AL到NHSE的交叉（crossover），甚至在强无序系统中也能促进安德森退局域化转变（Anderson delocalization transition）。通过分析揭示了无序、非厄米性和磁场强度之间的三重相互作用，识别了安德森局域化和趋肤积累（skin accumulation）的不同区域。

Conclusion: 磁场驱动的退局域化现象源于Zeeman效应诱导的自旋通道间链间耦合（inter-chain coupling），从而有效抑制了无序强度。这一发现丰富了非厄米系统中局域化现象的理解，揭示了磁场作为调控无序和非厄米性相互作用的新机制。

Abstract: Anderson localization (AL) and the non-Hermitian skin effect (NHSE) represent two paradigmatic localization phenomena driven, respectively, by disorder and non-Hermiticity. In one-dimensional (1D) non-Hermitian systems, these factors are known to compete and provide a smooth crossover between AL and NHSE upon parameter tuning. Here, we show that this interplay is fundamentally enriched in spinful systems, where an external magnetic field acts as an additional degree to manipulate the localization behavior. By investigating a disordered 1D spinful non-Hermitian chain, we demonstrate that under appropriately correlated disorder configurations across spin sectors, the magnetic field enhances the AL $\rightarrow$ NHSE crossover. Interestingly, this facilitates the Anderson delocalization transition even in strongly disordered systems where states would otherwise be Anderson localized. By analyzing the inverse participation ratio and the mean center of mass, we map the resulting triple interplay between disorder, non-Hermiticity, and the magnetic field strength, identifying regimes of Anderson localization and skin accumulation. We further reveal that this magnetic field driven delocalization phenomenon originates from an effective suppression of disorder strength via Zeeman-induced inter-chain coupling across the spin sectors.

</details>


### [116] [Anomalous thermoelectric Hall response of interacting 2D Dirac fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25705)
*A. Daria Dumitriu-I.,Feng Liu,Alexander E. Kazantsev,Alessandro Principi*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究分析了二维有质量狄拉克费米子（massive Dirac fermions）在电子-电子相互作用（electron-electron interaction）一阶近似下的反常热电霍尔响应（anomalous thermoelectric Hall response），发现即使在零温极限下热电霍尔系数也不为零，这归因于量子场论中不可避免的最小尺度上的局域性破坏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维有质量狄拉克费米子体系中电子-电子相互作用对反常热电霍尔响应的影响，特别关注零温极限下的行为是否与预期相符。

Method: 计算了两种响应：对Luttinger型引力势（Luttinger-type gravitational potential）的能斯特响应（Nernst response）以及粒子磁化强度（particle magnetization），后者用于消除虚假的非输运贡献。

Result: 发现对于任意相互作用，磁化强度可由一个异常简单的公式描述；令人惊讶的是，减去磁化电流后热电霍尔系数在零温极限下并不为零，这与预期相反。

Conclusion: 零温极限下热电霍尔系数非零的现象归因于量子场论中不可避免的最小尺度上的局域性破坏（violation of locality），这种破坏在红外物理中显现出来。

Abstract: We study the anomalous thermoelectric Hall response of two-dimensional massive Dirac fermions to first order in the electron-electron interaction. We compute both the Nernst response to a Luttinger-type gravitational potential and the particle magnetization, the latter being required to remove spurious non-transport contributions. We show that, for arbitrary interactions, the magnetization is described by a remarkably simple formula. Surprisingly, and contrary to expectations, subtracting the magnetization currents does not make the thermoelectric Hall coefficient vanish in the zero-temperature limit. We attribute this to violation of locality on the smallest length scales, which is inevitable in a quantized field theory, that happens to manifest itself in infrared physics.

</details>

### [117] [The Born Rule as the Unique Refinement-Stable Induced Weight on Robust Record Sectors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24619)
*Marko Lela*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在可容许希尔伯特记录层内，关于鲁棒记录扇区上诱导权重的条件结构唯一性定理。不同于标准玻恩规则路径，该定理将可加性置于不相交可容许延拓丛上，而非完整投影格上，从而获得扇区层面的可加律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于建立一种不同于标准玻恩规则（Born rule）路径的唯一性定理，该定理不依赖于完整投影格上的可加性，而是基于可容许延拓结构上的丛可加性来诱导扇区权重。

Method: 方法采用可容许延拓丛上的扩展丛赋值（extensive bundle valuation），从不相交可容许延拓丛的可加性继承扇区层面的可加律。通过两个明确的结构条件：可容许二元细化剖面的内部等价性（internal equivalence）和充分的可容许细化丰富性（refinement richness），建立唯一性结果。

Result: 在可容许二元饱和（admissible binary saturation）确保细化丰富性的条件下，二次赋值（quadratic assignment）是鲁棒记录扇区上唯一的非负细化稳定诱导权重。补充命题表明，若添加剖面函数连续性条件，则稠密可容许饱和已足够。

Conclusion: 该定理并非格列森型表示定理（Gleason-type representation theorem）的不同表述，而是关于从丛可加性在可容许延拓结构上诱导的扇区权重的独特唯一性定理。在归一化条件下，结果简化为标准玻恩赋值（Born assignment）。

Abstract: This paper proves a conditional structural uniqueness theorem for induced weight on robust record sectors within an admissible Hilbert record layer. Its theorem target and additive carrier differ from those of the standard Born-rule routes: additivity is not placed on the full projector lattice, but on disjoint admissible continuation bundles through an extensive bundle valuation, from which the sector-level additive law is inherited under admissible refinement. Accordingly, the result is not a Gleason-type representation theorem in different language, but a distinct uniqueness theorem about induced sector weight inherited from bundle additivity on admissible continuation structure. Under two explicit structural conditions, internal equivalence of admissible binary refinement profiles and sufficient admissible refinement richness, the quadratic assignment is the only non-negative refinement-stable induced weight on robust record sectors. In the main theorem, refinement richness is secured by admissible binary saturation. A supplementary proposition shows that dense admissible saturation already suffices if continuity of the profile function is added. Under normalization, the result reduces to the standard Born assignment.

</details>


### [118] [Causality is rare: some topological properties of causal quantum channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25315)
*Robin Simmons*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明在量子场论中，因果性通道（causal channels）在局域性通道（local channels）集合中是处处不稠密的（nowhere dense），且因果性幺正算符（causal unitaries）在所有幺正算符集合中的哈尔测度（Haar measure）为零，揭示了因果性约束的极端严格性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Sorkin不可能操作（Sorkin's impossible operations）表明量子场论中量子通道的因果性（causality）是超越通道局域性（locality）的额外约束。然而文献尚未阐明这种约束的严格程度，本文旨在量化这一约束强度。

Method: 通过数学分析证明因果性通道在局域性通道集合中的拓扑性质，并建立与量子信息理论的联系，分析因果性幺正算符在幺正算符集合中的测度特性。

Result: 因果性通道在局域性通道集合中是处处不稠密的，且因果性幺正算符在所有作用于格点的幺正算符集合中的哈尔测度为零，表明因果性约束极其严格。

Conclusion: 因果性约束在量子场论中具有极端严格性，这一结果与近期量子场论测量模型（QFT measurement models）存在重要联系和启示。

Abstract: Sorkin's impossible operations demonstrate that causality of a quantum channel in QFT is an additional constraint on quantum operations above and beyond the locality of the channel. What has not been shown in the literature so far is how much of a constraint it is. Here we answer this question in perhaps the strongest possible terms: the set of causal channels is nowhere dense in the set of local channels. We connect this result to quantum information, showing that the set of causal unitaries has Haar measure $0$ in the set of all unitaries acting on a lattice. Finally, we close with discussion on the implications and connections to recent QFT measurement models.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先重新阐述测量问题，然后分析物质与辐射场（radiation field）相互作用的大系综（large ensembles）中态平均的耗散性质，证明其对应于个体系统的随机时间演化（stochastic time-evolution）。最后在双缝实验（double-slit experiment）的理想化模型中勾勒解决方案。

Result: 研究表明量子力学时间演化中的耗散性质对应于个体系统状态的随机演化，并强调了耗散对于成功完成测量的重要性。在双缝实验的理想化模型中提出了测量问题的解决方案框架。

Conclusion: 通过分析量子力学时间演化中的耗散性质及其与随机演化的对应关系，论文在双缝实验的理想化模型中为量子力学的测量问题提供了一个解决方案的框架，突出了耗散在测量过程中的关键作用。

Abstract: This note starts with a recapitulation of what people call the ``Measurement Problem'' of Quantum Mechanics (QM). The dissipative nature of the quantum-mechanical time-evolution of averages of states over large ensembles of identical isolated systems consisting of matter interacting with the radiation field is discussed and shown to correspond to a stochastic time-evolution of states of individual systems. The importance of dissipation for the successful completion of measurements is highlighted. To conclude, a solution of the ``Measurement Problem'' is sketched in an idealized model of a double-slit experiment.

### [120] [Analytical Solutions of One-Dimensional ($1\mathcal{D}$) Potentials for Spin-0 Particles via the Feshbach-Villars Formalism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25375)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在系统研究一维Feshbach-Villars方程在代表性外部势场下的解，为相对论性标量束缚态提供统一的分析框架和基准结果。

Method: 从Klein-Gordon方程的Feshbach-Villars表述出发，推导对应的一维主方程，并分析其在多种势场下的解。对奇异势场采用Loudon型截断正则化处理，对平滑势场则直接分析其谱特性。

Result: 库仑势在截断极限下呈现预期的近简并偶-奇结构；Cornell势产生有限束缚态集；幂指数势给出本质相对论性谱；Pöschl-Teller和Woods-Saxon势分别展示了确定宇称和空间不对称性的影响。

Conclusion: 研究为相对论性标量束缚态提供了一套连贯的解析和数值基准，揭示了不同势场下相对论效应的特征，并与非相对论极限进行了系统比较。

Abstract: We present a unified analytical and numerical study of the one-dimensional Feshbach--Villars (FV) equation for spin-0 particles in the presence of several representative external potentials. Starting from the FV formulation of the Klein--Gordon equation, we derive the corresponding one-dimensional master equation and analyse its solutions for Coulomb, power-exponential, Cornell, Pöschl--Teller, and Woods--Saxon interactions. For the singular Coulomb and Cornell cases, a Loudon-type cutoff regularisation is implemented on the full line, allowing a mathematically controlled treatment of the origin and an explicit classification of the states by parity. The Coulomb problem exhibits the expected near-degenerate even--odd structure in the cutoff limit, while the Cornell potential combines short-distance Coulomb behaviour with long-distance confinement and produces a finite set of bound states for fixed parameters. The power-exponential potential with $p=1$ is reduced to a Whittaker-type equation and yields an intrinsically relativistic spectrum with no standard Schrödinger bound-state limit in the parameter regime considered. For the smooth short-range Pöschl--Teller and Woods-Saxon potentials, the FV formalism reveals, respectively, the effects of definite parity and spatial asymmetry on the spectrum, wave functions, and particle--antiparticle mixing. In all cases, we reconstruct the full FV spinor, analyse the associated charge density, and compare the relativistic behaviour with the corresponding non-relativistic expectations whenever such a limit exists. The results provide a coherent set of analytical and numerical benchmarks for relativistic scalar bound states in one dimension.

### [121] [Nonperturbative Resummation of Divergent Time-Local Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25512)
*Dragomir Davidovic*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究针对开放量子系统中时间局域生成元（time-local generators）在长时间尺度上发散的问题，通过解析延拓构建了非微扰动力学映射（nonperturbative dynamical maps）。研究以弱耦合无偏自旋-玻色子模型（weak-coupling unbiased spin-boson model）为例，展示了如何从发散生成元重构约化动力学，并揭示了发散信号与约化动力学不可逆性（noninvertibility）临界点之间的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放量子系统的时间局域生成元在长时间尺度上通常发散，尽管约化动力学本身保持正则性。这种发散现象需要被理解并处理，以建立从发散生成元重构约化动力学的非微扰框架。

Method: 通过解析延拓（analytic continuation）构建与发散生成元一致的非微扰动力学映射。在弱耦合无偏自旋-玻色子模型中，该方法实现了对TCL生成元（TCL generator）的非微扰重求和（nonperturbative resummation）。重构的映射通过TEMPO模拟在短时间尺度验证，并与精确可解的旋转波模型（rotating-wave model）在所有时间尺度对比。

Result: 在完整自旋-玻色子模型中，连续机制同时产生早期各向异性（early-time anisotropy）和晚期奇异性（late-time singularity）。早期各向异性包含可测量的相移，反映了环境关联和指针方向；晚期奇异性则标志约化动力学变得不可逆。相比之下，旋转波模型中的映射接近但未达到该奇点，在所有时间保持可逆性。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了从发散时间局域生成元重构约化动力学的非微扰框架，能够诊断不可逆性的出现，并识别环境诱导各向异性的实验可观测早期特征。这些结果为处理开放量子系统中生成元发散问题提供了系统方法。

Abstract: Time-local generators of open quantum systems are generically divergent at long times, even though the reduced dynamics remains regular. We construct, by analytic continuation, nonperturbative dynamical maps consistent with these generators. For the weak-coupling unbiased spin--boson model, this construction yields an explicit dynamical map that nonperturbatively resums the TCL generator and exposes how the divergences signal the approach to a singular time at which the reduced dynamics becomes noninvertible. The reconstructed map is validated against TEMPO simulations at short times and the exactly solvable rotating-wave model at all times. In the full spin--boson model, the same continuum mechanism produces both an early-time anisotropy, with a measurable phase shift that provides a signature of the environmental correlation and the pointer direction, and a late-time singularity at which the reduced dynamics becomes noninvertible. By contrast, in the rotating-wave model the map approaches this point without reaching it and remains invertible at all times. These results establish a nonperturbative framework for reconstructing reduced dynamics from divergent time-local generators, diagnosing the onset of noninvertibility, and identifying experimentally accessible early-time signatures of environment-induced anisotropy.

</details>


### [122] [Provably Efficient Long-Time Exponential Decompositions of Non-Markovian Gaussian Baths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25708)
*Zhen Huang,Zhiyan Ding,Ke Wang,Jason Kaye,Xiantao Li,Lin Lin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文严格界定了高斯浴（Gaussian bath）非马尔可夫环境模拟的复杂度，证明了对于广泛的光谱密度（spectral density）类别，所需指数函数数量与最大模拟时间T无关，实现了时间均匀复杂度（time-uniform complexity）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高斯浴广泛用于模拟非马尔可夫环境，但长时间精确模拟的成本仍不清楚，特别是在光谱密度呈现非解析行为时，如一系列现实模型中的情况。需要理解模拟复杂度对时间、温度和光谱密度奇异性的依赖关系。

Method: 通过严格界定在时间区间[0,T]上使用复指数和表示浴相关函数（bath correlation function）的复杂度，该方法应用于赝模（pseudomode）和分层运动方程（hierarchical equations of motion）方法的变体中。

Result: 对于广泛的光谱密度类别，所需指数函数数量与最大模拟时间T无关，实现了时间均匀复杂度。仅当光谱密度具有强奇异性（如阶跃不连续性和逆幂律发散）时，T依赖性才以多对数因子形式出现。温度依赖性对玻色环境温和，对费米环境完全消失。

Conclusion: 长时间模拟的真正瓶颈不是模拟持续时间本身，而是浴谱中尖锐的非解析特征的存在。这些结果对非马尔可夫开放量子系统的长时间模拟以及具有记忆核的经典广义朗之万方程（generalized Langevin equations）的马尔可夫嵌入具有指导意义。

Abstract: Gaussian baths are widely used to model non-Markovian environments, yet the cost of accurate simulation at long times remains poorly understood, especially when spectral densities exhibit nonanalytic behavior as in a range of realistic models. We rigorously bound the complexity of representing bath correlation functions on a time interval $[0,T]$ by sums of complex exponentials, as employed in recent variants of pseudomode and hierarchical equations of motion methods. These bounds make explicit the dependence on the maximal simulation time $T$, inverse temperature $β$, and the type and strength of singularities in an effective spectral density. For a broad class of spectral densities, the required number of exponentials is bounded independently of $T$, achieving time-uniform complexity. The $T$-dependence emerges only as polylogarithmic factors for spectral densities with strong singularities, such as step discontinuities and inverse power-law divergences. The temperature dependence is mild for bosonic environments and disappears entirely for fermionic environments. Thus, the true bottleneck for long-time simulation is not the simulation duration itself, but rather the presence of sharp nonanalytic features in the bath spectrum. Our results are instructive both for long-time simulation of non-Markovian open quantum systems, as well as for Markovian embeddings of classical generalized Langevin equations with memory kernels.

</details>


### [123] [The Pareto Frontiers of Magic and Entanglement: The Case of Two Qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24902)
*Alexander Roman,Marco Knipfer,Jogi Suda Neto,Konstantin T. Matchev,Katia Matcheva,Sergei Gleyzer*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究分析了两比特系统中魔法（magic）与纠缠（entanglement）的相互作用，重点关注给定纠缠水平下的最大和最小魔法值，并推导了相应的解析公式和量子态参数化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 魔法（magic）和纠缠（entanglement）是两种广泛用于表征量子资源的度量。研究旨在探索两比特系统中这两种量子资源之间的相互作用关系，特别关注给定纠缠水平下的极端情况。

Method: 使用二阶Rényi熵$M_2$量化魔法，使用并发度（concurrence）$Δ$量化纠缠。通过分析最大魔法$M_2^{(max)}(Δ)$和最小魔法$M_2^{(min)}(Δ)$的边界，研究两比特系统中这两种度量的关系。

Result: 发现最大魔法的帕累托前沿（Pareto frontier）$M_2^{(max)}(Δ)$由三个独立段组成，而最小魔法边界$M_2^{(min)}(Δ)$是单一连续线。为所有四种情况推导了简单解析公式，并明确参数化了给定纠缠水平下所有不同的最大或最小魔法量子态。

Conclusion: 研究系统刻画了两比特系统中魔法与纠缠的相互作用边界，提供了完整的解析描述和量子态参数化，为理解这两种量子资源的关系提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Magic and entanglement are two measures that are widely used to characterize quantum resources. We study the interplay between magic and entanglement in two-qubit systems, focusing on the two extremes: maximal magic and minimal magic for a given level of entanglement. We quantify magic by the Rényi entropy of order 2, $M_2$, and entanglement by the concurrence $Δ$. We find that the Pareto frontier of maximal magic $M_2^{(max)}(Δ)$ is composed of three separate segments, while the boundary of minimal magic $M_2^{(min)}(Δ)$ is a single continuous line. We derive simple analytical formulas for all these four cases, and explicitly parametrize all distinct quantum states of maximal or minimal magic at a given level of entanglement.

</details>


### [124] [Implementing non-Abelian Hatano-Nelson model in electric circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24642)
*Xiangru Chen,Jien Wu,Xingyu Chen,Zhenhang Pu,Yejian Hu,Jiuyang Lu,Manzhu Ke,Weiyin Deng,Zhengyou Liu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种具有非互易U(2)规范场的非阿贝尔Hatano-Nelson模型，在电路中实现了霍普链状复能谱编织和双极趋肤效应，丰富了非厄米物理的实验研究。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前非厄米（non-Hermitian）物理的实验探索主要集中于人工系统，且仅关注无规范场或阿贝尔（Abelian）规范场的系统。需要研究非阿贝尔（non-Abelian）规范场下的非厄米现象。

Method: 提出了一种具有非互易U(2)规范场的非阿贝尔Hatano-Nelson模型。该模型在电路中实现，通过规范场诱导两种非厄米现象：霍普链状复能谱编织和双极趋肤效应。

Result: 在电路中观测到霍普链状导纳谱（Hopf-link-shaped admittance spectra）和双极趋肤导纳模式（bipolar skin admittance modes）。规范场诱导了独特的谱拓扑结构和非厄米趋肤效应。

Conclusion: 该工作丰富了实验非厄米物理的研究范畴，为设计多功能非厄米器件提供了一种新方法。非阿贝尔规范场为探索复杂谱拓扑和非厄米现象开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian systems generally host complex spectra that bring unique spectral topologies, leading to the spectral braiding and non-Hermitian skin effect. The experimental exploration of non-Hermitian physics is mainly concentrated in artificial systems due to the flexibility in the introduction of the non-Hermiticity, but to date has focused only on the systems without gauge fields or with Abelian gauge fields. Here, we propose a non-Abelian Hatano-Nelson model with a nonreciprocal U(2) gauge field. The gauge field induces two non-Hermitian phenomena: the first is the Hopf-link-shaped complex energy braiding, and the second is the bipolar skin effect arising under the non-Abelian condition. The non-Abelian Hatano-Nelson model is implemented in electric circuits, and the Hopf-link-shaped admittance spectra and bipolar skin admittance modes are observed. Our work enriches the experimental non-Hermitian physics, and provides an approach to designing multifunctional non-Hermitian devices.

### [125] [Inequality for Strong-Weak Spontaneous Symmetry Breaking in Fermionic Open Quantum systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24671)
*Abhijat Sarma,Cenke Xu*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文证明了一个不等式，表明退相干（decoherence）驱动的费米子量子物质趋向于U(1)对称性的强弱自发对称破缺（SW-SSB），其中Rényi-2关联函数可作为诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 初始高斯（自由费米子）态在退相干作用下演化为非高斯混合态，通常无法精确求解。需要研究退相干对费米子量子物质对称性破缺的影响。

Method: 通过不等式证明，退相干费米子态的Rényi-2关联函数类被作为强弱自发对称破缺（SW-SSB）近似诊断的Rényi-2关联函数上界约束。

Result: 该不等式对任意退相干强度均成立，表明退相干驱动费米子量子物质趋向于U(1)对称性的强弱自发对称破缺（SW-SSB）。

Conclusion: 研究建立了该不等式与其他主题的联系，包括投影量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（projected quantum spin Hall insulator）和狄拉克自旋液体态（Dirac spin liquid states）。

Abstract: Under decoherence, an initial Gaussian (free-fermion) state evolves into a non-Gaussian mixed state, so the resulting decohered fermionic state is not exactly solvable in general. We show through an inequality that a class of Rényi-2 correlators of the decohered fermion state are upper-bounded by the Rényi-2 correlator serving as a proximate diagnostic of strong-weak spontaneous symmetry breaking (SW-SSB) of the charge-U(1) symmetry. This inequality holds for arbitrary decoherence strength and suggests that decoherence drives fermionic quantum matter toward U(1) SW-SSB. We also make connections between our inequality and other subjects such as projected quantum spin Hall insulator and Dirac spin liquid states.

### [126] [Explicit States with Two-sided Long-Range Magic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25023)
*Zhi Li*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文构建了具有"双侧长程魔力"的显式量子态，这些态无法通过任意顺序的Clifford电路和有限深度局域幺正电路制备，从而证明它们位于魔力层次结构的第一级之外。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非稳定化性（nonstabilizerness）或魔力（magic）是实现超越经典可模拟Clifford框架的量子优势的必要资源。近期研究开始探索多体态中魔力的结构，引入了长程魔力（long-range magic）和魔力层次结构（magic hierarchy）的概念。

Method: 作者构建了显式态，包括"魔力猫态"（magical cat state）$|ψ\rangle \propto |0^n\rangle + |+^n\rangle$以及某些非阿贝尔拓扑序（nonabelian topological orders）的基态，这些态被证明具有双侧长程魔力（two-sided long-range magic）。

Result: 这些态无法通过任意顺序的Clifford电路和有限深度局域幺正电路（finite-depth local unitary circuits）制备，从而被证明位于魔力层次结构的第一级之外。这为电路复杂性（circuit complexity）提供了新的示例和证明技术。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了长程魔力、多体相结构（structure of many-body phases）和量子纠错原理（principles of quantum error correction）之间的内在联系，为理解量子优势的资源特性提供了新视角。

Abstract: Nonstabilizerness, or magic, is a necessary resource for quantum advantage beyond the classically simulatable Clifford framework. Recent works have begun to chart the structure of magic in many-body states, introducing the concepts of long-range magic -- nonstabilizerness that cannot be removed by finite-depth local unitary (FDU) circuits -- and the magic hierarchy, which classifies quantum circuits by alternating layers of Clifford and FDUs. In this work, we construct explicit states that provably possess two-sided long-range magic, a stronger form of magic meaning that they cannot be prepared by a Clifford circuit and a FDU in either order, thus placing them provably outside the first level of the magic hierarchy. Our examples include the ``magical cat" state, $|ψ\rangle \propto |0^n\rangle + |+^n\rangle$, and ground states of certain nonabelian topological orders. These results provide new examples and proof techniques for circuit complexity, and in doing so, reveal the connection between long-range magic, the structure of many-body phases, and the principles of quantum error correction.

</details>


### [127] [Neural Operator Quantum State: A Foundation Model for Quantum Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25066)
*Zihao Qi,Christopher Earls,Yang Peng*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出神经算子量子态（Neural Operator Quantum State, NOQS）作为量子动力学的基础模型，能够学习将整个驱动协议映射到时演化量子态的解算子，实现单次前向传播预测未见协议的动力学演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法如张量网络和时依赖神经量子态需要为每个驱动协议重新运行模拟，这限制了量子多体系统在时依赖驱动协议下动力学模拟的效率。

Method: 提出神经算子量子态（NOQS）方法，通过训练学习薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）的解算子（solution operator），将整个驱动协议映射到时演化量子态，而非求解单个轨迹。

Result: 在二维伊辛模型（Ising model）上验证了NOQS的准确性，不仅能够预测未见分布内协议，还能预测分布外不同函数形式的驱动协议；单个模型可在不同时间分辨率间迁移，并能通过稀疏实验测量高效微调。

Conclusion: NOQS为量子动力学模拟引入了新范式，并为驱动量子系统提供了实用的计算-实验接口，实现单次前向传播预测未见协议演化而无需额外优化。

Abstract: Capturing the dynamics of quantum many-body systems under time-dependent driving protocols is a central challenge for numerical simulations. Existing methods such as tensor networks and time-dependent neural quantum states, however, must be re-run for every protocol. In this work, we introduce the Neural Operator Quantum State (NOQS) as a foundation model for quantum dynamics. Rather than solving the Schrödinger equation for individual trajectories, our approach aims to \emph{learn the solution operator} that maps entire driving protocols to time-evolved quantum states. Once trained, the NOQS predicts time evolution under unseen protocols in a single forward pass, requiring no additional optimization. We validate NOQS on the two-dimensional Ising model with time-dependent longitudinal and transverse fields, demonstrating accurate prediction not only for unseen in-distribution protocols, but also for qualitatively different, out-of-distribution functional forms of driving. Further, a single NOQS model can be transferred between different temporal resolutions, and can be efficiently fine-tuned with sparse experimental measurements to improve predictions across all observables at negligible cost. Our work introduces a new paradigm for quantum dynamics simulation and provides a practical computational-experimental interface for driven quantum systems.

</details>


### [128] [Optimal measurement-based quantum thermal machines in a finite-size system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25128)
*Chinonso Onah,Obinna Uzoh,Obinna Abah*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于测量的量子热机，利用耦合二能级系统作为工作介质，通过广义量子测量的反作用提取功。研究推导了优化标准并开发了数值算法，展示了在投影测量极限下的效率峰值、对称破缺扩大可利用能隙，以及在反馈脉冲误差下的鲁棒性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用耦合二能级系统作为工作介质，构建三冲程测量基引擎循环（three-stroke measurement-based engine cycle）。开发了两种数值算法来优化引擎功提取并提升其性能，工作介质采用类伊辛相互作用的耦合二能级系统。

Result: 数值结果表明：(1)在投影测量极限（projective-measurement limit）下出现效率峰值；(2)对称破缺（symmetry breaking）（失谐或弱耦合）扩大了可利用能隙（exploitable energy gap）；(3)在约10度反馈脉冲误差下性能保持鲁棒（>50%最优值）。

Conclusion: 该测量基量子热机框架具有平台无关性，可直接在当前超导、囚禁离子或核磁共振技术中实现，为可扩展的测量驱动量子热机提供了具体实现路径。

Abstract: We present a measurement-based quantum thermal machine that extracts work from the back-action of generalized quantum measurements whose working medium is a coupled two-level quantum system. Specifically, we derive universal optimization criteria for a three-stroke measurement-based engine cycle with coupled two-level system of Ising-like interaction as a working medium. Furthermore, we present two numerical algorithms to optimize the engine work extraction and enhance its performance. Our numerical results demonstrate: (i) efficiency peaks in the projective-measurement limit; (ii) symmetry breaking (detuning or weak coupling) enlarges the exploitable energy gap; and (iii) performance remains robust ($>50\%$ of optimum) under $\sim\!10^\circ$ feedback-pulse errors. The framework is platform-agnostic and directly implementable with current superconducting, trapped-ion, or NMR technologies, providing a concrete route to scalable, measurement-powered quantum thermal machines.

### [129] [Epitaxial CeO2 Films as a Host for Quantum Applications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25234)
*Pralay Paul,Kusal M. Abeywickrama,Nisha Geng,Mritunjaya Parashar,Levi Brown,Mohin Sharma,Darshpreet Kaur Saini,Melissa Ayala Artola,Todd A. Byers,Bibhudutta Rout,Yiwei Ju,Xiaoqing Pan,Sumit Goswami,Sreehari Puthan Purayil,Casey Kerr,Dhiman Biswas,Ben Summers,Bin Wang,Horst Hahn,Alisa Javadi,T. Venkatesan*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了CeO2作为零核磁矩宿主材料在量子应用中的潜力，通过PLD生长高质量薄膜并掺杂Tm和Er离子，发现Er掺杂CeO2具有更长的发光寿命，揭示了电子结构对非辐射复合通道的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在高纯度宿主中，量子发射体的相干性最终受限于发射体与具有非零核磁矩的晶格核之间的超精细相互作用（hyperfine interactions），这一限制只能通过同位素纯化来缓解。本研究探索CeO2作为完全由零核磁矩核组成的宿主材料的潜力。

Method: 采用脉冲激光沉积（PLD）生长高质量CeO2薄膜并掺杂Tm和Er离子。通过X射线衍射、原子力显微镜和离子沟道进行结构表征，确认单晶、原子级平滑的薄膜以及掺杂剂在Ce晶格位置的替代性掺入。进行光致发光寿命测量，并通过密度泛函理论（DFT）计算分析电子结构。

Result: Er掺杂CeO2的光致发光寿命（2.9-5.3 ms）显著长于Tm掺杂薄膜（14-68 μs）。在约1%掺杂浓度下，PLD生长的Er掺杂薄膜比先前报道的MBE生长薄膜具有更长的寿命。DFT计算显示未占据的O 2p态与Tm 4f态在价带最大值附近存在显著重叠，而Er 4f态保持良好隔离。

Conclusion: Tm掺杂CeO2中O 2p与Tm 4f态的电子相互作用可能引入了非辐射复合通道，解释了寿命降低的原因。这些发现强调了选择适当的掺杂剂-宿主组合和优化生长条件对于最小化量子应用中的非辐射通道的重要性。

Abstract: In highly purified host, the coherence of quantum emitters is ultimately limited by hyperfine interactions between the emitter and lattice nuclei possessing non-zero nuclear magnetic moments. This limitation can only be mitigated through isotopic purification. In this work, we investigate CeO2 as a host composed entirely of nuclei with zero nuclear moment. High-quality CeO2 thin films were grown by PLD and doped with Tm and Er ions. Structural characterization using X-ray diffraction, atomic force microscopy, and ion channeling confirms single-crystalline, atomically smooth films with dopants substitutionally incorporated at Ce lattice sites. Photoluminescence lifetime measurements show significantly longer lifetimes for Er-doped CeO2 (2.9 - 5.3 ms) compared with Tm-doped films (14 - 68 μs). Moreover, the Er-doped PLD films exhibit longer lifetimes at ~1% dopant concentration than previously reported for MBE-grown films. Density functional theory calculations reveal a substantial overlap between unoccupied O 2p and Tm 4f states near the valence band maximum, whereas Er 4f states remain well isolated. This electronic interaction likely introduces non-radiative recombination pathways in Tm-doped CeO2, explaining the reduced lifetimes. These findings highlight the importance of selecting appropriate dopant-host combinations and optimized growth conditions to minimize non-radiative channels for quantum applications.

### [130] [A derivation of the late-time volume law for local operator entanglement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25387)
*Guilherme Ilário Correr,John Goold,Marco Cattaneo*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过推导混沌系统中局部算符纠缠（LOE）的晚期表达式，展示了其体积律标度行为，并在一维混合场伊辛模型中进行数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局部算符纠缠（Local Operator Entanglement, LOE）已成为多体系统中量子混沌的指标。尽管数值研究显示混沌系统中LOE随时间线性增长并在晚期呈现体积律行为，但对其体积律涌现的完整解析理解仍然不足。

Method: 方法包括在刘维尔本征态基中表达晚期LOE，并基于三个主要假设：哈密顿量本征能的高阶非共振条件、初始局部算符矩阵元素的本征态热化假设（Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis, ETH）形式，以及在LOE最终表达式中用随机态替换哈密顿量本征态。

Result: 在这些假设下，作者获得了显示体积律标度的显式公式。通过一维混合场伊辛模型（1D mixed-field Ising model）的数值模拟，验证了所得公式并探索了假设的有效性范围。

Conclusion: 本文为混沌系统中局部算符纠缠体积律行为的解析理解做出了贡献，提供了明确的公式表达并通过数值模拟验证了理论推导的有效性。

Abstract: Local Operator Entanglement (LOE) has emerged an indicator of quantum chaos in many-body systems. Numerical studies have shown that, in chaotic systems, LOE grows linearly in time and displays a volume-law behavior at late times, scaling proportionally with the number of local degrees of freedom. Despite extensive numerical evidence, complemented by analytical studies in integrable systems, a fully analytical understanding of the emergence of the volume law remains incomplete. In this paper, we contribute toward this goal by deriving a late-time expression for LOE in chaotic systems that exhibits volume-law scaling. Our derivation proceeds by expressing the late-time LOE in the Liouville eigenstate basis and relies on three main assumptions: a higher-order non-resonance condition for the Hamiltonian eigenenergies, the Eigenstate Thermalization Hypothesis (ETH) ansatz for the matrix elements of the initial local operator, and the replacement of Hamiltonian eigenstates with random states in the final expression for LOE. Under these assumptions, we obtain an explicit formula displaying volume-law scaling. Finally, we complement our analytical derivation with numerical simulations of the 1D mixed-field Ising model, testing the resulting formula and exploring the regime of validity of our assumptions.

</details>

### [131] [Lattice and PT symmetries in tensor-network renormalization group: a case study of a hard-square lattice gas model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25492)
*Xinliang Lyu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在二维张量网络重整化群（TNRG）方法中纳入晶格对称性（反射与旋转）和PT对称性的方案，并通过硬方格晶格气体模型验证了该方法的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 张量网络重整化群（TNRG）是研究相变的重要数值方法，但目前主要适用于U(1)、SU(2)等全局在位对称性。对于晶格对称性和PT对称性在TNRG中的处理尚不完善，需要发展更全面的对称性纳入方案。

Method: 通过在粗粒化张量网络中正确定义晶格对称性（反射与旋转）和PT对称性，提出了一种能够纳入这些对称性的TNRG方案。以具有最近邻排斥的硬方格晶格气体（hard-square lattice gas）模型作为案例研究，该模型包含两个连续相变且对称性破缺涉及晶格和PT对称性。

Result: 通过估计模型两个相变的临界参数和标度维度（scaling dimensions），验证了所提方法的有效性。该方法使二维TNRG成为一个更完善的数值方法。

Conclusion: 本文的技术发展使二维张量网络重整化群方法能够更全面地处理包括晶格对称性和PT对称性在内的各类对称性，提升了该方法在研究连续相变中的应用范围。

Abstract: The tensor-network renormalization group (TNRG) is an accurate numerical real-space renormalization group method for studying phase transitions in both quantum and classical systems. Continuous phase transitions, as an important class of phase transitions, are usually accompanied by spontaneous breaking of various symmetries. However, the understanding of symmetries in the TNRG is well-established mainly for global on-site symmetries like U(1) and SU(2). In this paper, we demonstrate how to incorporate lattice symmetries (including reflection and rotation) and the PT symmetry in the TNRG in two dimensions (2D) through a case study of the hard-square lattice gas with nearest-neighbor exclusion. This model is chosen because it is well-understood and has two continuous phase transitions whose spontaneously-broken symmetries are lattice and PT symmetries. Specifically, we write down proper definitions of these symmetries in a coarse-grained tensor network and propose a TNRG scheme that incorporates these symmetries. We demonstrate the validity of the proposed method by estimating the critical parameters and the scaling dimensions of the two phase transitions of the model. The technical development in this paper has made the 2D TNRG a more well-rounded numerical method.

### [132] [Optimal threshold resetting in collective diffusive search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25338)
*Arup Biswas,Satya N Majumdar,Arnab Pal*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究阈值重置（threshold resetting）策略在N个非相互作用扩散搜索者的一维盒子中的目标搜索问题。通过优化缩放阈值距离u，显著降低了平均首次通过时间，并识别了临界种群大小N_c(u)和最优种群大小N_opt(u)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机重置（stochastic resetting）研究通常基于外部计时器，与系统内在动力学解耦。本文引入阈值重置作为事件驱动的优化策略，将重置机制直接耦合到内部动力学，为复杂随机搜索过程提供更高效的优化机制。

Method: 研究N个非相互作用扩散搜索者在一维盒子[0,L]中的阈值重置搜索，目标位于原点，阈值设在L处。通过优化缩放阈值距离u = x_0/L，分析平均首次通过时间（mean first-passage time）的降低效果。

Result: 当N ≥ 2时，通过优化u可显著降低平均首次通过时间。识别了临界种群大小N_c(u)，低于该值时阈值重置优于无重置动力学。对于固定u，平均首次通过时间随N呈非单调变化，在N_opt(u)处达到最小值。量化了可实现的加速效果并分析了TR的操作成本。

Conclusion: 阈值重置作为复杂随机搜索过程的高效且现实的优化机制，展现出非平凡的优化景观。这些发现强调了事件驱动重置策略在优化随机搜索性能方面的重要性。

Abstract: Stochastic resetting has attracted significant attention in recent years due to its wide-ranging applications across physics, biology, and search processes. In most existing studies, however, resetting events are governed by an external timer and remain decoupled from the system's intrinsic dynamics. In a recent Letter by Biswas et al, we introduced threshold resetting (TR) as an alternative, event-driven optimization strategy for target search problems. Under TR, the entire process is reset whenever any searcher reaches a prescribed threshold, thereby coupling the resetting mechanism directly to the internal dynamics. In this work, we study TR-enabled search by $N$ non-interacting diffusive searchers in a one-dimensional box $[0,L]$, with the target at the origin and the threshold at $L$. By optimally tuning the scaled threshold distance $u = x_0/L$, the mean first-passage time can be significantly reduced for $N \geq 2$. We identify a critical population size $N_c(u)$ below which TR outperforms reset-free dynamics. Furthermore, for fixed $u$, the mean first-passage time depends non-monotonically on $N$, attaining a minimum at $N_{\mathrm{opt}}(u)$. We also quantify the achievable speed-up and analyze the operational cost of TR, revealing a nontrivial optimization landscape. These findings highlight threshold resetting as an efficient and realistic optimization mechanism for complex stochastic search processes.

</details>


### [133] [Non-linear Sigma Model for the Surface Code with Coherent Errors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25665)
*Stephen W. Yan,Yimu Bao,Sagar Vijay*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究通过推导非线性σ模型分析表面码（surface code）在相干误差下的最大似然解码，揭示了最优解码与次优解码在复制极限下的本质区别，发现次优解码存在"热金属"（thermal-metal）相这一新的不可解码区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面码作为量子存储器具有潜力，但其在相干误差下的阈值尚未完全理解。研究旨在分析表面码在单量子比特幺正旋转（single-qubit unitary rotations）产生电任意子激发（electric anyon excitations）情况下的解码性能。

Method: 从微观推导出目标空间为$\mathrm{SO}(2n)/\mathrm{U}(n)$的非线性σ模型（non-linear sigma model），作为解码问题的有效长程理论。采用两种复制极限：$n\to1$对应已知旋转角度的最优解码，$n\to0$对应角度信息不完善的次优解码。

Result: 两种解码器存在显著差异：次优解码支持"热金属"相（thermal-metal phase），这是一种与不相干泡利误差下传统不可解码相本质不同的不可解码区域。最优解码中金属相不稳定，可能支持最大相干旋转角度下的解码。解码保真度与序参量场的扭结缺陷（twist defects）相关。

Conclusion: 研究通过数值模拟验证了分析预测，并讨论了σ模型的对称性和目标空间对表面码晶格的依赖性。当综合征位于非二分晶格（non-bipartite lattice）时，最优解码中也可能出现稳定的热金属相。

Abstract: The surface code is a promising platform for a quantum memory, but its threshold under coherent errors remains incompletely understood. We study maximum-likelihood decoding of the square-lattice surface code in the presence of single-qubit unitary rotations that create electric anyon excitations. We microscopically derive a non-linear sigma model with target space $\mathrm{SO}(2n)/\mathrm{U}(n)$ as the effective long-distance theory of this decoding problem, with distinct replica limits: $n\to1$ for optimal decoding, which assumes knowledge of the coherent rotation angle, and $n\to0$ for suboptimal decoding with imperfect angle information. This exposes a sharp distinction between the two decoders. The suboptimal decoder supports a ``thermal-metal'' phase, a non-decodable regime that is qualitatively distinct from the conventional non-decodable phase of the surface code under incoherent Pauli errors. By contrast, the metal phase cannot arise in optimal decoding, since the metallic fixed-point becomes unstable in the $n\to 1$ replica limit. We argue that optimal decoding may be possible up to the maximally-coherent rotation angle. Within the sigma model description, we show that the decoding fidelity is related to twist defects of the order-parameter field, yielding quantitative predictions for its system-size dependence near the metallic fixed point for both decoders. We examine our analytic predictions for the decoding fidelity as well as other physical observables with extensive numerical simulations. We discuss how the symmetries and the target space for the sigma model rely on the lattice of the surface code, and how a stable thermal metal phase can arise in optimal decoding when the syndromes reside on a non-bipartite lattice.

</details>

### [134] [The Symmetric Perceptron: a Teacher-Student Scenario](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25440)
*Giovanni Catania,Aurélien Decelle,Suhanee Korpe*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究引入并求解了对称二元感知机（symmetric binary Perceptron）的师生（teacher-student）表述，将其从传统的存储导向模型转变为具有保证解的植入式推理问题。通过退火和淬火自由熵计算，在三个控制参数（样本密度α、对称超平面距离κ和温度T）下绘制相图，揭示了学习过程中由二阶不稳定性创建教师相关亚稳态，随后通过一阶跃迁实现完全对齐的组织结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统对称感知机主要关注存储能力，本研究旨在将其转变为具有保证解的植入式推理问题（planted inference problem）。通过引入师生表述，将标签纳入两个区域，从而创建可分析的学习场景。

Method: 采用对称二元感知机的师生表述，在无噪声示例下分析贝叶斯最优（Bayes-optimal）机制，并在两种不同势函数/分类规则下研究热噪声效应。使用高维极限下的退火（annealed）和淬火（quenched）自由熵计算来绘制相图。

Result: 在三个控制参数（样本密度α、对称超平面距离κ和温度T）下绘制了相图。识别出一种稳健的学习场景：学习过程由二阶不稳定性组织，该不稳定性创建教师相关（teacher-correlated）的亚最优状态，随后通过一阶跃迁（first-order transition）实现完全对齐（full alignment）。

Conclusion: 该结构依赖于势函数的选择，亚最优解的亚稳态性（metastability）与其向植入配置（planted configuration）熔解之间的相互作用，这对基于蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）的优化算法具有重要意义。

Abstract: We introduce and solve a teacher-student formulation of the symmetric binary Perceptron, turning a traditionally storage-oriented model into a planted inference problem with a guaranteed solution at any sample density. We adapt the formulation of the symmetric Perceptron which traditionally considers either the u-shaped potential or the rectangular one, by including labels in both regions. With this formulation, we analyze both the Bayes-optimal regime at for noise-less examples and the effect of thermal noise under two different potential/classification rules. Using annealed and quenched free-entropy calculations in the high-dimensional limit, we map the phase diagram in the three control parameters, namely the sample density $α$, the distance between the origin and one of the symmetric hyperplanes $κ$ and temperature $T$, and identify a robust scenario where learning is organized by a second-order instability that creates teacher-correlated suboptimal states, followed by a first-order transition to full alignment. We show how this structure depends on the choice of potential, the interplay between metastability of the suboptimal solution and its melting towards the planted configuration, which is relevant for Monte Carlo-based optimization algorithms.

</details>


### [135] [Krylov-space anatomy and spread complexity of a disordered quantum spin chain](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25724)
*Bikram Pain,David E. Logan,Sthitadhi Roy*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过Krylov空间分析量子态结构，发现Krylov扩展复杂度（spread complexity）能清晰区分遍历相（ergodic phase）与多体局域相（MBL phase），前者复杂度随Fock空间维度线性增长，后者呈亚线性增长。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索无序相互作用自旋链中量子态在Krylov空间的结构与复杂度，特别是在遍历相和多体局域相（many-body localised phase）中的差异。Krylov基由哈密顿量从初始态生成，为衡量量子态复杂度提供了基优化的度量框架。

Method: 研究方法基于Krylov空间表示，通过哈密顿量从初始态生成Krylov基，分析时间演化态在该基上的扩展行为。采用Krylov扩展复杂度（spread complexity）作为核心度量，并通过对本征态扩展复杂度统计的大偏差分析（large-deviation analysis）来深入探究相变特征。

Result: 研究结果显示，长时间Krylov扩展复杂度能显著区分两个相：在遍历相中，无限时间复杂度随Fock空间维度线性增长，表明态扩展至Krylov链的有限部分；而在MBL相中呈亚线性增长，意味着长时间态仅占据链的消失部分。MBL相中无限时间态沿Krylov链的分布呈现拉伸指数衰减（stretched-exponential decay），反映了不同本征态贡献的衰减长度尺度分布广泛。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，Krylov扩展复杂度是区分遍历相和MBL相的有效序参量。本征态扩展复杂度的统计大偏差分析进一步证实：遍历相几乎包含所有本征态的贡献，而MBL相的复杂度主要由消失部分的本征态主导，这些本征态相对于典型本征态具有异常大的复杂度。

Abstract: We investigate the anatomy and complexity of quantum states in Krylov space, in the ergodic and many-body localised (MBL) phases of a disordered, interacting spin chain. The Krylov basis generated by the Hamiltonian from an initial state provides a representation in which the spread of the time-evolving state constitutes a basis-optimised measure of complexity. We show that the long-time Krylov spread complexity sharply distinguishes the two phases. In the ergodic phase, the infinite-time complexity scales linearly with the Fock-space dimension, indicating that the state spreads over a finite fraction of the Krylov chain. By contrast, it grows sublinearly in the MBL phase, implying that the long-time state occupies only a vanishing fraction of the chain. Further, the profile of the infinite-time state along the Krylov chain exhibits a stretched-exponential decay in the MBL phase. This behaviour reflects a broad distribution of decay lengthscales, associated with different eigenstates contributing to the long-time state. Consistently, a large-deviation analysis of the statistics of eigenstate spread complexities shows that while the ergodic phase receives contributions from almost all eigenstates, the complexity in the MBL phase is dominated by a vanishing fraction of eigenstates, which have anomalously large complexity relative to the typical ones.

</details>

Method: 利用电场驱动手性向列相液晶中的斯格明子，通过挠曲电效应（flexoelectric effect）实现指向矢场（director field）形变，从而控制斯格明子在二维平面内的运动轨迹和速度。

Result: 电场能够驱动斯格明子沿预先编程的轨迹在二维平面内以可变速度运动。该效应源于形变指向矢场的挠曲电极化（flexoelectric polarization）。

Abstract: Design of soft matter capable of controllable microscale dynamics is a frontier of modern science. Jiahao Chen et al. demonstrate that an electric field can drive particle-like solitons-skyrmions in a chiral nematic along a preprogrammed trajectory with a variable speed within a two-dimensional plane. The effect is rooted in flexoelectric polarization of a deformed director field.

### [137] [Classification of interfacial water governed by water-polymer interactions in hydrated polymers: A molecular dynamics simulation study of ethylene-based and acrylate polymers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25198)
*Atsuki Hashimoto,Kokoro Shikata,Kang Kim,Nobuyuki Matubayasi*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 通过分子动力学模拟研究了七种含水聚合物的水合结构与动力学，揭示了三种水合类型：高水合型（PVA、PHEA、PHEMA）、疏水型（PMEMA、PBA）和柔性水合型（PEG、PMEA），为理解水-聚合物相互作用控制的界面水提供了分子层面框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究不同聚合物中水合结构与动力学的分子机制，特别是水含量对玻璃化转变温度（glass transition temperature）$T_g$的影响、聚合物链波动、水-聚合物功能基团间氢键寿命（hydrogen-bond lifetimes）以及受限水的局域化与交换动力学。

Method: 采用分子动力学模拟（molecular dynamics simulations）分析七种含水聚合物：PVA、PHEA、PHEMA、PBA、PMEMA、PEG和PMEA。通过四个视角整合分析：$T_g$的水含量依赖性、二面角分布表征的聚合物链波动、水与聚合物功能基团间氢键寿命$τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$，以及van Hove相关函数（van Hove correlation function）的独特部分量化的受限水局域化与交换动力学。

Result: 含羟基聚合物（PVA、PHEA、PHEMA）表现出较高的干态$T_g$值，水合后显著降低；链波动受限，$τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$遵循Arrhenius行为，形成局域化水合壳。PMEMA和PBA显示低平衡水含量和疏水特性；干态$T_g$值中等且对水含量不敏感，链波动小，$τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$也遵循Arrhenius行为，疏水聚集促进水局域化。PEG和PMEA干态$T_g$值低且水含量依赖性弱；醚或甲氧基氧原子周围更大的旋转自由度导致更大的链波动和松散结合水，低于$T_g$时水与醚或甲氧基氧原子间$τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$表现出超Arrhenius行为。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了三种水合类型：高水合型（PVA、PHEA、PHEMA）、疏水型（PMEMA、PBA）和柔性水合型（PEG、PMEA），为解释由水-聚合物相互作用控制的界面水提供了分子层面框架。

Abstract: We perform molecular dynamics simulations to investigate hydration structures and dynamics in seven water-containing polymers: PVA, PHEA, PHEMA, PBA, PMEMA, PEG, and PMEA. The analysis integrates four perspectives: the water-content dependence of the glass transition temperature $T_g$, polymer chain fluctuations characterized by dihedral angle distributions, hydrogen-bond lifetimes $τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$ between water and polymer functional groups, and the localization and exchange dynamics of confined water quantified by the distinct part of van Hove correlation function. Hydroxyl-containing polymers (PVA, PHEA, and PHEMA) exhibit relatively high dry-state $T_g$ values and its pronounced depression upon hydration. Chain fluctuations are limited, and $τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$ follows Arrhenius behavior, forming localized hydration shells. In contrast, PMEMA and PBA show low equilibrium water contents and hydrophobic character; although their dry-state $T_g$ values are moderately lower and less sensitive to water content, chain fluctuations remain small, and $τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$ also obeys Arrhenius behavior, with hydrophobic aggregation promoting water localization. PEG and PMEA display low dry-state $T_g$ values and weak water-content dependence. Greater rotational freedom around ether or methoxy oxygen atoms leads to larger chain fluctuations and loosely bound water. Below $T_g$, $τ_{\mathrm{HB}}$ between water and ether or methoxy oxygen atoms exhibits super-Arrhenius behavior. These results clarify three hydration types: highly hydrated (PVA, PHEA, and PHEMA), hydrophobic (PMEMA and PBA), and flexibly hydrated (PEG and PMEA), and provide a molecular-level framework for interpreting interfacial water governed by water-polymer interactions.

### [138] [Mapping the limits of equilibrium in sheared granular liquid crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25252)
*Jacopo Bilotto,Martin Trulsson,Jean-François Molinari*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了非热（athermal）细长颗粒在致密颗粒流中的取向动力学，发现无摩擦颗粒在充分剪切后进入准平衡态，其取向统计可由经典液晶理论描述，而摩擦引入则导致系统远离平衡态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 细长颗粒在粘性流体剪切中遵循Jeffery轨道已广为人知，但在致密颗粒流中是否存在类似轨道尚不明确。本文旨在探究非热细长颗粒在致密颗粒流中的取向行为，特别是摩擦对系统平衡态的影响。

Method: 通过剪切足够长时间的无摩擦细长颗粒棒，研究其取向动力学。引入颗粒间摩擦以观察系统从准平衡态向远离平衡态的转变，并使用有效Ericksen数（effective Ericksen number）量化非平衡旋转驱动与空间有序的对比。

Result: 无摩擦细长颗粒棒在充分剪切后进入准平衡态，其取向统计可由经典液晶理论定量描述，噪声来源于剪切引起的碰撞。然而，在低长径比（aspect ratio）和引入颗粒间摩擦时，这种平衡类比出现系统性破坏：低长径比时平衡理论错误预测各向同性态；摩擦引入使系统从空间屏蔽（steric screening）转向摩擦传动（frictional gearing）。

Conclusion: 研究结果提供了致密驱动系统中从准平衡态向远离平衡稳态转变的定量图谱，界定了热液晶理论在非热物质中的适用范围。摩擦导致的破坏直接与系统被驱动远离平衡态相关，有效Ericksen数可作为量化这一转变的关键参数。

Abstract: Athermal elongated particles are well-known to follow Jeffery orbits when sheared in viscous fluids. It is less clear if similar orbits appear in dense granular flows. We show that when sheared for long enough, sufficiently elongated frictionless granular rods, rather than following noisy Jeffery-like orbits, exist in a quasi-equilibrium state, whose orientational statistics are quantitatively described by classical liquid crystal theory, where the noise is provided by collisions due to shear. At the same time, we demonstrate a systematic breakdown of this equilibrium analogy at two distinct limits: at low aspect ratios, where the equilibrium theory incorrectly predicts an isotropic state, and as inter-particle friction is introduced, where the system moves from steric screening to frictional gearing. Even within this frictionally geared state, the rotational dynamics remain distinct from classical Jeffery orbits. We link this frictional breakdown directly to the system being driven far from equilibrium, as quantified by an effective Ericksen number that compares non-equilibrium rotational driving to steric ordering. Our results provide a quantitative map of the transition from a quasi-equilibrium to a far-from-equilibrium steady state in a dense, driven system, defining the limits of applicability for thermal liquid crystal theory in athermal matter.

</details>


### [139] [Identifying the Threshold Chain Length for Stress Overshoot in Ring-Linear Polymer Blends under Uniaxial Elongation: The Role of Multiple Threading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25505)
*Takahiro Murashima,Katsumi Hagita,Toshihiro Kawakatsu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环形-线性聚合物共混物在单轴拉伸流中的流变行为，特别是应力过冲现象的出现机制，一直是激烈争论的课题，需要深入理解其链长依赖性。

Method: 采用粗粒化分子动力学模拟研究等分子量柔性链1:1环形-线性共混物的拉伸粘度链长依赖性，通过缠结数Z = N/Ne量化穿线程度。

Result: 研究发现了应力过冲出现的明确阈值：短链共混物(Z≤2)呈现单调应力增长，当链长达到阈值(Z≈4)时出现明显应力过冲。该过冲源于穿线-脱线转变，在阈值链长下多个线性链穿透单个环形链，提供足够拓扑约束使环形链在拉伸流中显著伸展。

Conclusion: 该转变可通过拉伸方向和垂直方向平面内的二维小角中子散射图案进行实验验证，为环形链回缩过程提供直接结构特征，可供未来实验验证。

Abstract: The rheological behavior of ring-linear polymer blends under uniaxial elongational flow has remained a subject of intense debate, particularly regarding the emergence of stress overshoot. Herein, we employ coarse-grained molecular dynamics simulations to investigate the chain-length dependence of elongational viscosity in 1:1 ring-linear blends of flexible chains with the equal molecular weight. Our results reveal a distinct threshold in the degree of threading, quantified by the number of entanglements Z = N /Ne (where N is the number of beads per chain and Ne is the entanglement chain length), for the appearance of stress overshoot: while blends with shorter chains (Z $\le$ 2) exhibit monotonic stress growth, a clear stress overshoot emerges when the chain length reaches a threshold value (Z $\approx$ 4). Consistent with previous reports, this overshoot originates from a thread-to-unthread transition. At the threshold chain length, multiple linear chains penetrate a single ring, providing sufficient topological constraints to significantly stretch the ring under elongational flow. We predict that this transition can be experimentally validated via 2D small-angle neutron scattering patterns in the plane of the stretching and perpendicular directions, offering a direct structural signature of the ring recoil process for future experimental verification.

### [140] [Entropic phase separation in polymer--vitrimer melts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25532)
*A. A. Rispo Constantinou,B. Magyari,G. Ianniruberto,E. van Ruymbeke,D. J. Read*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文开发了适用于缔合型（associative）玻璃态聚合物（vitrimer）的自由能模型，并通过分子动力学模拟验证其准确性。研究发现，即使在没有组分间能量相互作用的情况下，此类熔体仍会发生相分离，且相图与解离型（dissociative）系统定性相似。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统塑料需要在耐久性（热固性塑料）和可再加工性（热塑性塑料）之间做出选择。玻璃态聚合物（vitrimers）作为一类新型聚合物网络，兼具这两种特性。然而，将其与传统热塑性塑料混合时，相分离会导致材料不均匀，需要建立相应的理论模型来理解这一现象。

Method: 本文调整了现有的解离型（dissociative）聚合物网络自由能模型，使其适用于缔合型（associative）玻璃态聚合物（vitrimer）体系。通过将模型预测结果与新颖的分子动力学（molecular-dynamics）模拟结果进行比较，验证了模型的准确性。

Result: 研究发现，即使在没有组分间能量相互作用的情况下，此类熔体仍会发生相分离。相图与解离型（dissociative）系统定性相似，且相分离开始的临界转化度（critical degree of conversion）与每个玻璃态聚合物链上的功能位点数量成反比关系。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了适用于玻璃态聚合物混合体系的自由能模型，揭示了其相分离行为的基本规律。该模型为理解玻璃态聚合物与传统热塑性塑料混合时的相分离现象提供了理论框架，有助于优化此类材料的配方设计。

Abstract: Traditional plastics demand a choice between durability (thermosets) and reprocessability (thermoplastics). Vitrimers are a recent class of polymer network combining both these qualities. Their increased cost of production can be offset by mixing them with a traditional thermoplastic; however, phase separation in such blends can lead to inhomogenous materials. In this paper, we adapt an existing model for the free energy of dissociative polymer networks to their associative, vitrimeric counterpart. We test the accuracy of the model's predictions by comparing them with the results of novel molecular-dynamics simulations. We demonstrate that such melts can undergo phase separation even in the absence of energetic interactions between the components. We find furthermore that the phase diagram of the melts is qualitatively similar to that of dissociative systems, and that the critical degree of conversion for the onset of phase separation depends reciprocally on the number of function sites per vitrimer chain.

</details>


### [141] [Dissolution of a two-component drop onto macrophase due to surface tension effect](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25588)
*Alexey Kabalnov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视并扩展了针对奥斯特瓦尔德熟化（Ostwald ripening）的稳定化模型，分析了双组分液滴在过量拉普拉斯压力（Laplace pressure）作用下的溶解过程，提出了覆盖整个配方范围的改进溶解速率方程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微溶组分添加剂已知能减缓或完全抑制分散系统中的奥斯特瓦尔德熟化。本文旨在重新审视并扩展先前针对奥斯特瓦尔德熟化的稳定化模型，使其覆盖整个组成范围、组分摩尔体积及其活度系数。

Method: 分析双组分液滴在过量拉普拉斯压力作用下的溶解问题，识别溶解的三个阶段：预锁定（pre-lock-in）、锁定状态（lock-in state）和晚期锁定（late lock-in）。提出改进的溶解速率方程，覆盖整个配方范围。

Result: 研究发现，当难溶组分初始浓度超过特定阈值时，溶解动力学几乎遵循经典立方定律（classical cubic law）。改进的溶解速率方程扩展了先前公式，能够描述整个溶解过程中的浓度变化和动力学行为。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了更全面的双组分液滴溶解模型，揭示了锁定机制在稳定化过程中的关键作用，提出的改进方程为理解添加剂抑制奥斯特瓦尔德熟化的机制提供了更完善的理论框架。

Abstract: Additives of sparingly soluble components are known to slow down or completely inhibit Ostwald ripening in dispersed systems. In this paper series, our earlier model of the stabilization against Ostwald ripening is revisited and extended over the whole range of compositions, molar volumes of components, and their activity coefficients. In the first paper, a simpler problem, the dissolution of a two-component drop under the action of excess Laplace pressure inside is analyzed. Three stages of dissolution are identified. In the first stage, called pre-lock-in, the concentration of the poorly soluble component undergoes a quick increase, and the system enters the lock-in state, in which the Laplace pressure effect on the chemical potential of the more soluble component is nearly completely counterbalanced by the Raoult effect. After this, the dissolution kinetics slows down and enters a steady state. In the process, the concentration of the sparingly soluble component continues to increase, first slowly and then more rapidly in the very end of the particle lifetime; this latter stage is called the 'late lock-in'. Despite all those variations, if the initial concentration of the poorly soluble component is above a certain threshold, the dissolution kinetics nearly follows the classical cubic law. An improved equation for the rate of dissolution is proposed that covers the whole formulation range and represents an extension over our previous formula.

### [142] [How unconstrained machine-learning models learn physical symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24638)
*Michelangelo Domina,Joseph William Abbott,Paolo Pegolo,Filippo Bigi,Michele Ceriotti*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种测量机器学习模型中对称性内容的严格度量方法，并建立了诊断谱失效模式的框架。研究表明，通过战略性地注入最小必要归纳偏置，可以在保持无约束架构高表达性和可扩展性的同时保证物理保真度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理模拟的机器学习模型通常需要精确满足基本对称性，但无约束模型（unconstrained models）常表现出竞争性性能，并能通过简单数据增强策略学习到近似等变行为。需要建立严格度量来评估此类模型中学习表示（learned representations）的对称性内容。

Method: 引入严格度量（rigorous metrics）来测量学习表示中的对称性内容，并评估输出满足等变条件（equivariant condition）的准确性。将这些度量应用于两个基于Transformer的无约束模型：用于原子模拟的图神经网络（graph neural network）和用于粒子物理的PointNet风格架构（PointNet-style architecture），研究对称性信息如何在架构层间处理及在训练中学习。

Result: 基于这些洞察，建立了诊断机器学习模型中谱失效模式（spectral failure modes）的严格框架。通过该分析证明，通过战略性地注入最小必要归纳偏置（minimum required inductive biases），可以实现更优的稳定性和准确性，同时保持无约束架构的高表达性和可扩展性。

Conclusion: 研究展示了在保持无约束架构优势的同时保证物理保真度的可行路径，通过最小必要归纳偏置的战略注入，实现了表达性、可扩展性与物理准确性的平衡。

Abstract: The requirement of generating predictions that exactly fulfill the fundamental symmetry of the corresponding physical quantities has profoundly shaped the development of machine-learning models for physical simulations. In many cases, models are built using constrained mathematical forms that ensure that symmetries are enforced exactly. However, unconstrained models that do not obey rotational symmetries are often found to have competitive performance, and to be able to \emph{learn} to a high level of accuracy an approximate equivariant behavior with a simple data augmentation strategy. In this paper, we introduce rigorous metrics to measure the symmetry content of the learned representations in such models, and assess the accuracy by which the outputs fulfill the equivariant condition. We apply these metrics to two unconstrained, transformer-based models operating on decorated point clouds (a graph neural network for atomistic simulations and a PointNet-style architecture for particle physics) to investigate how symmetry information is processed across architectural layers and is learned during training. Based on these insights, we establish a rigorous framework for diagnosing spectral failure modes in ML models. Enabled by this analysis, we demonstrate that one can achieve superior stability and accuracy by strategically injecting the minimum required inductive biases, preserving the high expressivity and scalability of unconstrained architectures while guaranteeing physical fidelity.

*Yuda Bi,Chenyu Zhang,Qiheng Wang,Vince D Calhoun*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该研究为理解延迟泛化现象（grokking）提供了可检验的有限尺寸相变框架，通过将群阶p作为广延变量、谱头尾对比作为序参量，应用凝聚态物理诊断方法证实了相变描述的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 延迟泛化现象（grokking）通常用相变语言描述，但缺乏可证伪的有限尺寸输入。本研究旨在提供这些输入，使相变描述从类比提升为可定量检验的有限尺寸主张。

Method: 将群阶p作为可接受的广延变量，将保留的谱头尾对比作为表示层面的序参量，应用凝聚态物理风格的诊断链，包括粗网格扫描和密集近临界加法审计。

Result: 类Binder交叉揭示了共享的有限尺寸边界，敏感性比较强烈反对平滑交叉解释（近临界审计中ΔAIC=16.8）。相变语言在延迟泛化现象中可作为定量有限尺寸主张进行检验。

Conclusion: 延迟泛化现象中的相变语言可以作为定量有限尺寸主张进行检验，而不仅仅是类比，尽管目前相变阶数仍未解决。

Abstract: Grokking -- the delayed onset of generalization after early memorization -- is often described with phase-transition language, but that claim has lacked falsifiable finite-size inputs. Here we supply those inputs by treating the group order $p$ of $\mathbb{Z}_p$ as an admissible extensive variable and a held-out spectral head-tail contrast as a representation-level order parameter, then apply a condensed-matter-style diagnostic chain to coarse-grid sweeps and a dense near-critical addition audit. Binder-like crossings reveal a shared finite-size boundary, and susceptibility comparison strongly disfavors a smooth-crossover interpretation ($Δ\mathrm{AIC}=16.8$ in the near-critical audit). Phase-transition language in grokking can therefore be tested as a quantitative finite-size claim rather than invoked as analogy alone, although the transition order remains unresolved at present.

### [144] [When Is Collective Intelligence a Lottery? Multi-Agent Scaling Laws for Memetic Drift in LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24676)
*Hidenori Tanaka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该研究揭示了基于大语言模型的多智能体系统中共识形成的微观机制，通过量化单纯形闲谈模型解释了采样驱动的模因漂移如何导致群体极化，并预测了从漂移主导到选择主导的交叉转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管基于大语言模型（LLMs）的多智能体系统越来越多地应用于重要决策场景，但其结果究竟反映集体推理、系统偏见还是随机性仍不清楚。近期命名游戏研究表明，即使个体智能体没有先验偏好，群体也能迅速达成共识，需要揭示其微观机制。

Method: 研究引入了最小模型——量化单纯形闲谈（Quantized Simplex Gossip, QSG），其中智能体保持内部信念状态但相互学习采样输出。通过类比中性进化，将这种采样驱动机制称为模因漂移（memetic drift），并推导了极化行为的标度律。

Result: QSG模型预测了从漂移主导（共识如彩票）到选择主导（弱偏见被放大）的交叉转变。研究推导了极化行为随群体规模、通信带宽、上下文适应率和智能体内部不确定性的标度律，并在QSG模拟和LLM命名游戏实验中验证了这些预测。

Conclusion: 这些结果为研究多智能体系统中社会表征形成的集体机制提供了理论框架，揭示了采样驱动的模因漂移如何作为共识形成的微观起源，并量化了不同参数对群体极化行为的影响。

Abstract: Multi-agent systems powered by large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in settings that shape consequential decisions, both directly and indirectly. Yet it remains unclear whether their outcomes reflect collective reasoning, systematic bias, or mere chance. Recent work has sharpened this question with naming games, showing that even when no individual agent favors any label a priori, populations rapidly break symmetry and reach consensus. Here, we reveal the mechanism by introducing a minimal model, Quantized Simplex Gossip (QSG), and trace the microscopic origin of this agreement to mutual in-context learning. In QSG, agents maintain internal belief states but learn from one another's sampled outputs, so one agent's arbitrary choice becomes the next agent's evidence and can compound toward agreement. By analogy with neutral evolution, we call this sampling-driven regime memetic drift. QSG predicts a crossover from a drift-dominated regime, where consensus is effectively a lottery, to a selection regime, where weak biases are amplified and shape the outcome. We derive scaling laws for drift-induced polarization as a function of population size, communication bandwidth, in-context adaptation rate, and agents' internal uncertainty, and we validate them in both QSG simulations and naming-game experiments with LLM populations. Together, these results provide a framework for studying the collective mechanisms of social representation formation in multi-agent systems.

</details>

### [145] [Mapping cone Thom forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25087)
*Hao Zhuang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为光滑闭2-形式（smooth closed 2-form）诱导的de Rham映射锥上链复形构造显式的Mathai-Quillen型映射锥Thom形式，该形式携带由2-形式带来的额外信息。

Method: 方法基于映射锥协变导数，该导数携带了2-形式引入的额外信息。主要工具是Berezin积分，用于显式构造映射锥Thom形式。

Result: 主要结果表明：该Thom形式相对于映射锥微分（mapping cone differentiation）是闭的；沿纤维的积分结果为1；并且满足横截公式（transgression formula）。

Conclusion: 本文成功构造了满足闭性、归一化条件和横截公式的映射锥Thom形式，为de Rham映射锥理论提供了具体的几何实现。

Abstract: For the de Rham mapping cone cochain complex induced by a smooth closed 2-form, we explicitly write down the associated mapping cone Thom form in the sense of Mathai-Quillen. Our construction uses the mapping cone covariant derivative, carrying the extra information brought by the 2-form. Our main tool is the Berezin integral. As the main result, we show that this Thom form is closed with respect to the mapping cone differentiation, its integration along the fiber is 1, and it satisfies the transgression formula.

### [146] [Robust topological BIC nanocavities for upconversion directional emission](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25050)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 这项工作建立了一个在纳米尺度上工程化相干定向光发射的通用框架，为高性能芯片级集成纳米光子应用奠定了坚实基础。该策略为精确操控单粒子光-物质相互作用提供了新途径，具有重要的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Photonic bound states in the continuum (BICs) provide a revolutionary paradigm for boosting light-matter interactions in integrated nanocavity systems. Nevertheless, precise manipulation of open cavity-emitter architectures still faces critical challenges, especially in realizing deterministic directional radiation and suppressing the perturbation of intrinsic cavity modes induced by emitters as local impurities. Conventional investigations on cavity-emitter coupling are predominantly based on ensemble measurements, which inevitably mask the intrinsic physics underlying individual light-matter interactions. Here, we propose a robust strategy to control the upconversion and emission of a single-particle emitter using a topological plasmonic cavity with broken σh mirror symmetry. This structured design enables the transition from symmetry-protected BICs to a multi-BIC regime with finite but ultrahigh confinement, where nontrivial phase evolution and hybridization of transverse electric and magnetic modes open a well-defined far-field radiation channel for directional emission. Leveraging this scheme, we experimentally demonstrate dramatically enhanced radiation intensity from a single point-like emitter, together with uniform and deterministic directional emission, while achieving excellent structural robustness against local perturbations. This work establishes a general framework for engineering coherent directional light emission at the nanoscale, which lays a solid foundation for high-performance chip-scale integrated nanophotonic applications.

### [147] [WKB for semiclassical operators: How to fly over caustics (and more)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25601)
*San Vũ Ngoc*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文对Maslov-WKB方法进行了统一的微局部分析处理，利用微局层论方法严格证明了单自由度半经典算子的Bohr-Sommerfeld-Einstein-Brillouin-Keller量子化条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Wentzel-Kramers-Brillouin（WKB）方法在寻找薛定谔方程近似解时在焦散（caustics）处失效，Maslov提出了克服这一困难的简单推广。本文旨在利用现代微局部分析（microlocal analysis）进展，为这一广义Maslov-WKB方法提供统一的理论框架。

Method: 采用微局层论方法（microlocal sheaf-theoretic approach），对广义Maslov-WKB方法进行统一处理。该方法基于近期微局部分析的进展，为半经典算子（包括伪微分算子和Berezin-Toeplitz算子）提供严格的数学框架。

Abstract: The method initiated by Wentzel, Kramers, and Brillouin to find approximate solutions to the Schrödinger equation lies at the origin of the spectacular development of microlocal and semiclassical analysis. When used naively, the approach appears to break down at caustics, but Maslov showed how a simple generalization could overcome this difficulty. In this paper, after a partial historical review, we take advantage of more recent advances in microlocal analysis to present a unified treatment of this generalized Maslov-WKB method, using a microlocal sheaf-theoretic approach. This framework provides a rigorous proof of the Bohr Sommerfeld Einstein Brillouin Keller quantization conditions for the eigenvalues of general semiclassical operators (pseudodifferential and Berezin Toeplitz) in one degree of freedom. We also review some applications and extensions.

### [148] [Interfacial Permeability, Reflectivity and Preferential Internal Mixing of Phase-Separated Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25447)
*Oihan Joyot,Zoé Ferrand,Fernando Muzzopappa,Pierre Weiss,Fabian Erdel*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个理论与实验框架，用于量化生物分子凝聚体（biomolecular condensates）界面传输的两个关键参数：偏置界面反射率（biased interfacial reflectivity）和界面阻力（interfacial resistance），揭示了这些参数如何影响凝聚体内部的优先混合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生物分子凝聚体通过空间浓缩分子来组织生化过程，但其界面传输可能显著衰减，导致增强的滞留和优先内部混合。量化描述这种行为的两个关键机制——偏置界面反射率和界面阻力——在实验上一直具有挑战性。

Method: 研究扩展了先前开发的半荧光恢复后光漂白（half-FRAP）方法，通过谱分解（spectral decomposition）解决了具有半透性界面的球形扩散问题。通过评估积分恢复曲线的信息内容，证明了它们编码了足够信息来恢复界面参数。

Result: 将该框架应用于由聚赖氨酸（poly-lysine）和透明质酸（hyaluronic acid）组成的可调谐凝聚体（coacervates），发现其界面表现出强烈的偏置反射率和显著的阻力，两者都驱动优先内部混合。这些参数依赖于盐浓度，将界面传输与分子间相互作用强度和相图位置联系起来。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了界面性质与凝聚体动力学之间的定量联系，揭示了它们的相互作用如何产生不同的传输机制，为理解生物分子凝聚体的功能调控提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Biomolecular condensates organize biochemical processes by spatially concentrating molecules while allowing for dynamic exchange with their surroundings. However, transport across their interface can be strongly attenuated, leading to enhanced retention and preferential internal mixing. Two key mechanisms have been proposed to describe this behavior: biased interfacial reflectivity, which compares how strongly particles are reflected at the interface when attempting to enter or leave the condensate, and interfacial resistance, which sets the kinetic rate at which particles can cross the interface. Quantifying these parameters experimentally has remained challenging. Here, we present a theoretical and experimental framework to address this issue, extending our previously developed half-FRAP approach. We solve the spherical diffusion problem with a semipermeable interface by spectral decomposition. By evaluating the information content of the integrated recovery curves, we show that they encode sufficient information to recover interfacial parameters over extended regions of parameter space. Applying our framework to tunable coacervates composed of poly-lysine and hyaluronic acid, we find that their interfaces exhibit strongly biased reflectivity and substantial resistance, both driving preferential internal mixing. These parameters depend on salt concentration, linking interfacial transport to intermolecular interaction strength and position in the phase diagram. Our results establish a quantitative connection between interfacial properties and condensate dynamics, revealing how their interplay gives rise to distinct transport regimes.

</details>
