### [149] [Cosmological coupled black holes immersed in dark sector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24609)
*Chen-Hao Wu,Yue Chu,Ya-Peng Hu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文构建了一个浸没在各向异性暗物质背景中的黑洞精确解析解，揭示了黑洞质量与宇宙膨胀共同演化，其耦合由暗物质晕轮廓支配。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受宇宙学耦合黑洞（cosmological coupled black holes）理论和观测发展的启发，旨在构建一个浸没在各向异性暗物质背景中的黑洞精确解析解。

Method: 采用[Cadoni等人, JCAP 03 (2024) 026]建立的框架，通过将静态种子度规推广到动态的FLRW背景，推导出黑洞质量与宇宙膨胀共同演化的解。

Result: 获得了半径依赖的耦合指数（radius-dependent coupling exponent）的显式形式，揭示相互作用由暗物质晕轮廓（dark halo profile）支配，为宇宙学耦合提供了潜在实现方案。

Conclusion: 该模型将质量增长解释为周围暗物质流体对哈勃流（Hubble flow）的动态响应，区别于修改黑洞内部状态方程的方法，为超大质量黑洞周围的暗物质晕普遍存在提供了理论解释。

Abstract: Motivated by theoretical and observational developments of cosmological coupled black holes, we construct an exact analytical solution for a black hole immersed in an anisotropic dark sector background, adopting the framework established by [Cadoni et al., JCAP 03 (2024) 026]. By generalizing a static seed metric to a dynamical FLRW background, we derive a solution where the black hole mass co-evolves with the cosmic expansion. We then obtain the explicit form of the radius-dependent coupling exponent, revealing that the interaction is governed by the dark halo profile. Considering the ubiquity of the dark halos surrounding supermassive black holes, our model provides a potential realization of cosmological coupling, interpreting the mass growth as the dynamical response of the surrounding dark sector fluid to the Hubble flow, distinct from the method of modifying the black hole's internal equation of state.

</details>


### [150] [Unitary time-reversal on non-orientable spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24650)
*Ovidiu Racorean*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文探讨了时间反演对称性在量子力学中的本质，揭示了时空可定向性与时间反演算子性质之间的深刻联系：可定向时空需要反幺正（anti-unitary）时间反演算子，而非可定向时空则允许幺正（unitary）时间反演算子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间反演对称性在量子力学中具有特殊地位，传统上需要反幺正算子来确保物理一致性。然而，近期量子引力和黑洞物理学的进展表明，在非可定向拓扑的时空中，时间反演可能通过纯幺正算子实现，这引发了对其本质的重新思考。

Method: 通过分析时空可定向性（orientability）与时间反演算子性质之间的理论联系，探讨非可定向几何如何通过拓扑方式编码时间反演。研究比较了可定向与非可定向时空中时间反演算子的不同数学实现。

Result: 研究表明，可定向时空要求反幺正时间反演算子，这与传统量子理论一致；而非可定向时空允许幺正时间反演算子，这种算子与负能态（negative energy states）相容。非可定向几何连接具有相反时间方向的渐近时空，从而拓扑地编码时间反演。

Conclusion: 时空的可定向性决定了时间反演算子的本质：可定向时空需要反幺正算子，而非可定向时空允许幺正实现。这一发现揭示了量子力学基本对称性与时空拓扑结构之间的深刻联系，对量子引力理论具有重要意义。

Abstract: Time reversal symmetry occupies a distinctive role in quantum mechanics, fundamentally requiring an anti-unitary operator to ensure a physically consistent representation. As such, the time reversal operator combines a unitary transformation with complex conjugation, enabling the necessary inversion of the imaginary unit that appears in quantum commutation relations and dynamical equations. Attempts to represent time reversal as a purely unitary operation encounter fundamental contradictions, including violations of canonical commutation relations and issues with the positivity of energy spectra. However, recent advances in quantum gravity and black hole physics reveal that in spacetimes with non-orientable topology - where a global temporal orientation is not well defined - time reversal may be realized by a purely unitary operator. Such non-orientable geometries connect two asymptotically spacetimes with opposite time directions, thereby encoding time reversal topologically and removing the need for complex conjugation. In this work, we explore the deep connection between spacetime orientability and the nature of the time reversal operator, demonstrating that orientable spacetimes require anti-unitary time reversal consistent with conventional quantum theory, while non-orientable spacetimes allow unitary time reversal operators consistent with negative energy states.

</details>


### [151] [Fixing the center-of-mass frame of numerical relativity waveforms using the post-Newtonian center-of-mass charge](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24661)
*Aniket Khairnar,Leo C. Stein,Michael Boyle,Nils Deppe,Lawrence E. Kidder,Keefe Mitman,Jordan Moxon,Kyle C. Nelli,William Throwe,Nils L. Vu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文改进了准圆轨道、非进动双星系统引力波数值模拟中的邦迪-范德伯格-梅茨纳-萨克斯（BMS）坐标系固定方法，通过引入后牛顿理论的质心运动物理振荡模型，显著提升了拟合参数的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟产生的引力波BMS坐标系固定对于构建精确波形模型至关重要。准确比较数值相对论波形与其他模型需要固定任意BMS坐标系，而现有方法仅使用线性拟合近似质心运动存在不足。

Method: 本文改进了准圆轨道、非进动（quasicircular, nonprecessing）双星系统的质心（center-of-mass, CoM）坐标系固定方法。通过计算后牛顿（post-Newtonian）理论的质心加速电荷结果，捕捉其物理外旋振荡，替代了过去仅使用线性拟合的近似方法。

Result: 分析表明，使用解析结果显著提升了拟合参数（平移和加速向量）对拟合窗口持续时间和位置的鲁棒性。当窗口置于旋近（inspiral）中心时，鲁棒性改善最大：加速向量鲁棒性提升约25倍，平移向量提升约20倍。

Conclusion: 该方法已集成到Python包scri的BMS坐标系固定程序中，适用于柯西-特征演化（Cauchy-characteristic evolution）产生的波形。改进的质心坐标系固定方法为引力波数值模拟与理论模型的精确比较提供了更可靠的基础。

Abstract: The Bondi--van der Burg--Metzner--Sachs (BMS) frame of gravitational waves produced by numerical relativity (NR) simulations is crucial for building accurate waveform models. A proper comparison of NR waveforms with other models requires fixing the arbitrary BMS frame. In this work we improve the center-of-mass (CoM) frame fixing for quasicircular, nonprecessing binary systems. Past work approximated the CoM motion with just a linear fit. We compute a post-Newtonian result of the boosted CoM charge to also capture its physical out-spiraling oscillations. We show that using the analytical results improves the robustness of the fit parameters -- translation and boost vectors -- to the choice of duration and time of the fitting window. Our analysis demonstrates a maximum improvement in robustness when the window is placed at the center of the inspiral. We quantified this improvement by computing the ratio of variances of fit parameters when the fit window size is varied. The largest improvement in robustness of parameters is by a factor of $\sim 25$ for the boost vector and $\sim 20$ for the translation vector. Finally, we incorporate this method into the BMS frame-fixing routine of the python package $\texttt{scri}$ for waveforms produced with Cauchy-characteristic evolution.

</details>


### [152] [Topological signatures in Kerr-Sen AdS black hole thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24686)
*Mohd Rehan,Md Sabir Ali,Sushant G. Ghosh*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文采用拓扑方法研究Kerr-Sen AdS黑洞的热力学相变，发现其具有三个不同相（小、中、大黑洞分支），总拓扑荷为+1，且该拓扑不变量在伸缩子场变化下保持不变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑洞热力学与拓扑学为理解相变提供了坐标无关的坚实基础。本文旨在通过拓扑方法研究异型弦理论中出现的Kerr-Sen AdS黑洞的热力学性质，特别是其相变结构。

Method: 采用段氏拓扑流理论（Duan's topological current theory）和一种新颖的复留数方法（complex residue method），通过构建广义壳外自由能（generalized off-shell free energy）并分析参数空间中的相应矢量场，寻找对应壳上黑洞态的零点并计算其环绕数（winding numbers）。

Result: Kerr-Sen AdS黑洞展现出三个不同的热力学相：小、中、大黑洞分支，分别由环绕数为+1、-1和+1的临界点表征，总拓扑荷（total topological charge）W = +1。该拓扑数在伸缩子荷参数（dilaton charge parameter）变化下保持不变，表明伸缩子场不改变Kerr-AdS和RN-AdS黑洞的基本拓扑类。

Conclusion: 拓扑学为黑洞相变提供了深刻见解，对全息对偶性（holographic dualities）具有潜在意义。旋转参数对相结构和多临界点出现起关键作用，而伸缩子场不影响基本拓扑类。

Abstract: Black hole thermodynamics and topology have emerged as a strong foundation for a coordinate-independent understanding of phase transitions. Using both Duan's topological current theory and a novel complex residue method, we perform a topological study of the Kerr-Sen AdS black hole arising in heterotic string theory. In turn, we find the zero points corresponding to on-shell black hole states and calculate their winding numbers to find the global topological charge by building the generalized off-shell free energy and examining the corresponding vector field in a parametric space. Our analysis reveals that the Kerr-Sen AdS black hole exhibits three distinct thermodynamic phases -- small, intermediate, and large black hole branches -- characterized by critical points with winding numbers $+1$, $-1$, and $+1$ respectively, culminating in a total topological charge $W = +1$. Significantly, this topological number remains invariant under variations of the dilaton charge parameter, indicating that the dilaton field does not alter the fundamental topological class established for Kerr-AdS and RN-AdS black holes. However, the rotation parameter proves crucial in determining the phase structure and the emergence of multiple critical points. We systematically examine three limiting configurations: the full Kerr-Sen AdS spacetime, the GMGHS AdS limit ($a = 0$), and the asymptotically flat Kerr-Sen case ($Λ= 0$). In addition, we propose a novel approach that analytically continues the thermodynamic characterisation into the complex plane. The characterized complex function, derived from the off-shell Gibbs free energy, possesses isolated singular points whose residues directly encode the winding numbers. Our results indicate that topology offers deep insights into black hole phase transitions, with potential implications to holographic dualities.

</details>


### [153] [Suppression of Trapped Surface Formation by Quantum Gravitational Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24729)
*Ram Brustein,A. J. M. Medved,Hagar Meir*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子场论方法分析坍缩薄壳，发现即使壳层达到引力半径，视界也不会形成，为解释天体物理黑洞可能是无视界的规则致密天体提供了理论依据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典广义相对论预测大质量球对称坍缩系统会形成视界并最终导致奇点，但该分析基于普朗克长度为零的极限，忽略了量子几何涨落。本研究旨在探讨量子涨落如何改变这一经典结论。

Method: 将球对称坍缩薄壳的几何描述为1+1维有效量子场论，采用弯曲时空量子场论标准技术，在保持普朗克长度有限的情况下分析壳层接近视界时的粒子产生过程。

Result: 壳层接近视界时产生的粒子数在普朗克长度趋于零的极限下保持有限，总粒子数正比于贝肯斯坦-霍金熵，总能量等于壳层质量。关键发现是相关零矢量的标量膨胀参数乘积的量子期望值始终非零。

Conclusion: 即使壳层达到引力半径，视界也不会形成，经典史瓦西几何不再适用于描述壳层外部几何。这为天体物理黑洞可能是规则且无视界的致密天体提供了理论漏洞。

Abstract: Classical general relativity predicts that a contracting, spherically symmetric matter system with a large-enough mass will result in the formation of a trapped region whose outer boundary is an apparent horizon where the gravitational redshift diverges. The incompleteness theorems then lead to the conclusion that the outcome of the collapse is the singular geometry of a Schwarzschild black hole. Both analyses rely on solving Einstein's equations, a set of partial differential equations, valid in the limit that the Schwarzschild radius is finite but the Planck length is set to zero, so that quantum fluctuations of the geometry are completely absent. Here, we keep both parameters finite, allowing the geometry to fluctuate quantum mechanically, and take the limit of vanishing Planck length only at the end. Expressing the geometry of a spherically symmetric, collapsing, thin shell of matter in terms of an effective quantum field theory in 1+1 dimensions, we show, using the standard techniques of quantum field theory in curved spacetime, that the production of particles as the shell approaches its would-be horizon is finite in the limit of vanishing Planck length. The total number of produced quanta of the gravitational field scales as the Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, while their total energy scales as the mass of the shell. Importantly, the quantum expectation value of the product of the scalar expansion parameters for the associated null vectors is never vanishing. The conclusion is that an apparent horizon is not formed even when the shell has reached its gravitational radius. As the collapse continues, the classical Schwarzschild geometry can no longer be used to describe the shell's exterior geometry. This provides the sought-after loophole that is needed to explain how astrophysical black holes could be compact objects that are regular and horizonless.

</details>


### [154] [Primordial black hole formation from transient $f(T)$ cosmology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24759)
*Gerasimos Kouniatalis,Theodoros Papanikolaou,Spyros Basilakos,Emmanuel N. Saridakis*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了在最小耦合的$f(T)$远平行宇宙学中，通过瞬态偏离标准辐射主导时期来增强原初黑洞（PBH）形成的机制。模型显示修正引力效应能显著降低密度扰动的坍缩阈值，导致PBH形成率指数级增强，并使小行星质量级的PBH可能构成暗物质的全部或大部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索修正引力理论（modified gravity）单独产生原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）的可能性，而不需要特别修改辐射主导时期的物理。这为理解PBH形成机制和暗物质（dark matter）候选体提供了新途径。

Method: 采用最小耦合的$f(T)$远平行（teleparallel）宇宙学模型，该模型在有限时期内产生瞬态偏离标准辐射主导。通过引入有效扭转（torsion）分量降低总状态方程参数至1/3以下，从而改变背景演化并降低密度扰动在视界重入时的坍缩阈值。

Result: 研究发现瞬态软化效应显著降低了密度扰动在视界重入时的坍缩阈值，导致PBH形成率指数级增强。修正的背景演化改变了温度与视界质量的关系，在PBH质量函数中产生局部特征。对于典型参数，小行星质量级的PBH在扰动幅度$σ^2 \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$时可构成暗物质的显著部分甚至全部，且与现有观测约束一致。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，仅通过修正引力理论即可有效产生原初黑洞，无需特别修改辐射主导时期的物理。这为PBH形成机制提供了新的理论框架，并展示了修正引力宇宙学在解释暗物质候选体方面的潜力。

Abstract: We study primordial black hole (PBH) formation in a minimally coupled $f(T)$ teleparallel cosmology that generates a transient departure from standard radiation domination. The model is constructed so that modified-gravity effects are negligible at early and late times, but become dynamically relevant over a finite epoch, during which an effective torsion component reduces the total equation-of-state parameter below 1/3.We show that this transient softening lowers the collapse threshold for overdensities at horizon re-entry, leading to an exponential enhancement of PBH formation. In addition, the modified background alters the relation between temperature and horizon mass, producing a localized feature in the PBH mass function. For representative parameters, PBHs with asteroid-scale masses can account for a significant fraction, or even the entirety, of dark matter for perturbation amplitudes $σ^2 \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{-3})$, while remaining consistent with current constraints. Our results demonstrate that modified gravity alone can efficiently generate PBHs, without requiring ad hoc modifications of the radiation sector.

</details>


### [155] [Curvature Corrections to the Yukawa Potential in Tolman Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24927)
*J. V. Zamperlini,C. C. Barros*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于量子相互作用与强引力场（如中子星系统）之间的相互影响。在高度弯曲的时空中，需要理解引力如何修正基本相互作用势，特别是汤川势。

Method: 方法基于托尔曼度规描述的静态球对称时空，推导了这些度规下汤川势的显式修正。研究特别聚焦于托尔曼IV和VI两种解，并在局部惯性系中分析了修正的性质。

Result: 结果显示，与先前研究不同，托尔曼度规修正保留了局部惯性系中相互作用势的径向对称性。数值估计表明，对于IV解，天体物理对象产生的能量移动约为$10^{-34}$ MeV量级。VI解虽然在中心奇异，但在流体球半径的大部分区域产生可比较的修正。研究详细分析了每种情形下曲率修正对局部观测者表现为排斥或吸引的性质。

Conclusion: 结论强调了时空几何在塑造量子相互作用中的关键作用，为未来在相对论性恒星背景下研究核相互作用提供了理论基础。这些结果突出了引力修正对基本相互作用的重要性。

Abstract: This work investigates curvature-induced modifications to the Yukawa potential in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes described by Tolman metrics, focusing on their implications for compact stellar objects, with particular application to solutions IV and VI. Motivated by the interplay of quantum interactions and strong gravitational fields in systems like neutron stars, we derive explicit corrections to the Yukawa potential for these metrics. Contrary to previous findings suggesting that curvature corrections break the radial symmetry of the interacting potential near a highly charged black hole, we demonstrate that Tolman metric corrections preserve this symmetry in the local inertial frame. Numerical estimates for astrophysical objects reveal energy shifts of the order of $10^{-34}$ MeV for solution IV. The Tolman VI solution, while singular at the center, yields comparable corrections for most of the fluid sphere radius. A detailed analysis of the repulsive or attractive nature of these curvature corrections for a local observer is provided for each scenario. These results highlight the role of spacetime geometry in shaping quantum interactions and provide a foundation for future studies of nuclear interactions within the context of relativistic stars.

### [156] [Topological Quantization of Complex Velocity in Stochastic Spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25016)
*Jorge Meza-Domíguez,Tonatiuh Matos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究通过平均随机引力波背景，将量子力学流体力学表述中的两个速度场统一为单个复速度场，揭示了其作为信息几何载体的作用，并推导出复测地线方程和拓扑相位条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子力学的流体力学表述包含两个速度场：测地线（经典）速度 $π_μ$ 和随机（量子）速度 $u_μ$。研究旨在通过平均随机引力波背景来统一这两个速度场，探索其几何结构和物理意义。

Method: 通过对随机引力波背景进行平均，将两个速度场统一为单个复速度 $η_μ=π_μ-iu_μ$，该复速度源自物质振幅 $\mathcal{K}$ 的对数导数。该对象作为配置空间上拉回丛 $π_{2}^{*}(T^{*}M)$ 的截面存在，并定义了平坦的 $U(1)$ 联络。

Result: $η_μ$ 作为基本的信息几何载体，其中 $u_μ$ 将度规涨落的方差 $\langle h_{μν}h_{αβ}\rangle$ 映射到费希尔度规和冯·诺依曼熵。得到的几何结构坍缩为优雅的复测地线方程 $η^ν\nabla_νη_μ=\nabla_μ(\frac{1}{2}η^νη_ν)$，而非平凡时空拓扑施加了完整群量子化条件。

Conclusion: 该拓扑相位表明在原子干涉测量和宇宙学关联中存在可观测特征，为普朗克尺度时空随机性质提供了实验窗口。这一几何框架将量子力学的流体力学表述与信息几何和拓扑结构联系起来。

Abstract: The hydrodynamic formulation of quantum mechanics features two velocity fields: a geodesic (classical) velocity $π_μ$ and a stochastic (quantum) velocity $u_μ$. We show that averaging over a stochastic gravitational wave background unifies these into a single complex velocity $η_μ=π_μ-iu_μ$, derived from the logarithmic derivative of a matter amplitude $\mathcal{K}$. This object lives as a section of the pullback bundle $π_{2}^{*}(T^{*}M)$ over configuration space and defines a flat $U(1)$ connection, satisfying $D_μ\mathcal{K}=0$. Crucially, $η_μ$ acts as a fundamental information-geometric carrier, where $u_μ$ maps the variance of metric fluctuations $\langle h_{μν}h_{αβ}\rangle$ to the Fisher metric and von Neumann entropy. The resulting geometric structure collapses into an elegant complex geodesic equation $η^ν\nabla_νη_μ=\nabla_μ(\frac{1}{2}η^νη_ν)$, while non-trivial spacetime topology imposes a holonomy quantization condition. This topological phase suggests observable signatures in atom interferometry and cosmological correlations, providing an experimental window into the stochastic nature of spacetime at the Planck scale.

</details>


### [157] [Critical Behavior of Photon Rings in Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25049)
*Xi Wan,Zhenyu Zhang,Fang-Stars Wei,Yehui Hou,Bin Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了克尔-贝托蒂-罗宾逊时空中光子环的临界行为，该时空描述了一个浸没在背景磁场中的旋转黑洞。通过分析光子在小磁场近似下的径向和角向运动，确定了表征径向压缩、方位角超前和时间延迟的三个关键参数，并研究了它们对黑洞自旋、磁场强度和观测者倾角的依赖关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究磁场环境下旋转黑洞的光子环临界行为，为探测磁化黑洞环境提供理论框架。背景磁场会改变测地线结构，从而影响光子环的精细结构，这具有重要的观测意义。

Method: 采用克尔-贝托蒂-罗宾逊（Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson）时空描述浸没在背景磁场中的旋转黑洞。在小磁场近似下分析光子的径向和角向运动，聚焦于不稳定球面轨道，确定表征径向压缩（γ）、方位角超前（δ）和时间延迟（τ）的三个关键参数。通过近临界透镜方程分析高阶像的性质。

Result: 研究结果表明，磁场会改变测地线结构，并导致光子环精细结构的可观测变化。三个关键参数（γ, δ, τ）依赖于黑洞自旋、磁场强度和观测者倾角，对于轴上和离轴观测者均表现出不同的依赖关系。高阶像的分析进一步揭示了磁化黑洞环境的特征。

Conclusion: 本研究为探测磁化黑洞环境提供了一个有用的理论框架。通过分析磁场对光子环临界行为的影响，可以观测到光子环精细结构的变化，这为理解磁场环境下黑洞的几何和动力学特性提供了新的途径。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the critical behavior of photon rings in the Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson spacetime, describing a rotating black hole immersed in a background magnetic field. We analyze the radial and angular motions of photons under the small magnetic field approximation. Focusing on unstable spherical orbits, we determine three key parameters, $γ$, $δ$, and $τ$, which characterize radial compression, azimuthal advancement, and time delay. We then examine how these parameters depend on the black hole spin, magnetic field strength, and observer inclination for both on-axis and off-axis observers, and we further analyze the properties of higher-order images through near-critical lens equations. The results show that the magnetic field modifies the geodesic structure, and leads to observable changes in the fine structure of photon rings, providing a useful framework for probing magnetized black hole environments.

</details>


### [158] [Particle motions and gravitational waveforms in rotating black hole spacetimes of loop quantum gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25084)
*Yang Yang,Yu-Xuan Bai,Yong-Zhuang Li,Yu Han*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了量子引力修正对两种旋转黑洞时空的影响，包括视界、类时测地线运动和引力波辐射。通过修正的Newman-Janis算法从球对称环量子引力黑洞构造了这两种时空，分析了正则化参数ξ对观测特征的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在探索环量子引力（loop quantum gravity）中的全息修正（holonomy correction）如何影响旋转黑洞的观测特征。通过研究正则化参数ξ对黑洞物理性质的影响，为未来通过引力波观测探测量子引力效应提供理论基础。

Method: 采用修正的Newman-Janis算法从两种球对称环量子引力黑洞构造旋转黑洞时空。通过分析正则化参数ξ对类时测地线运动的影响，研究其对角动量L和能量范围的作用。在引力波辐射方面，使用极端质量比旋近（extreme-mass-ratio inspiral）简化模型，在领头阶后牛顿近似下计算引力波形。

Result: 研究发现：当自旋参数a较小时，正则化参数ξ显著影响轨道角动量L。在赤道周期性轨道中，随着ξ增加，固定L下的允许能量范围也增加；在非赤道运动中，随着ξ增加，有效约束轨迹向赤道平面的Carter常数允许范围减小。对于引力波辐射，增加ξ会增强波形偏差，特别是在事件视界附近。

Conclusion: 本文结果初步揭示了全息修正对旋转黑洞潜在可观测特征的一些普遍性印记。正则化参数ξ对类时测地线运动和引力波辐射均有显著影响，为通过观测探测量子引力效应提供了理论依据。

Abstract: In this article, we investigate the influence of the quantum gravity corrections on the horizons, timelike geodesic motions and the gravitational wave emission in two different rotating black hole spacetimes which are constructed via the revised Newman-Janis algorithm from two spherically symmetric loop quantum gravity black holes. The quantum gravity effect is encoded in the regularization parameter $ξ$ of the holonomy correction, and the constraint range of $ξ$ is provided. For the timelike geodesic motion, we find that when the spin parameter $a$ is small, $ξ$ significantly affects the orbital angular momentum $L$. In equatorial periodic orbits, as $ξ$ increases, the allowed energy range for fixed $L$ also increases, while in generic off-equatorial motion, as $ξ$ increases, the permissible range of the Carter constant which effectively confines trajectories toward the equatorial plane decreases. For the gravitational wave emission, by using a simplified extreme-mass-ratio inspiral model within the leading order post-Newtonian approximation, we compute the gravitational waveforms and show how increasing $ξ$ enhances the waveform deviations, particularly near the event horizon. To summarize, the results in this article preliminarily reveal some universal features that holonomy corrections imprint on potentially observable signatures of rotating black holes.

### [159] [Constraining fractionality using some observational tests](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25153)
*H. Moradpour,S. Jalalzadeh,R. Jalalzadeh,A. H. Ziaie*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究分析了该分数-分形黑洞对应的四种观测效应：夏皮罗延迟（Shapiro delay）和萨尼亚克延迟（Sagnac delay）、阴影（shadow）、轨道进动（orbital precession）以及引力透镜（gravitational lensing），并采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法进行数据分析。

Result: MCMC分析揭示了该度规在处理太阳系测试（solar-system tests）方面的潜力，同时强调了研究分数时空（fractional spacetimes）和分数天体的必要性。

Conclusion: 研究表明分数-分形施瓦西黑洞模型在解释观测现象方面具有潜力，并指出了进一步探索分数时空物理的重要性。

Abstract: Recently, a fractional version of the Schwarzschild-Tangherlini black hole with a fractal horizon has been introduced. Motivated by the key role of the Schwarzschild solution in gravitational and astrophysical studies, some consequences of this fractional-fractal generalization of the Schwarzschild black hole have been investigated. In this line, the corresponding i) Shapiro and Sagnac time delays, ii) shadow, iii) orbital precession, and iv) gravitational lensing are studied and confronted with observational data. MCMC analysis also unveils i) the potential of this metric in dealing with the solar-system tests and ii) the necessity of studying fractional spacetimes and objects.

### [160] [Sign Errors in "The Four Laws of Black Hole Mechanics"](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25171)
*Richard P. Behiel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文指出Bardeen、Carter和Hawking在1973年发表的《黑洞力学四定律》中存在两个相互抵消的符号错误，并提供了修正指南。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该论文旨在识别和纠正Bardeen、Carter和Hawking（BCH）经典论文中的符号错误，这些错误可能使读者在逐步推导过程中感到困惑。

Method: 通过分析BCH论文中的推导过程，特别是从方程(32)出发，识别出方程(33)和(34)中涉及红移化学势（redshifted chemical potential）和红移温度（redshifted temperature）的最后两个积分项的符号错误。

Result: 发现两个相互抵消的符号错误：1）方程(33)和(34)的最后两个积分项应为负号而非正号；2）方程(20)后定义的总粒子数N和总熵S缺少负号，导致这些量无法保持正值。

Conclusion: 这两个符号错误相互抵消，修正N和S的定义使其保持正值后，方程(33)和(34)即变为正确。BCH论文的所有结论仍然有效，该注释仅为读者提供推导过程中的符号修正指南。

Abstract: In 1973, Bardeen, Cater, and Hawking published "The Four Laws of Black Hole Mechanics", establishing the mathematical framework that would later be understood as the thermodynamics of black holes. Central to the paper is equation (33), which writes the variation of the total energy-momentum integral in terms of physically meaningful quantities: angular momentum, particle number, and entropy. Equation (33) feeds into the differential mass formula, equation (34), which is the first law of black hole mechanics. This note identifies two compensating sign errors in the BCH paper. The first error, demonstrated by a derivation from equation (32), is that equations (33) and (34) should carry minus signs rather than plus signs on the last two integrals, those involving the redshifted chemical potential and the redshifted temperature. he second error is that the definitions of total particle number N and total entropy S given after equation (20) are missing minus signs that are required for these quantities to be positive. These two errors cancel, in that reversing the signs in the definitions of N and S to ensure positive quantities makes equations (33) and (34) correct.
  All conclusions of the BCH paper remain valid. This note is intended merely as a guide for readers who, in working through the derivation step by step, might otherwise be puzzled by the sign discrepancies. Numbered equations refer to the BCH paper; lettered equations are introduced in this note.

</details>


### [161] [Magnetic Modification of Black Hole Photospheres with Image Contraction, Efficiency Shifts and Redshift Boosts in Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson Spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25210)
*Javokhir Sharipov,Pankaj Sheoran,Sanjar Shaymatov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了均匀磁场中史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）吸积盘的光学和辐射特征，发现磁场会改变光子传播、扩大特征半径、收缩直接成像并显著降低辐射效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索均匀磁场对黑洞吸积盘物理特征的影响，特别是使用Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson（SBR）度规来描述非旋转黑洞在磁场中的时空几何结构。

Method: 研究方法包括：首先研究零测地线（null geodesics）以分析磁场如何改变光子传播；然后计算磁场依赖的关键特征半径偏移；接着采用光线追踪（ray-tracing）方法构建观测到的吸积盘图像；最后建立吸积盘动力学的解析框架。

Result: 研究发现：磁场使事件视界（event horizon）、光子球（photon sphere）和最内稳定圆轨道（innermost stable circular orbit）半径单调增加；透镜化发射带收缩到更窄的碰撞参数范围；直接图像收缩而最大能量通量、辐射温度和红移因子增强；辐射效率随磁场强度显著下降，当β=BM∼0.1时效率下降约91%。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，均匀磁场通过放大有效引力场来改变黑洞吸积盘的辐射特征，导致关键特征半径向外移动，成像特征改变，并且辐射效率随磁场强度增加而急剧下降。

Abstract: We investigate the optical and radiative signatures of an accretion disk around a Schwarzschild black hole (BH) immersed in a uniform magnetic field. The spacetime geometry is described by the Schwarzschild-Bertotti-Robinson (SBR) metric, which represents the non-rotating sector of the recently discovered Kerr-Bertotti-Robinson exact solution to the Einstein-Maxwell equations. We begin with the study of null geodesics and demonstrate that the self-consistent magnetic field fundamentally alters photon propagation, causing an expansion of light bundles relative to the Schwarzschild case due to modified initial conditions in the orbital equation. We then compute the magnetic field-dependent shifts of key characteristic radii: the event horizon ($r_h$), photon sphere ($r_{ph}$), and innermost stable circular orbit ($r_{ISCO}$). We find that all three increase monotonically with field strength $B$, revealing a magnetic amplification of the effective gravitational field. For $B=0.05$, we find that the lensed emission bands contract to a narrower impact parameter range, $b\in(4.976,5.149)\cup(5.19,6.128)$. Employing ray-tracing formalism, we construct observed accretion disk images and quantify magnetic modifications, showing that the direct image contracts while maximum energy flux, radiation temperature, and redshift factor are enhanced. Complementing these numerical findings, we develop an analytical framework for the accretion disk dynamics. We derive the modified Keplerian frequency $Ω_K$, along with the specific energy $E$ and angular momentum $L$ for circular orbits. From these, we obtain the exact ISCO radius $r_{\text{ISCO}}$, which shows an outward shift. This outward shift reveals that the radiative efficiency decreases dramatically with increasing magnetic field strength $B$. For $β= BM \sim 0.1$, the efficiency drops by approximately $91\%$.

</details>


### [162] [Non-Minimally Coupled Scalar Field, Area Quantization and Black Hole Entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25292)
*Sahil Devdutt,Akriti Garg,Ayan Chatterjee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在标量场非最小耦合引力理论中，推导了旋转/非旋转黑洞视界面积算符的本征谱，发现面积谱是等间距的，依赖于Barbero-Immirzi参数和视界上的标量场值，这支持了Bekenstein-Mukhanov提议并给出了黑洞熵及其量子修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力候选理论中黑洞熵的枚举依赖于视界上微观态的量子性质。本文旨在推导标量场非最小耦合引力理论中旋转/非旋转黑洞的视界面积算符本征谱，从视界对称性代数出发明确确定面积谱。

Method: 采用弱孤立视界（weak isolated horizon）形式体系，从视界对称性的代数推导面积算符的本征谱。该方法基于量子力学观点，无需特定量子引力理论即可直接得出视界几何自然离散的结论。

Result: 面积算符的本征谱明确依赖于Barbero-Immirzi参数和视界上的标量场值。面积谱是等间距的，这与Bekenstein-Mukhanov提议一致，并导出了黑洞熵及其量子修正。

Conclusion: 从视界对称性代数可以明确推导出面积算符的本征谱，表明视界几何在量子力学意义上自然离散。等间距的面积谱支持Bekenstein-Mukhanov提议，为黑洞熵及其量子修正提供了理论基础。

Abstract: The enumeration of black hole entropy in candidate theories of quantum gravity utilises the quantum properties of microstates residing on the black hole horizon. For example, in Loop Quantum Gravity, the computation of entropy is based on the spectrum of area operator, and one determines the possible number of area mirocrostates corresponding to a given classical horizon area. In this paper, we derive the eigenspectrum of the horizon area operator for rotating/non-rotating black holes in a gravitational theory non-minimally coupled to scalar fields. Using the weak isolated horizon formalism, we show that the spectrum of area operator follows unambiguously from the algebra of horizon symmetry. More precisely, from the quantum mechanical point of view, the horizon geometry must be naturally discrete, a conclusion which is arrived at directly, without the need for any particular theory of quantum gravity. The area spectrum depends on the Barbero-Immirzi parameter as well as the value of scalar field on horizon. The area spectrum is equidistant, which is consistent with the Bekenstein-Mukhanov proposal and gives rise to black hole entropy and their quantum corrections.

### [163] [Non parametric constraints of gravitational-electromagnetic luminosity distance ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25305)

Result: 将方法应用于GWTC-3目录（GWTC-3 catalogue）中的双黑洞并合数据，对宇宙学参数和群体参数（cosmological and population parameters）进行联合分析。结果表明与广义相对论（general relativity）以及先前基于参数方法（parametric methods）的分析结果一致。

Conclusion: 新开发的非参数方法为约束引力波与电磁波距离比提供了模型独立的分析框架，应用于实际观测数据得到了与广义相对论一致的结果，验证了方法的有效性。

Abstract: The ratio between the gravitational waves (GW) and electromagnetic waves (EMW) luminosity distance ratio is a key observable that allows to test the nature of gravity, using gravitational waves emitted from compact binary coalescences. We develop a new non parametric method for constraining the GW-EMW distance ratio, in order to perform model independent analysis of observational data, not based on any specific theoretical of phenomenological assumption.
  We apply the method to the analysis of binary black hole mergers data from the GWTC-3 catalogue, performing a joint analysis of cosmological and population parameters. The results are consistent with general relativity and with previous analyses based on parametric methods.

### [164] [Black holes as portals to an Euclidean realm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25313)
*Fan Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了黑洞（black holes）可能作为从欧几里得度规（Euclidean metric signature）区域进入我们宇宙的入口门户，类似于大爆炸（big bang）作为出口的观点。分析表明，黑洞内部需要包含德西特核心（de Sitter cores）以满足度规符号转变边界（metric signature transition boundary）的规则性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机源于一种单循环宇宙学情景（one-cycle cosmological scenario），其中大爆炸标志着从欧几里得度规区域退出的时刻。研究者希望探讨黑洞是否可能作为镜像入口门户（mirroring entryways），与作为出口的大爆炸形成对称结构。

Method: 通过分析黑洞内部结构（interior structure of BHs），研究检验了何种黑洞构造能够与这种物理图像一致。特别关注了德西特核心（de Sitter cores）的存在必要性，以满足度规符号转变边界（metric signature transition boundary）的规则性条件（regularity conditions）。

Result: 研究得出结论，黑洞内部需要包含德西特核心来包裹入口门户，这与大爆炸后暴胀阶段（inflationary stage）类似。此外，分析表明很可能需要存在一个非暴胀物质（non-inflationary matter）的类空壳层（spacelike shell）。

Conclusion: 在单循环宇宙学框架下，黑洞可能作为从欧几里得度规区域进入我们宇宙的入口门户。为实现这一物理图像，黑洞内部需要包含德西特核心，并且很可能需要非暴胀物质的类空壳层来满足度规转变的规则性条件。

Abstract: Motivated by a one-cycle cosmological scenario where the big bang marks the egress from a Euclidean metric signature regime, we investigate the possibility of black holes (BH) hosting the mirroring entryways. Analogous to the inflationary stage following the exit end, the entry portals must be enveloped by de Sitter cores inside BHs, in order to satisfy regularity conditions at the metric signature transition boundary. We examine the interior structure of BHs that could be consistent with such a physical picture, and conclude that the presence of a spacelike shell of non-inflationary matter is likely required.

### [165] [Testing the strong equivalence principle with multimessenger binary neutron star mergers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25413)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力常数G的恒定性是强等效原理和广义相对论的基石，但其可能的时间变化仍是基础物理检验的关键目标。引力波天文学，特别是与电磁观测相结合，为在强场和动力学体系中探测这一原理提供了前所未有的新机遇。

Method: 本研究开发了一个包含缓慢变化引力常数的引力波波形模型，同时考虑了其对致密双星动力学和膨胀宇宙中引力波传播的影响。将该框架应用于双中子星合并事件GW170817，并结合来自GRB 170817A的电磁观测对光度距离、天空定位和双星倾角的独立约束，进行了联合贝叶斯分析以区分变化G效应与天体物理简并性。

Result: 分析未发现引力常数时间变化的证据，将其分数时间导数约束在$\dot{G}/G \in [-3.36 \times 10^{-9}, 5.34\times10^{-10}]~{\rm yr^{-1}}$范围内，这是迄今为止从真实引力波观测中获得的最严格界限。

Conclusion: 研究结果证明了多信使天文学作为相对论体系中强等效原理精密探测工具的强大能力，为在强场和动力学条件下检验基础物理定律提供了新途径。

Abstract: The constancy of the gravitational constant $G$ is a cornerstone of the strong equivalence principle and of general relativity, yet its possible temporal variation remains a key target in tests of fundamental physics. Gravitational-wave (GW) astronomy, especially when combined with electromagnetic observations, provides an unprecedented new opportunity to probe this principle in the strong-field and dynamical regime. In this work, we develop a GW waveform model with a slowly varying gravitational constant, incorporating its effects both on compact binary dynamics and GW propagation in an expanding universe. Applying this framework to the binary neutron star merger GW170817, together with independent electromagnetic constraints on the luminosity distance, sky localization and binary inclination from GRB 170817A, we perform a joint Bayesian analysis that disentangles varying-$G$ effects from astrophysical degeneracies. We find no evidence for a temporal variation of the gravitational constant, and constrain its fractional time derivative to $\dot{G}/G \in [-3.36 \times 10^{-9}, 5.34\times10^{-10}]~{\rm yr^{-1}}$, representing the most stringent bounds obtained to date from real GW observations. Our results demonstrate the power of multi-messenger astronomy as a precision probe of the strong equivalence principle in the relativistic regime.

</details>


### [166] [Quasinormal modes and AdS/CFT correspondence of a rotating BTZ-like black hole in the Einstein-bumblebee gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25470)
*Fangli Quan,Zhong-Wu Xia,Rui Ding,Qiyuan Pan,Jiliang Jing*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力理论中旋转BTZ类黑洞的准正规模，发现洛伦兹对称性破缺参数仅影响频率的虚部，且对AdS/CFT对偶的普适关系保持成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力理论中旋转BTZ类黑洞的准正规模（quasinormal modes），旨在探索洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry breaking）参数对扰动衰减行为的影响，并检验AdS/CFT对偶（AdS/CFT correspondence）在该理论中的有效性。

Method: 通过解析方法获得了标量、费米子和矢量扰动在爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力理论中旋转BTZ类黑洞周围的准正规模的精确表达式，并分析了洛伦兹对称性破缺参数ℓ对频率实部和虚部的影响。

Result: 发现洛伦兹对称性破缺参数ℓ仅影响准正规模频率的虚部，且ℓ越大扰动场衰减越慢；频率实部仅依赖于角量子数，与标准BTZ黑洞相同。在AdS/CFT对偶框架下，边界算符的左右共形权重（conformal weights）的普适关系仍然成立。

Conclusion: 研究结果强有力地支持了AdS/CFT对偶在爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力理论中的有效性，有助于更好地理解具有洛伦兹对称性破缺的爱因斯坦-大黄蜂引力理论。

Abstract: We obtain exact expressions for the quasinormal modes (QNMs) of the massive scalar, fermionic and vector perturbations around a rotating BTZ-like black hole in the Einstein-bumblebee gravity. We find that the Lorentz symmetry breaking (LSB) parameter $\ell$ leaves its imprint only on the imaginary parts of the quasinormal frequencies and the corresponding perturbation field decays more slowly for a larger $\ell$, except for the left-moving quasinormal frequencies $ω_L$ with positive mass and the right-moving ones $ω_R$ with negative mass for the fundamental modes under the vector perturbation where the imaginary parts are independent of $\ell$. We also note that, regardless of the kind of perturbations, the real parts depend only on the angular quantum number, which are the same as those in the standard BTZ black hole. Furthermore, we investigate the AdS/CFT correspondence from the QNMs and observe that the expected universal relation for the left and right conformal weights ($h_L,h_R$) of the boundary operators dual to various fields still holds even for the BTZ-like black hole in the Einstein-bumblebee gravity. These results strongly support the AdS/CFT correspondence and could help us better understand the Einstein-bumblebee gravity with the Lorentz symmetry violation.

</details>


### [167] [Implementing Bell causality in Quantum Sequential Growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25503)
*Ritesh Srivastava,Sumati Surya*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了因果集量子引力中量子顺序增长动力学的量子贝尔因果性条件的不同实现方式，重点关注非对易跃迁算符。研究发现，对于两种最自然的算符排序选择，跃迁算符代数简化为对易代数；而第三种依赖于前驱集大小的排序选择则产生新的对易关系，但不保证对易性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索因果集量子引力（causal set quantum gravity）中量子顺序增长（quantum sequential growth, QSG）动力学的量子贝尔因果性（quantum Bell causality, QBC）条件的实现方式。特别关注非对易跃迁算符（non-commuting transition operators）的情况，旨在寻找QSG的非对易实现。

Method: 研究方法基于非奇异动力学假设，考察了三种不同的算符排序选择：两种最自然的排序方式，以及第三种依赖于前驱集（precursor set）大小的排序方式。通过分析跃迁算符代数（transition operator algebra）的结构，特别是"反链子代数"（antichain subalgebra）的性质，来研究对易关系。

Result: 研究发现：对于前两种算符排序选择，跃迁算符代数简化为对易代数（commutative algebra）。第三种排序产生了新的对易关系（commutation relations），进一步约束了代数但不保证对易性。如果"反链子代数"的任何生成元属于其中心，则整个代数具有对易性。尝试构建最简单的d=2表示时，发现反链子代数生成元的泡利矩阵表示（Pauli matrix representation）会导致不一致性。

Conclusion: 该研究表明，寻找非平凡的量子顺序增长表示面临数学复杂性挑战，代数结构的复杂性阻碍了获得跃迁算符的一般形式。如果存在非平凡表示，其维度必须高于二维。这项工作可视为寻找QSG非对易实现的第一步。

Abstract: We explore different implementations of the quantum Bell causality (QBC) condition in the quantum sequential growth (QSG) dynamics of causal set quantum gravity, for non-commuting transition operators. Assuming a non-singular dynamics we show that for the two most natural choices of operator orderings for the QBC, the transition operator algebra reduces to a commutative one. As a third choice, we take the operator ordering to depend on the size of the precursor set. We find several new commutation relations which further constrain the algebra but do not imply commutativity. On the other hand, if any of the generators of the ``antichain subalgebra'' belongs to its center, then this implies commutativity of the full algebra. The complexity of the algebra prevents us from obtaining a general form for the transition operators, which hinders computability. In an attempt to construct the simplest non-trivial d=2 representation, we find that a Pauli matrix representation of the generators of the antichain subalgebra leads to inconsistencies, implying that if a non-trivial representation exists, it must be higher dimensional. Our work can be viewed as a first step towards finding a non-commutative realisation of QSG.

</details>


### [168] [An effective cosmological constant as black hole primary hair](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25598)
*Christos Charmousis,Pedro G. S. Fernandes,Mokhtar Hassaine*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了广义Proca理论，通过放宽正则化方案中的刚性约束，将作用量中的系数视为自由参数，从而发现了更广泛的解空间，其中包括具有原生毛发的静态球对称黑洞解。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法是将作用量中各项的系数视为自由参数，而非受限于特定正则化方案。这种处理方式允许研究更广泛的广义Proca理论（Generalized Proca theories），并分析其静态球对称黑洞解。

Result: 研究揭示了一个更广泛的解空间，该空间允许具有原生毛发（primary hair）的静态球对称黑洞解。令人惊讶的是，即使在没有裸宇宙学项的情况下，宇宙学常数（cosmological constant）也自然地作为积分常数出现。

Conclusion: 通过放宽正则化约束，广义Proca理论展现出更丰富的物理内容，包括自然出现的宇宙学常数和具有原生毛发的黑洞解，这为理解引力与矢量场相互作用提供了新的视角。

Abstract: We study Generalized Proca theories inspired by the recent regularised Proca theory of four-dimensional Gauss-Bonnet gravity. By abandoning the rigid constraints typically imposed by specific regularization schemes, we treat the coefficients of the terms in the action as free parameters. This approach uncovers a broader solution space that admits static and spherically symmetric black hole solutions characterized by primary hair, where, surprisingly, the cosmological constant arises naturally as a constant of integration even in the absence of a bare cosmological term.

### [169] [Repetitive Penrose Process in Kerr-Taub-NUT black hole spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25630)

Main category: gr-qc

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 首先回顾克尔-陶布-NUT黑洞的时空结构，包括视界（event horizon）和能层（ergosphere）结构；然后利用黑洞的不可约质量（irreducible mass）分析可提取能量；最后通过建立守恒定律和设置迭代停止条件来研究重复彭罗斯过程。

Result: 结果表明：引力磁荷$l$会使事件视界和能层半径增大；同时，可提取能量随引力磁荷的增加而减少；通过数值计算获得了每次迭代中黑洞参数的变化以及重复彭罗斯过程的相应物理量。

Conclusion: 引力磁荷对克尔-陶布-NUT黑洞的彭罗斯能量提取过程具有显著影响，不仅改变了黑洞的几何结构，还降低了能量提取效率，这为理解带有拓扑荷的黑洞能量提取机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: In this article, we study the repetitive Penrose process for the Kerr-Taub-NUT black hole (BH). First of all, we briefly review the spacetime of the Kerr-Taub-NUT BH, including horizon and ergosphere structures. The results indicate that the event horizon and ergosphere radii increase under the influence of the gravitomagnetic charge $l$. Subsequently, we find by using the irreducible mass of the BH that the extractable energy decreases with the rise of the gravitomagnetic charge. We then turn to the repetitive Penrose process by writing the conservation laws and setting the corresponding iterative stopping conditions. Furthermore, we numerically calculate the change in the BH's parameters, along with the corresponding quantities of the repetitive Penrose process, for each iteration.

### [170] [Exact lambdavacuum solutions in higher dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25651)
*I. A. Sarmiento-Alvarado,P. Wiederhold,T. Matos*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于获得高维爱因斯坦场方程在非零宇宙学常数下的精确解，这些解具有明确的数学结构，能够统一描述多种已知的时空度规。

Method: 方法基于先前工作中确定的$\mathfrak{sl}(n,\mathbb{R})$中的对易常数矩阵集$\{A_a\}$和常数矩阵$g_0$，通过不同选择构造$(n+2)$维爱因斯坦场方程的解。

Result: 获得了依赖于矩阵参数$\{A_a\}$和$g_0$的精确解族，具体展示了如何得到de Sitter度规、Anti-de Sitter度规、Birmingham度规、Nariai度规和Anti-Nariai度规的高维推广，以及广义Nariai和Anti-Nariai解的直接拓扑积结构。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一个统一的框架，通过矩阵参数$\{A_a\}$和$g_0$的不同选择，系统地生成高维爱因斯坦场方程的多种精确解，包括在宇宙学背景下的解。

Abstract: In this work, we obtain exact solutions to the $(n+2)$-dimensional Einstein Field Equations with a non-zero cosmological constant for $n > 1$.
  These solutions depend on a set $\{ A_a, a=1,2,\ldots , m \}$ of pairwise commuting constant matrices in $\mathfrak{sl} ( n, \mathbb{R} )$ and on a constant matrix $g_0$ in $\mathcal{I} (\{ A_a, a=1,\ldots , m \})$, determined in previous work.
  Different choices of $\{ A_a, a=1,\ldots , m \}$ and $g_0$ correspond to different solutions.
  As examples, we show how to obtain the de Sitter metric, the Anti-de Sitter metric, the Birmingham metric, the Nariai metric and the Anti-Nariai metric in higher dimensions.
  The generalized Nariai and Anti-Nariai solutions are direct topological products of $AdS_{\frac{n}{2} + 1} \times H^{\frac{n}{2} + 1}$, $dS_{\frac{n}{2} + 1} \times S^{\frac{n}{2} + 1}$, $AdS_2 \times H^n$, $AdS_n \times H^2$, $dS_2 \times S^n$ and $dS_n \times S^2$.
  In addition, we study a solution in the context of cosmology.

### [171] [Soliton turbulence of a strongly driven one-dimensional Bose gas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24832)
*Manon Ballu,Romain Dubessy,Aurélien Perrin,Hélène Perrin,Anna Minguzzi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了一维弱相互作用玻色气体在周期性振荡线性势驱动下的非平衡动力学，揭示了气体在弱驱动和强驱动两种不同机制下分别形成弱扰动孤子和类湍流强纠缠孤子态，并通过动量分布的幂律衰减特征区分这两种机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索一维弱相互作用玻色气体在周期性振荡线性势驱动下的非平衡动力学行为，特别关注气体在达到准稳态后孤子的形成与演化特征，以及不同驱动强度下系统的物理机制转变。

Method: 研究方法包括：1）在箱型势阱中研究弱相互作用一维玻色气体；2）施加周期性振荡线性势作为驱动；3）分析瞬态后达到的准稳态；4）使用逆散射变换（inverse scattering transform）表征孤子特性；5）通过时空映射和动量分布分析系统行为。

Result: 研究结果显示：在弱驱动振幅下，孤子间仅存在弱扰动，动量分布呈现幂律衰减 $n(k) \sim k^{-2}$；在强驱动振幅下，系统达到类湍流机制，孤子强烈纠缠，动量分布呈现 $n(k) \sim k^{-α}$ 的幂律衰减，其中指数 $α\in [7,9]$。两种机制的特征均可在动量分布中识别。

Conclusion: 该研究证实了周期性驱动的一维玻色气体在不同驱动强度下会形成两种不同的物理机制，分别以弱扰动孤子和强纠缠孤子态为特征，且这两种机制可通过动量分布的幂律衰减特征进行区分。所提出的实验方案在当前实验装置中具有可行性。

Abstract: We study the out-of-equilibrium dynamics of a weakly interacting one-dimensional Bose gas in a box trap, subjected to a drive realized by a periodically oscillating linear potential. After a transient regime, the gas reaches a quasi-steady state, characterized by the presence of several solitons. At weak driving amplitude, the solitons are only weakly perturbed by one another, while at strong driving amplitude a regime analogous to turbulence is reached, where the solitons are strongly intertwined with each other. We show that a hallmark of both regimes can be found in the momentum distribution, which displays a power-law decay $n(k) \sim k^{-2}$ at weak driving amplitude and $n(k) \sim k^{-α}$ with a power-law exponent $α\in [7,9]$ at large amplitude. We further characterize each of the two regimes by following the space-time maps and characterizing the solitons using the inverse scattering transform. The protocol analyzed in this study is amenable to experimental realization in current experimental setups.

</details>


### [172] [Dynamics of two particles with quasiperiodic long-range interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25045)
*Yun Zou*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过数值精确对角化（ED）方法，分析了准周期长程相互作用下一维晶格中两个全同无自旋费米子的动力学行为，揭示了强准周期调制下出现的稳健相关动力学区域，其特征为近似恒定的粒子间距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索准周期长程相互作用如何塑造少体量子动力学，特别关注在开放边界条件（OBC）下两个全同无自旋费米子的动力学行为。

Method: 采用数值精确对角化（exact diagonalization, ED）方法，将这一不可积系统作为连续时间量子行走（continuous-time quantum walk）进行研究。

Result: 在足够强的准周期长程相互作用调制下，系统出现稳健的相关动力学区域，其特征为近似恒定的粒子间距。通过调节准周期调制的相位，观察到三种不同的现象表现：局域化、最近邻分离振荡和次近邻分离转变。此外，还识别出系统中纠缠熵的抑制，包括振荡行为的情况。

Conclusion: 研究结果突显了准周期长程相互作用如何塑造少体量子动力学，系统的行为由相互作用的性质及边界条件的选择共同决定。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamics of two identical spinless fermions on a one-dimensional lattice with open boundary conditions (OBC), subject to quasiperiodic long-range interactions. Using numerical exact diagonalization (ED), we study this non-integrable system as a continuous-time quantum walk and uncover a robust correlated dynamical regime. This regime, characterized by an approximately constant inter-particle distance, emerges under sufficiently strong quasiperiodic modulation of the long-range interactions. Further, the study shows that the behavior is determined by the nature of the interaction and the choice of boundary condition. Notably, by tuning the phase of the quasiperiodic modulation, we observe three distinct manifestations of this phenomenon: localization, nearest-neighbor separation oscillations, and next-nearest-neighbor separation transitions -- each arising for specific initial separations. Furthermore, we identify the suppression of entanglement entropy in the system, including instances of oscillatory behavior. Our results highlight how quasiperiodic long-range interactions shape few-body quantum dynamics.

</details>


### [173] [Dynamically Stable Vortices in Exciton-Polariton Condensates Engineered by Repulsive Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25143)
*P. Raman,R. Radha,Pankaj K. Mishra,Paulsamy Muruganandam*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究通过解析和数值方法分析了开放耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述的激子极化激元凝聚体动力学与稳定性，重点考察了二元和短程三体相互作用的影响，揭示了不同相互作用参数下涡旋-反涡旋对的形成机制与稳定性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于深入理解开放耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程描述的激子极化激元凝聚体（exciton-polariton condensates）动力学行为，特别关注二元和短程三体相互作用对系统稳定性的影响，以及这些相互作用如何调控涡旋结构的形成与演化。

Method: 采用解析与数值相结合的研究方法，通过渐近描述识别参数区域，推导不稳定性振幅方程，并利用开放耗散Gross-Pitaevskii方程（open-dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation）模拟系统动力学，分析暗孤子蛇形不稳定性（snake instability）导致的涡旋形成机制。

Result: 研究发现排斥性三体相互作用与二元相互作用结合时支持稳定的涡旋-反涡旋对（vortex-antivortex pair）形成；而吸引性三体相互作用与二元相互作用结合则会触发蛇形不稳定性，导致边界驱动的涡旋解体。在库效应影响下，边界效应更为显著，吸引性三体相互作用相比排斥性相互作用更容易使涡旋失稳。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明三体相互作用的符号对激子极化激元凝聚体中涡旋结构的稳定性具有决定性影响：排斥性相互作用域支持稳定的涡旋结构，而吸引性相互作用则促进涡旋解体，这为调控极化激元凝聚体中的拓扑激发提供了重要理论指导。

Abstract: We present an analytical and numerical study of the dynamics and stability of exciton-polariton condensates described by the open-dissipative Gross-Pitaevskii equation, incorporating both binary and short-range three-body interactions. Using an asymptotic description, we identify the parameter regime and derive equations for the instability amplitude, providing insights into vortex formation via the snake instability of dark solitons. We find that a repulsive three-body interaction, when combined with a binary interaction, supports stable vortex-antivortex pair formation. On the other hand, the reinforcement of attractive three-body interactions with binary interaction triggers the emergence of snake instability, leading to boundary-driven vortex disintegration. The time evolution of the instability under the influence of reservoir effects indicates that the boundary effects are more pronounced, to the extent of destabilizing the vortices with attractive three-body interactions compared to repulsive three-body interactions, thereby underscoring the stable nature of vortices in the repulsive domain.

</details>


### [174] [A High-Flux Source of Cold Strontium with a Loading Rate of $4 \times 10^{10}$ atoms/s for Open Release](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25312)
*Thomas Walker,Anna L. Marchant,Elliot Bentine,Oliver Buchmueller,Katherine Clarke,Christopher Foot,Leonie Hawkins,Kenneth M. Hughes,Kamran Hussain,Ludovico Iannizzotto-Venezze,Alice Josset,Hamza Labiad,Dillen Lee,Timothy C. Thornton-Sparkes,Tristan Valenzuela,Maurits van der Grinten,Andrew Vick,Mark G. Bason,Charles F. A. Baynham,Richard Hobson*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该论文展示了一种基于二维磁光阱（2D MOT）和塞曼减速器（Zeeman slower）的高通量冷锶原子源，实现了4×10¹⁰原子/秒的加载速率，这是目前报道的最高锶原子加载通量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在开发一种能够产生与碱金属物种相当通量的冷锶原子源，同时兼容长期运行所需的炉温条件，并满足前沿量子实验的真空压力要求。

Method: 采用二维磁光阱（2D MOT）和塞曼减速器（Zeeman slower）组合系统，将冷原子源加载到独立科学腔室中的三维磁光阱（3D MOT）。通过磁阱测量真空压力，并分析炉子和2D MOT源的原子通量和速度分布。

Result: 实现了4×10¹⁰原子/秒的加载速率，这是目前报道的最高锶原子加载通量。磁阱寿命在8-24秒之间，具体取决于炉温。原子通量和速度分布与自由分子流（free molecular flow）模型合理吻合。

Conclusion: 该研究证明能够在与碱金属物种相当的水平上轻松产生冷锶原子通量，同时满足长期运行和前沿量子实验的要求。设计已免费公开，以惠及量子研究社区。

Abstract: We present a high-flux source of cold strontium atoms based on a two-dimensional magneto-optical trap (2D MOT) and a Zeeman slower. We use the source to load a 3D MOT in a separate science chamber, observing a loading rate of $4 \times 10^{10}$ atoms/s -- to our knowledge, the highest reported loading flux for strontium. To characterise the vacuum pressure in the science chamber, we load the atoms into a magnetic trap and measure a lifetime of between 8 and 24 seconds, depending on oven temperature. Finally, we characterise the atom flux and velocity distributions from the oven and from the 2D MOT source, finding reasonable agreement with models in the free molecular flow regime. Our results show it is possible to readily produce a cold strontium flux at comparable levels to alkali species, at oven temperatures compatible with long-term operation, and at vacuum pressures suitable for state-of-the-art quantum experiments. We make our design available at no cost, to benefit researchers in the quantum community.

### [175] [Josephson effects in an interaction-asymmetric junction across the BCS-BEC crossover](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25577)
*Tingyu Zhang,Hiroyuki Tajima*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究理论分析了超冷费米气体中的约瑟夫森效应，其中约瑟夫森结两侧可独立调节至BCS-BEC渡越区域的不同位置。研究计算了直流和交流约瑟夫森电流，发现了相互作用偏置的里德尔峰（Riedel peak），揭示了配对谱权重与化学势之间的竞争关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索超冷费米气体中约瑟夫森效应的理论特性，特别是在BCS-BEC渡越（BCS-BEC crossover）区域中，当约瑟夫森结两侧可独立调节至不同相互作用强度时的物理行为。这有助于理解强耦合量子气体中的超流输运现象。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数方法（nonequilibrium Green's function approach）结合隧道哈密顿形式（tunnel Hamiltonian formalism），计算整个渡越区域的直流和交流约瑟夫森电流。通过同步调节结两侧从BCS到BEC区域来研究直流电流，并通过固定一侧相互作用强度而调节另一侧来研究交流约瑟夫森结。

Result: 计算得到了直流约瑟夫森电流随相互作用强度的函数关系，并给出了在深BCS和深BEC极限下的渐近表达式。当一侧固定在BCS极限而另一侧调节至BEC区域时，发现了隧穿电流的峰值，这对应于相互作用偏置的里德尔峰（interaction-biased Riedel peak）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，在整个BCS-BEC渡越过程中，配对谱权重增加与化学势降低对约瑟夫森隧穿的贡献存在竞争关系。该工作证明了里德尔峰在强耦合量子气体中的实现，为理解超冷费米系统中的超流输运提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We theoretically study the Josephson effect in ultracold Fermi gases, where the two sides of the Josephson junction are independently tuned to different regions of the Bardeen-Cooper-Schrieffer (BCS)-Bose-Einstein condensation (BEC) crossover. Using the nonequilibrium Green's function approach combined with the tunnel Hamiltonian formalism, we evaluate the DC and AC Josephson currents throughout the entire crossover region. We calculate the DC Josephson current as a function of interaction strength by tuning both sides of the junction synchronously from the BCS to the BEC regimes, and give the asymptotic expression of the current in the deep BCS and BEC limits. We also study the AC Josephson junction through the interaction-asymmetric junction by fixing the interaction in one reservoir and tuning that of the other one. A peak of the tunneling current is found when one side is fixed in the BCS limit and the other side is tuned into the BEC regime, which corresponds to the interaction-biased Riedel peak. Our results indicate the competition between contributions of increasing pair spectral weight and decreasing chemical potential to Josephson tunneling throughout the BCS-BEC crossover, and demonstrate the realization of the Riedel peak in strong-coupling quantum gases.

</details>


### [176] [Diffusion in interacting two-dimensional systems under a uniform magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25659)
*Łukasz Iwanek,Marcin Mierzejewski,Adam S. Sajna*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了均匀磁场下二维相互作用费米子系统的扩散弛豫动力学，发现在无限温度区域，费米子截断维格纳近似能准确捕捉中等相互作用强度的平衡动力学，并揭示了相互作用强度与磁场对扩散传输的竞争效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道磁场中相互作用粒子的动力学研究极具挑战性，因为这一物理现象与二维系统中的电子关联性（electronic correlations）密切相关，而目前缺乏直接的理论方法。研究旨在探索二维相互作用费米子系统在均匀磁场下的扩散弛豫动力学。

Method: 采用费米子截断维格纳近似（fermionic truncated Wigner approximation）研究无限温度区域（infinite temperature regime）的平衡动力学，并使用兰佐斯方法（Lanczos method）作为基准验证维格纳近似的可靠性，主要分析相对较小的梯子系统（ladder systems）。

Result: 研究发现，当相互作用强度超过跳跃能量（hopping energy）时，磁场效应对扩散传输（diffusive transport）被抑制；而当相互作用与动能相当时，磁通量（magnetic flux）显著降低扩散系数。这一现象在足够大的系统（约400个格点以上）中尤为明显，此时有限尺寸效应（finite-size effects）对粒子传输影响较小。

Conclusion: 费米子截断维格纳近似在中等相互作用强度下能准确描述二维系统的平衡动力学，研究结果揭示了相互作用与磁场对扩散传输的复杂竞争关系，并指出这些发现可在当前的光学晶格平台（optical lattice platforms）上直接验证。

Abstract: The dynamics of interacting particles in orbital magnetic fields are notoriously difficult to study, as this physics is inherently connected to electronic correlations in two-dimensional systems, for which no straightforward theoretical methods are available. Here, we report on the diffusive relaxation dynamics of two-dimensional interacting fermionic systems under a uniform magnetic field in the infinite temperature regime. We first show that the fermionic truncated Wigner approximation captures the equilibration dynamics unexpectedly well for intermediate interaction strengths when going beyond one dimension. This high accuracy holds at least for relatively small ladder systems, which are accessible to the Lanczos method that we use to benchmark the reliability of the Wigner approximation. We find that strong interactions, which exceed the hopping energy, suppress magnetic-field effects on diffusive transport. However, when the interactions are comparable to the kinetic energy, the diffusion is significantly reduced by the magnetic flux. This is observed for sufficiently large systems (above approximately 400 lattice sites), where finite-size effects weakly affect particle transport. We suggest that our results should be directly accessible on current optical lattice platforms.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 实验在Institut Laue Langevin (ILL)的PF2设施进行，通过测量中子消失（neutron disappearance）作为外加磁场（applied magnetic field）的函数来测试振荡。磁场以阶梯方式变化，以在不同质量分裂（mass splittings）范围内共振增强振荡概率。

Result: 未观测到中子消失的证据，并在95%置信水平下对中子-隐藏中子振荡周期设定了保守限制：在|δm| ∈ [60, 400] peV范围内τ_{nn'} > 200 ms，在|δm| ∈ [400, 1550] peV范围内τ_{nn'} > 100 ms。

Conclusion: 该实验未发现中子-隐藏中子振荡的证据，为这一超出标准模型现象设定了新的实验限制，特别是在60-1550 peV质量分裂范围内提供了振荡周期的严格上限。

Abstract: We report the results of the second iteration of an experiment searching for neutron-hidden-neutron oscillations in a beam of ultracold neutrons, conducted at the PF2 facility of the Institut Laue Langevin (ILL). Oscillations were tested via neutron disappearance as a function of an applied magnetic field, in the context of a phenomenological two-parameter model assuming zero hidden potentials. The magnetic field was varied in a step-wise manner in order to resonantly enhance the oscillation probability at different mass splittings ($δm$) across a 60--1550 peV range. No evidence for neutron disappearance is observed and conservative limits on the neutron-hidden-neutron oscillation period ($τ_{nn'}$) have been set at 95 % confidence level: $τ_{nn'} > 200$ms for $|δm| \in [60, 400]$ peV and $τ_{nn'} > 100$ ms for $|δm| \in [400, 1550]$ peV

### [178] [Measurement of dijet angular distributions and search for beyond the standard model physics in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25458)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文报道了在13 TeV质子-质子对撞中双喷注角分布（dijet angular distributions）的测量，使用CMS探测器收集的138 fb⁻¹数据，首次与次次领头阶（NNLO）微扰量子色动力学（pQCD）预测进行比较，并设置了对多种新物理场景的最严格限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究双喷注角分布旨在检验微扰量子色动力学（perturbative quantum chromodynamics, pQCD）在极高能量下的预测，并搜索超出标准模型（beyond Standard Model）的新物理现象，如夸克复合性（quark compositeness）、额外空间维度（extra spatial dimensions）等。

Method: 使用CMS探测器在LHC上收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据，对应积分亮度138 fb⁻¹，测量双喷注角分布并进行探测器效应修正，首次与包含次领头阶电弱修正（next-to-leading-order electroweak corrections）的次次领头阶微扰量子色动力学预测进行比较。

Result: 数据总体上与理论预测一致，但在双喷注质量2.4-4.8 TeV和6 TeV以上区间观察到归一化分布形状的微小差异；对夸克复合性等新物理场景设置了迄今最严格的限制，包括夸克接触相互作用（quark contact interactions）在95%置信水平下排除到17（37）TeV尺度。

Conclusion: 研究提供了对微扰量子色动力学预测的精确检验，并为多种超出标准模型的新物理场景设定了迄今最严格的实验限制，包括类轴子粒子（axion-like particles）与胶子的耦合以及反常三胶子耦合（anomalous triple-gluon coupling）的上限。

Abstract: A measurement is presented of dijet angular distributions in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV, using data collected with the CMS detector at the CERN LHC and corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. For the first time, the dijet angular distributions, corrected for detector effects, are compared with the predictions of perturbative quantum chromodynamics at next-to-next-to-leading order, including next-to-leading-order electroweak corrections. While data are generally found to be in agreement with predictions, a small difference in shape of the normalized distributions is seen for dijet masses ranging from 2.4 to 4.8 TeV and above 6 TeV. The distributions are used to search for proposed signatures of quark compositeness, extra spatial dimensions, quantum black holes, dark-matter mediators, axion-like particles, and anomalous gluon couplings. The most stringent limits to date are set for most of these scenarios. Quark contact interactions are excluded at 95% confidence level (CL) up to a scale of 17 (37) TeV for destructive (constructive) interference in a benchmark scenario, valid to next-to-leading order in quantum chromodynamics, and in which only left-handed quarks participate. The coupling of axion-like particles to the gluon, $c_{\text{g}}/f_{\text{a}}$, is constrained to be lower than 0.42 TeV$^{-1}$ at 95% CL. The anomalous triple-gluon coupling, $C_{\text{G}}/Λ^2$, in a standard model effective field theory is constrained to be lower than 0.0076 TeV$^{-2}$ at 95% CL.

### [179] [Amplitude analysis and branching fraction measurement of the decay $D^0 \to K^+K^-π^0π^0$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25649)
*BESIII Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 首次对单卡比博压低衰变 $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ 进行振幅分析，确定了不同中间过程的相对幅度和相位。测量了该衰变的绝对分支比，发现主导过程为 $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+K^{*}(892)^-$，且该过程以S波为主。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在首次对单卡比博压低（singly Cabibbo-suppressed）衰变 $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ 进行振幅分析，以确定不同中间过程的相对幅度（relative amplitudes）和相位（phases）。此类分析有助于理解粲介子（charm meson）衰变中的强相互作用机制。

Method: 采用振幅分析（amplitude analysis）方法，利用BESIII探测器在质心能量3.773 GeV处收集的 $e^+e^-$ 对撞数据，对应积分亮度为20.3 $\rm fb^{-1}$。通过分析衰变过程的不同中间态贡献，测量了绝对分支比（absolute branching fraction）和极化分数。

Result: 测量得到 $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ 的绝对分支比。主导中间过程为 $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+K^{*}(892)^-$，其分支比为 $(2.79 \pm 0.13_{\rm{stat.}} \pm 0.11_{\rm{syst.}}) \times 10^{-3}$。振幅分析显示该衰变以S波（S-wave）为主，纵向极化分数（longitudinal polarization fraction）为 $0.468\pm0.046_{\rm{stat.}}\pm0.011_{\rm{syst.}}$。

Conclusion: 首次完成了对 $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ 衰变的振幅分析，确定了 $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+K^{*}(892)^-$ 为S波主导过程，并精确测量了其分支比和纵向极化分数。这些结果为理解粲介子衰变中的强相互作用提供了重要实验数据。

Abstract: An amplitude analysis of the singly Cabibbo-suppressed decay $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ is performed, for the first time, to determine the relative magnitudes and phases of different intermediate processes. The analysis uses $e^+e^-$ collision data collected with the BESIII detector at the center-of-mass energy 3.773~GeV corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 20.3 $\rm fb^{-1}$. The absolute branching fraction of $D^0 \to K^+ K^- π^0 π^0$ is measured to be \BF. The dominant intermediate process is $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+K^{*}(892)^-$, with a branching fraction of $(2.79 \pm 0.13_{\rm{stat.}} \pm 0.11_{\rm{syst.}}) \times 10^{-3}$. Amplitude analysis reveals that the $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+K^{*}(892)^-$ decay is S-wave dominant. The longitudinal polarization fraction of $D^0 \to K^{*}(892)^+ K^{*}(892)^-$ is measured to be $0.468\pm0.046_{\rm{stat.}}\pm0.011_{\rm{syst.}}$.

### [180] [Worldwide Reactor Neutrino Propagation to Underground Labs: Matter Effects and Flux Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25655)
*Keyu Han,Juncheng Qian,Shaomin Chen*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一个高精度预测框架，用于计算地下实验室中的反应堆中微子通量，考虑了全球反应堆运行数据、反应堆-探测器距离以及地球物质效应（MSW效应），以评估地球结构特征对反应堆中微子通量预测精度的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球中微子（geoneutrinos）作为地球物理研究的独特探针，通过探测$^{238}$U、$^{232}$Th和$^{40}$K放射性衰变产生的电子反中微子，可以揭示地球内部热源的分布。然而，商业核电站持续产生相同类型的电子反中微子，这构成了地球中微子实验中难以消除的主要背景。随着地球中微子测量和反应堆背景建模接近亚百分之一精度，即使是微小的物质诱导修正也需要定量评估。

Method: 开发了一个高精度预测框架，使用全球反应堆运行数据、反应堆-探测器距离以及中微子在地球中传播的物质效应（MSW效应）。为高效求解三味中微子MSW演化方程，在真空质量基中实现了二阶Strang分裂求解器。

Result: 在该框架内计算了反应堆中微子振荡概率，包括在一维（球对称）和三维（包含横向不均匀性）地球模型下的MSW效应，并与真空振荡情景进行比较，以评估地球结构特征对反应堆中微子通量预测精度的影响。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了一个综合预测框架，能够定量评估地球物质效应对反应堆中微子通量预测的影响，这对于提高地球中微子实验的精度和减少反应堆背景干扰具有重要意义。

Abstract: As a unique probe for geophysical research, geoneutrinos can reveal the distribution of internal heat sources in the Earth by detecting electron antineutrinos produced by the radioactive decay of $^{238}$U, $^{232}$Th, and $^{40}$K. However, commercial nuclear power plants continuously produce the same type of electron antineutrinos, which constitute a primary background difficult to eliminate in geoneutrino experiments. As geoneutrino measurements and reactor background modeling approach sub-percent precision, even small matter-induced corrections to reactor antineutrino propagation require quantitative assessment. In this paper, we develop a high-precision prediction framework for reactor neutrino fluxes at underground labs, using global reactor operating data, reactor-to-detector distances, and matter effects (MSW) on neutrino propagation through the Earth. To solve the three-flavor MSW evolution efficiently, we implement a second-order Strang-splitting solver in the vacuum mass basis. Within this framework, we have calculated the reactor neutrino oscillation probabilities, including the MSW effect under one-dimensional (spherically symmetric) and three-dimensional (including lateral inhomogeneities) Earth models, and compared them with the vacuum oscillation scenario, to assess the impact of Earth's structural features on the accuracy of reactor neutrino flux predictions.

### [181] [Permeation of hydrogen across graphdiyne: molecular dynamics vs. quantum simulations and role of membrane motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24827)
*Mateo Rodríguez,José Campos-Martínez,Marta I. Hernández*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过量子力学计算和分子动力学模拟，评估了石墨炔（graphdiyne）膜在氢气分离过程中量子效应的作用，发现虽然量子效应显著，但分子动力学模拟能合理再现温度依赖性，且量子修正提供了渗透率的置信区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究显示石墨炔（graphdiyne, GDY）是分离气体混合物中小分子的理想二维膜，但当轻分子（如H₂）通过亚纳米孔时，量子效应可能在渗透动力学中起重要作用。本研究旨在评估经典动力学方法在此类问题中的适用性。

Method: 采用严格的量子力学计算和等效的分子动力学（MD）模拟，研究H₂分子通过静态GDY膜的传输过程。力场基于改进的Lennard-Jones公式，参数通过精确的从头算（ab initio）计算优化。同时使用Feynman-Hibbs有效势进行量子修正。

Result: 在250-350K温度范围内，量子效应仍然显著，但MD模拟能合理再现量子渗透率随温度的变化关系。经Feynman-Hibbs量子修正的MD渗透率提供了量子渗透率的下限，而纯经典模拟给出上限，从而确定了渗透结果的置信区间。考虑GDY层热运动时，渗透率增强，因为膜原子振动显著降低了渗透势垒。

Conclusion: 虽然量子效应在轻分子渗透过程中显著，但分子动力学模拟结合量子修正能提供可靠的渗透率估计范围。更重要的是，模拟膜的热运动对于准确预测气体传输特性至关重要，因为膜振动能显著降低渗透势垒。

Abstract: Previous research based on electronic structure calculations and molecular dynamics (MD) simulations have demonstrated that graphdiyne (GDY) is a very suitable two-dimensional membrane for the separation of small molecules in a gas mixture of different species. However, quantum effects may play a role in the dynamics of these permeation processes when light molecules are the ones involved in the crossing of the GDY subnanometric pores. In this work we report rigorous quantum-mechanical calculations together with equivalent MD simulations of the transport of H2 molecules through a static GDY membrane, as a case study for the validity of the application to these problems of classical dynamics. The force fields employed are based on an improved Lennard-Jones formulation, with parameters optimized by means of accurate ab initio calculations. It is found that, although quantum effects are still significant at the temperatures of interest (between 250 and 350 K), MD simulations are able to reasonably reproduce the dependence of the quantum permeances with the temperature. Moreover, MD permeances computed with quantum corrections through Feynman-Hibbs effective potentials provide a lower bound to quantum permeances, while the pure classical counterpart gives an upper bound, thus leading to a well delimited range of confidence of the permeation results. Furthermore, within MD simulations it is possible to incorporate the thermal motion of the GDY layer and in this situation it is observed an enhancement of the permeances with respect to the fixed membrane case, due to a significant reduction of the permeation barriers when the GDY atoms are allowed to vibrate. It seems apparent therefore, that modeling the membrane motion is crucial to provide reliable simulations of the gas transport features.

</details>


### [182] [Implementation of the multigrid Gaussian-Plane-Wave algorithm with GPU acceleration in PySCF](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24881)
*Rui Li,Xing Zhang,Qiming Sun,Yuanheng Wang,Junjie Yang,Garnet Kin-Lic Chan*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文介绍了一种GPU加速的多网格高斯-平面波密度拟合（FFTDF）方法，用于Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论中的高效Fock矩阵构建和核梯度计算，在PySCF的GPU4PySCF模块中实现，相比CPU实现获得了最高25倍的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在开发高效的GPU加速方法，以解决Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论（Kohn-Sham density functional theory）中Fock矩阵构建和核梯度（nuclear gradient）计算的计算瓶颈问题，为从头算分子动力学（ab initio molecular dynamics）和高通量计算提供基础。

Method: 采用GPU加速的多网格高斯-平面波密度拟合（GPU-accelerated multigrid Gaussian-Plane-Wave density fitting, FFTDF）方法，通过CUDA内核实现基于网格的并行化策略来收缩高斯基函数对（Gaussian basis function pairs），并在NVIDIA GPU上达到FP64峰值性能的80%。

Result: 该方法对高达f壳层（f-shell）的高角动量函数保持了效率，在包含1536个原子和20480个基函数的分子和固体基准测试中，H100 GPU相比28核共享内存节点的CPU实现获得了最高25倍的加速。对于256个水分子团簇，单块H100 GPU可在约30秒内完成基态能量和核梯度计算。

Conclusion: 该实现作为开源基础，为从头算分子动力学和高通量计算等多种应用提供了高效的GPU加速解决方案，显著提升了Kohn-Sham密度泛函理论计算的计算效率。

Abstract: We introduce a GPU-accelerated multigrid Gaussian-Plane-Wave density fitting (FFTDF) approach for efficient Fock builds and nuclear gradient evaluations within Kohn-Sham density functional theory, as implemented in the GPU4PySCF module of PySCF. Our CUDA kernels employ a grid-based parallelization strategy for contracting Gaussian basis function pairs and achieve up to 80% of the FP64 peak performance on NVIDIA GPUs, with no loss of efficiency for high angular momentum (up to f-shell) functions. Benchmark calculations on molecules and solids with up to 1536 atoms and 20480 basis functions show up to 25x speedup on an H100 GPU relative to the CPU implementation on a 28-core shared memory node. For a 256-water cluster, the ground-state energy and nuclear gradients can be computed in ~30 seconds on a single H100 GPU. This implementation serves as an open-source foundation for many applications, such as ab initio molecular dynamics and high-throughput calculations.

</details>


### [183] [Deep learning of committor and explainable artificial intelligence analysis for identifying reaction coordinates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25237)
*Toshifumi Mori,Kei-ichi Okazaki,Kang Kim,Nobuyuki Matubayasi*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了通过将深度学习应用于转移概率（committor）来识别复杂分子系统中反应坐标（reaction coordinate）的框架，并整合可解释人工智能（XAI）技术定量评估输入变量的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂分子系统中，表征过渡路径的反应坐标（reaction coordinate）对于理解分子机制至关重要。然而，深度学习模型通常以黑盒方式运行，难以确定哪些输入变量主导预测结果。

Method: 该框架通过将深度学习应用于转移概率（committor）来识别反应坐标，以集体变量（collective variables）作为神经网络输入，通过训练网络以转移概率为学习目标来预测反应坐标。同时整合可解释人工智能（eXplainable Artificial Intelligence, XAI）技术定量评估输入变量对预测的贡献。

Result: 该方法能够识别起主导作用的集体变量，并证明使用重要集体变量时转移概率在表面上的分布被明确定义的边界所分隔。可解释人工智能技术使研究者能够定量评估单个输入变量对预测的贡献。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了一种可解释的深度学习策略，用于从反应坐标中确定分子机制，适用于广泛的复杂分子系统。这种方法通过整合可解释人工智能技术，解决了深度学习模型的黑盒问题，增强了方法的透明度和可靠性。

Abstract: In complex molecular systems, the reaction coordinate (RC) that characterizes transition pathways is essential to understand underlying molecular mechanisms. This review surveys a framework for identifying the RC by applying deep learning to the committor, which provides the most reliable measure of the progress along a transition path. The inputs to the neural network are collective variables (CVs) expressed as functions of atomic coordinates of the system, and the corresponding RC is predicted as the output by training the network on the committor as the learning target. Because deep learning models typically operate in a black-box manner, it is difficult to determine which input variables govern the predictions. The incorporation of eXplainable Artificial Intelligence (XAI) techniques enables quantitative assessment of the contributions of individual input variables to the predictions. This approach allows the identification of CVs that play dominant roles and demonstrates that the committor distribution on the surface using important CVs is separated by well-defined boundaries. The framework provides an explainable deep learning strategy for assigning a molecular mechanism from the RC and is applicable to a wide range of complex molecular systems.

</details>

### [184] [Global detector network to search for high-frequency gravitational waves (GravNet): conceptual design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24645)
*Dorian Amaral,Diego Blas,Yuliia Borysenkova,Dmitry Budker,Alessandro D'Elia,Giorgio Dho,Alejandro Díaz-Morcillo,Daniele Di Gioacchino,Sebastian Ellis,Claudio Gatti,Benito Gimeno,Jordan Gué,Stefan Horodenski,Saarik Kalia,Younggeun Kim,Tom Krokotsch,Tomas Kvietkauskas,Adrián Lambíes-Asensio,Carlo Ligi,Giovanni Maccarrone,Giovanni Mazzitelli,Juan Monzó-Cabrera,José R. Navarro-Madrid,José Reina-Valero,Alessio Rettaroli,Kristof Schmieden,Tim Schneemann,Matthias Schott,Simone Tocci,Sandro Tomassini,Oleg Tretiak,Luca Visinelli,Changhao Xu*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出GravNet（全球探测器网络），一种用于搜索MHz至GHz频段高频引力波的新型实验方案。该方案基于多个地理分离的实验测量设备的同步测量，通过分析远距离探测器信号间的相关性来增强检测显著性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高频引力波（MHz至GHz频段）可能源于现代宇宙学中一些最紧迫和基本问题的相关现象。虽然引力波诱导的信号可能存在于单个探测器中，但将其与仪器或环境噪声区分极具挑战性。

Method: GravNet概念基于多个地理分离的实验测量设备的同步测量。本文特别讨论了在强磁场中运行的腔体（cavities）作为该方案的技术最成熟、实验最先进的实现方式。研究还进行了使用非超导腔体的首次演示实验。

Result: 通过分析多个远距离探测器信号间的相关性，检测显著性得到显著增强，同时能够研究引力波信号的性质和起源。演示实验为本文讨论的数据分析策略提供了基础。

Conclusion: GravNet作为高频引力波搜索的全球网络具有良好前景，本文概述了其未来发展和前景。该方案为探索高频引力波开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We propose GravNet (Global detector network to search for high-frequency gravitational waves), a novel experimental scheme enabling the search for gravitational waves in the MHz to GHz frequency range. Such high-frequency gravitational waves could arise from a variety of phenomena connected to some of the most pressing and fundamental questions in modern cosmology. The GravNet concept is based on synchronous measurements of signals from multiple experimental measurement devices operating at geographically separated locations. While gravitational-wave-induced signatures may be present in the signal of a single detector, distinguishing them from instrumental or environmental noise is highly challenging. By analyzing correlations between signals from several distant detectors, the detection significance is substantially enhanced, while simultaneously enabling studies of the nature and origin of the gravitational-wave signal. In this work, we discuss the GravNet concept specifically in the context of cavities operated in strong magnetic fields, as these currently represent the most technically mature and experimentally advanced realization of the scheme. As part of this proposal, a first demonstration experiment using a non-superconducting cavity has been performed, providing the basis for the data-analysis strategies discussed in this work. Finally, we outline the prospects and future development of GravNet as a global network for high-frequency gravitational-wave searches.

</details>


### [185] [Development of a one-dimensional position sensitive detector for Compton X-ray polarimeters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25078)
*Abhay Kumar,Santosh V. Vadawale,N. P. S. Mithun,Tanmoy Chattopadhyay,S. K. Goyal,A. R. Patel,M. Shanmugam*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 该研究开发了一种用于硬X射线偏振测量的新型探测器原型，采用两端读出NaI(Tl)闪烁体作为吸收体，通过位置敏感测量提升偏振测量灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硬X射线偏振测量（hard X-ray polarimetry）长期面临技术挑战，缺乏灵敏的偏振计限制了高能天体物理过程的理解。随着硬X射线镜面技术的发展，开发灵敏的焦平面硬X射线偏振计成为可能。

Method: 研究采用NaI(Tl)闪烁体作为吸收体，尺寸为100x20x5 mm³，两端由硅光电倍增管（SiPM）阵列以符合模式读出。通过表征探测器原型，研究能量和位置分辨率随辐照位置的变化，以及光输出特性。

Result: 两端符合读出使每个吸收体的SiPM本底降低一个数量级，显著增强了仪器的偏振测量灵敏度。研究还展示了在20-80 keV能量范围内原型探测器的初步结果。

Conclusion: 使用更快、光产额更好的闪烁体（如NaI）作为吸收体可显著提升仪器灵敏度。位置敏感探测器和吸收体通过测量相互作用位置和已知能量沉积，能提供光谱信息并减轻偏振测量中离轴事件的系统效应。

Abstract: The scientific potential of X-ray polarimetry has long been recognized, but the challenges in measuring polarization have left it largely unexplored, particularly in the hard X-ray regime. While tremendous advancement has been made in soft X-ray polarimetery, the lack of sensitive hard X-ray polarimeters and polarisation measurements continues to limit our understanding of high-energy astrophysical processes. With the development of hard X-ray mirrors, it is now possible to develop a sensitive focal plane hard X-ray polarimeter. One such effort is CXPOL, a prototype developed at PRL, India, which consists of a plastic scintillator as active scatterer readout by PMT surrounded by CsI(Tl) scintillators in cylindrical array with SiPM readout from one side. First results of the prototype have been demonstrated in 20 to 80 keV energy range. The sensitivity of the instrument can be significantly enhanced using faster and better light yield scintillator like NaI as absorbers. Further, the use of a position-sensitive scatterer and absorbers, can also provide spectroscopic information by measuring the interaction position along the length and from the known energy depositions in the detectors. Position sensitive detectors are also helpful in mitigating the systematic effects introduced by the off-axis events in the polarisation measurements. Here, we demonstrate the detection sensitivity in the 100x20x5 mm^3 NaI(Tl) scintillator absorber readout on both ends by SiPM arrays operating in co-incidence. In this work, we characterize the first prototype of this detector system and investigate the variation in energy and position resolution, and light output with irradiation position along the length of the detector. The two end readout in co-incidence also reduces the overall SiPM background per absorber by an order of magnitude, further enhancing the polarimetric sensitivity of the instrument.

</details>

### [186] [Quantifying plasticity: a network-based framework linking structure to dynamical regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25180)
*Igor Branchi*

Main category: q-bio.NC

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种基于网络的塑性（plasticity）操作化定义，将其形式化为系统规模与连接强度的比值，并发现最优塑性范围出现在临界状态（critical regime），从而将塑性转化为预测系统变化能力的量化工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 塑性是复杂系统（如大脑或生物体）的基本属性，但通常仅作为描述性概念从观察结果中推断得出。研究旨在将塑性转化为可预测的量化工具，以评估系统在变化发生前的适应能力。

Method: 采用基于网络的操作化方法，将塑性形式化为系统规模与系统元素间连接强度的比值。系统规模决定可访问状态空间的维度，而连接强度调节系统状态，从而建立理论框架分析塑性、临界状态与系统动态之间的关系。

Result: 研究发现最优塑性范围出现在中等连接强度，该平衡点与临界状态（critical regime）重合。这提供了理论基准，使有效塑性（effective plasticity）成为标准化度量单位，可用于比较不同系统的适应效能。该框架在精神病理学等领域得到验证，能够预测心理状态间的转变。

Conclusion: 塑性作为结构调谐参数驱动临界性，而非仅仅伴随其发生。该网络操作化解释了较大系统如何更稳健地维持临界动态，并区分了功能状态转变与热力学相变。框架适用于生态学、经济学和社会系统等多个领域，促进复杂性科学的跨学科整合。

Abstract: Plasticity is a fundamental property of complex systems, such as the brain or an organism. Yet it typically remains a descriptive concept inferred retrospectively from observed outcomes, such as modifications in activity or morphology. Here, the network-based operationalization of plasticity is further formalized as the ratio between system size and connectivity strength among system elements. Within this framework, system size determines the dimensionality of the accessible state space, while connectivity strength tunes the system's regime. An optimal range of plasticity -- balancing capacity for change and capacity to maintain coherence -- emerges at intermediate connectivity strength. Notably, this balance coincides with the critical regime, which provides a theoretically motivated benchmark that enables a normalized unit of measure, termed effective plasticity, and comparisons of adaptive efficacy across diverse systems. Plasticity is thus transformed into a predictive tool that quantifies a system's capacity for change before it occurs. Its validity is supported across disciplines and, in particular, by evidence from psychopathology where it anticipates transitions between mental states. At a mechanistic level, plasticity acts as a structural tuning parameter for criticality, reframing their relationship as causal, with plasticity driving criticality rather than merely accompanying it. Furthermore, this network-based operationalization explains how larger systems can more robustly maintain critical dynamics. Crucially, the proposed perspective distinguishes functional regime shifts from thermodynamic phase changes, identifying plasticity as the system-level regulator that shapes and constrains the dynamic repertoire. This framework is applicable across domains, including ecology, economics, and social systems, and may foster cross-disciplinary integration within complexity science.

</details>
