### [187] [Converting vertical heat supply into horizontal motion for microtechnological pumping and autonomous waste heat recovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25626)
*Jan-Niklas Schäfer,Tillmann Carl,Kristin Kühl,Sonja Kiehren-Ehses,Jan Aurich,Georg von Freymann,Clarissa Schönecker*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种将垂直方向废热直接转换为水平流体运动的新机制，实现微环境中自主、自驱动的泵送功能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高性能计算基础设施的快速发展及其广泛应用产生了大量废热，这些废热不仅造成能源的不可持续损失，还需要超越传统热管理方案的冷却解决方案。

Method: 该方法基于结合几何对称破缺（geometric symmetry breaking）与异质热导率（heterogeneous thermal conductivities）的概念，诱导局部热毛细马兰戈尼流（thermocapillary Marangoni flows）。通过概念实现、实验验证和数值模拟进行原理验证。

Result: 实验与数值模拟的流场显示出良好的一致性，证明该方法具有可扩展性，能够在实际面积加热条件下工作。

Conclusion: 该方法为微技术应用、芯片实验室架构、被动热管理和热驱动微流体系统提供了多样化的泵送设计方案。

Abstract: The rapid advancement of high-performance computing infrastructure and its extended application produce an increasing amount of waste heat. This heat constitutes an unsustainable loss of energy as well as requires cooling solutions that transcend conventional thermal management. Here, we demonstrate a novel mechanism that converts vertical waste heat supply directly into horizontal fluid motion, enabling autonomous, self-powered pumping in microenvironments. Our approach is based on a concept that combines geometric symmetry breaking with heterogeneous thermal conductivities to induce local thermocapillary Marangoni flows. We provide an implementation of the concept as well as an experimental and numerical proof-of-concept, showing good agreement between the respective flow fields. The approach is scalable and operates under realistic areal heating conditions. It enables versatile pumping designs for microtechnological applications, lab-on-a-chip architectures, passive thermal management and heat-driven microfluidic systems.

</details>

### [188] [Particle Physics and Gravitational Waves as complementary windows on the Universe](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25578)
*Steven D. Bass,Laura Baudis,Gianfranco Bertone,Oliver Buchmueller,Babette Döbrich,Reinhard Genzel,Anne M. Green,Klaus Helbing,Michèle Heurs,Karl Jakobs,Markus Klute,Samaya Nissanke,Hiranya Peiris,Albino Perego,Stefan Pokorski,Matthias Schott,Stefano Vitale,Georg Weiglein,Jochen Weller*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文探讨了引力波（gravitational waves）与粒子物理（particle physics）在探测宇宙深层结构方面的协同作用，包括致密夸克物质（dense quark matter）、暗物质（dark matter）场景、早期宇宙相变（phase transitions）以及宇宙演化等研究领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 粒子物理和引力波为宇宙深层结构提供了互补的探测手段。引力波测量能够揭示致密夸克物质结构、不同暗物质场景，并为早期宇宙一级相变（first order phase transitions）提供灵敏度，这些研究与未来粒子对撞机实验关注的TeV能标物理密切相关。

Method: 本文采用视角文章（Perspectives article）的形式，系统探索下一代引力波测量与粒子物理实验之间的物理协同性（physics synergies）。通过分析中子星（neutron stars）和黑洞（black holes）合并产生的引力波、随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational waves backgrounds）等信号，建立与粒子物理的联系。

Result: 引力波测量能够探测早期宇宙的物理过程，包括可能达到远超对撞机能标的能量尺度。这些测量为宇宙演化与膨胀提供了新的探测手段，与电磁辐射测量形成互补。特别地，随机引力波背景对TeV能标的敏感性对未来粒子对撞机实验具有关键意义。

Conclusion: 引力波与粒子物理实验之间存在显著的协同研究机会。引力波能够深入探测早期宇宙，触及远超对撞机能标的物理过程，为理解宇宙深层结构提供了独特而互补的视角。这种跨领域的协同研究将推动对基础物理的深入理解。

Abstract: Particle physics and gravitational waves provide complementary probes of the deep structure of the Universe. Gravitational waves from the mergers of neutron stars and black holes are sensitive to the structure of dense quark matter and to different dark matter scenarios. Measurements of stochastic gravitational waves backgrounds can teach us about possible first order phase transitions in the early Universe, including providing sensitivity to the TeV scale which is of key interest to future particle collider experiments. Gravitational waves measurements will also give new probes of the evolution and expansion of the Universe, complementary to measurements with electromagnetic radiation. This Perspectives article explores the physics synergies between the science opportunities provided by next generation gravitational waves measurements and particle physics experiments. Gravitational waves can also probe deep into the early Universe reaching physics much above possible collider energies if the signals can be detected.

</details>


### [189] [Large-scale weak lensing convergence in nonlinear general relativity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24838)
*Hayley J. Macpherson*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究采用端到端非线性广义相对论框架分析弱引力透镜收敛效应，通过数值相对论模拟与广义相对论光线追踪，比较非线性计算与微扰理论预测，确认了低红移下多普勒透镜效应的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在利用端到端非线性广义相对论框架研究弱引力透镜收敛效应，通过结合数值相对论模拟与广义相对论光线追踪，系统比较非线性计算与微扰理论预测的差异。

Method: 采用数值相对论（numerical relativity）模拟大尺度结构形成，结合广义相对论光线追踪（general relativistic ray-tracing）进行端到端非线性计算，对20个合成观测者（synthetic observers）的数据与微扰理论（perturbation theory）预测进行比较。

Result: 研究确认了红移低于z∼0.6时多普勒透镜效应（Doppler lensing）的重要性；线性微扰理论预测非线性收敛的精度在3-30%范围内；较小角尺度比较大角尺度与线性理论匹配更好；差异主要低于宇宙方差（cosmic variance）水平。

Conclusion: 线性微扰理论在研究的红移和角尺度范围内能较好地预测非线性收敛效应，特别是较小角尺度表现更优，而观测到的差异主要处于宇宙方差水平以下。

Abstract: In this work we investigate the weak lensing convergence using an end-to-end nonlinear general relativistic framework. Combining numerical relativity simulations of large-scale structure formation with general relativistic ray-tracing, we compare our nonlinear calculation to the expectation based on perturbation theory for a set of 20 synthetic observers. We focus on large angular scales $\ell < 100$ across a broad range of redshifts with $0.05<z<3$. We confirm the importance of Doppler lensing for redshifts below $z\sim$0.6, as predicted by previous works. On average across our observers, linear perturbation theory predicts the nonlinear convergence to within 3-30% across all redshifts and angular scales we study. In general, we find smaller angular scales are better matched by linear theory than larger angular scales. While we cannot definitively identify the source of the discrepancy, for our particular study of redshift slices on observers' light cones the differences are mostly below the level of cosmic variance.

### [190] [Structural Analysis of a Scalar-Tensor Realization of Interacting Dark Energy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25595)
*Pradosh Keshav MV,NS Kavya,Kenath Arun*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究了一类由共形耦合标量-张量框架中密度驱动的自发对称性破缺产生的相互作用暗能量模型，通过晚期宇宙学数据约束模型参数，发现当前观测不支持与ΛCDM的统计显著差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在研究一类由密度驱动的自发对称性破缺产生的相互作用暗能量模型，探索其结构特性与观测约束。动机在于理解标量-张量实现与唯象相互作用模型之间的结构区别。

Method: 在受控绝热追踪机制下，将产生的时代依赖相互作用应用于接近ΛCDM的微扰背景中。使用晚期宇宙学数据（包括Planck 2018 CMB透镜重建、红移空间畸变和Pantheon+SH0ES超新星数据）进行约束分析。

Result: 未发现相互作用相对于ΛCDM的统计显著偏好；当前观测将模型约束在标量质量大于哈勃尺度的层级机制中。激活指数可变时保持参数空间中的扩展简并方向，固定时则消除此自由度。

Conclusion: 结果界定了对称性破缺相互作用暗能量模型的可行参数机制，并阐明了微观物理驱动的标量-张量实现与唯象相互作用模型之间的结构区别。

Abstract: We investigate a class of interacting dark energy (IDE) models arising from density-driven spontaneous symmetry breaking in a conformally coupled scalar-tensor framework. In this construction, the dark matter-scalar interaction is dynamically activated as the cosmological density evolves, and the redshift dependence of the coupling follows a logistic profile whose steepness is determined by the local curvature of the symmetry-breaking potential. Working in the controlled adiabatic tracking regime, we implement the resulting epoch-dependent interaction in a perturbative background close to $Λ$CDM and confront the model with late-time cosmological data, including Planck 2018 CMB lensing reconstruction, redshift-space distortions, and Pantheon+SH0ES supernova data. We analyze realizations in which the activation index is allowed to vary and compare them with a restricted realization in which it is fixed to the canonical quadratic minimum value, thereby probing the structural role of the activation profile. We find no statistically significant preference for interaction over $Λ$CDM; current observations constrain the model to a hierarchical regime in which the scalar remains heavier than the Hubble scale at activation and background deformations remain perturbatively small. Allowing the activation index to vary preserves an extended degeneracy direction in parameter space, whereas fixing it removes this freedom and leads to a contraction of the allowed posterior region once geometric and growth data are combined. Our results delineate the viable parameter regime of symmetry-breaking IDE and clarify the structural distinction between microphysically motivated scalar-tensor realizations and phenomenological interacting models.

</details>

### [191] [Probing picosecond depairing currents in type-II superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24711)
*E. Wang,M. Chavez-Cervantes,J. Satapathy,T. Matsuyama,G. Meier,X. Zhang,L. You,F. Marijanovic,J. B. Curtis,E. Demler,A. Cavalleri*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过皮秒电脉冲技术，成功测量了第二类超导体的本征临界电流密度（Jc*），超越了传统直流测量中因涡旋运动和自热效应导致的限制，为超导微观性质研究提供了新手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 获取第二类超导体的本征临界电流密度（Jc*）具有重要的基础研究和技术应用价值，既能探究超导微观性质，又能提高强磁场设备和电力系统中的电流极限。然而，传统直流测量得到的临界电流密度（Jc）通常低于本征极限，主要受涡旋运动和自热效应限制。

Method: 研究采用超快皮秒电脉冲技术，该技术在涡旋惯性不动的时标上与材料相互作用，能够承载高达本征退配对极限（Jc* >> Jc）的超电流。实验以NbN和YBa2Cu3O7（YBCO）分别作为s波和d波超导体的代表材料，探测其皮秒临界电流。

Result: 在NbN中，观察到皮秒退配对的尖锐起始点，其电流密度高达Jc*=2.2 Jc，这一极限与基于BCS理论的微观动力学描述相符。相反，YBCO表现出超导性随皮秒电流逐渐抑制的特征，反映了其d波对称性。

Conclusion: 该结果为超导体研究提供了超越传统输运测量的强大新探针。达到退配对电流的能力也可能为超导电子学开辟稳健的新平台。

Abstract: Accessing the intrinsic critical current density (Jc*) in type II superconductors has significant fundamental and technological potential, both as a probe of the microscopic superconducting properties and as a means to increase current limits in high magnetic field devices and in electrical power systems. Yet, the experimental critical current density in type II superconductors (Jc), when measured with DC currents, is generally lower than the intrinsic limit, mostly due to vortex motion and self-heating. Here, we show that ultrafast picosecond electrical pulses, which interact with the material on timescales over which vortices are inertially immobile, carry supercurrents up to the intrinsic depairing limit Jc* >> Jc. We probe picosecond critical currents in NbN and YBa2Cu3O7 (YBCO), as representative s-wave and d-wave superconductors, respectively. In NbN, we find a sharp onset of the picosecond depairing at a current density as large as Jc*=2.2 Jc, a limit that is well described by microscopic dynamics based on BCS theory. In contrast, YBCO exhibits a gradual suppression of superconductivity as a function of the picosecond current, reflecting its d-wave symmetry. These results offer a powerful new probe of superconductors beyond the reach of conventional transport measurements. The ability to reach the depairing current may also lead to robust new platforms for superconducting electronics.

</details>


### [192] [Geometric superfluid stiffness of Kekulé superconductivity in magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24766)
*Ke Wang,Qijin Chen,Rufus Boyack,K. Levin*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过隧道谱和超流刚度分析扭曲石墨烯超导性，发现有限动量对密度波（PDW）态能同时解释低能隧道权重和低温超流刚度的T²抑制，并预测密度或位移场调控下残余零偏导增强与低温刚度降低的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在解释扭曲石墨烯超导性中观察到的矛盾现象：显著的隧道谱低能权重与低温超流刚度的T²抑制，这两种观测从互补角度反映了同一序参量。

Method: 采用隧道谱（tunneling spectroscopy）和超流刚度（superfluid stiffness）两种互补观测手段，分析有限动量对密度波（pair-density-wave, PDW）态的理论模型，该模型与已报道的Kekulé特征一致。

Result: PDW序产生Bogoliubov费米面和有限零偏导（zero-bias conductance）；相同的无能隙准粒子也进入几何超流响应，导致低温刚度抑制在平带极限下持续存在。研究进一步预测密度或位移场调控下，增强的残余零偏导应伴随降低的低温刚度。

Conclusion: 有限动量PDW态能协调扭曲石墨烯超导性中的观测矛盾，并为隧道谱与相位刚性之间的直接实验联系提供预测性特征，即密度或位移场调控下零偏导增强与低温刚度降低的关联。

Abstract: Superconductivity in twisted graphene is probed by tunneling spectroscopy and superfluid stiffness, two observables that access the same order parameter from complementary perspectives. We show that a finite-momentum pair-density-wave (PDW) state, consistent with reported Kekulé signatures, reconciles substantial low-energy tunneling weight with an approximately $T^2$ suppression of the low-temperature superfluid stiffness. The PDW order produces a Bogoliubov Fermi surface and finite zero-bias conductance. The same gapless quasiparticles also enter the geometric superfluid response, yielding a low-temperature stiffness suppression that persists in the flat-band limit. We further predict that, under density or displacement-field tuning, enhanced residual zero-bias conductance should accompany reduced low-temperature stiffness, providing a direct experimental link between tunneling spectroscopy and phase rigidity in twisted graphene.

### [193] [Exact theory of superconductivity in a strongly correlated Fermi-arc model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.24977)
*Xianliang Zhou,Fei Yang,Miao Liu,Yin Shi,Sheng Meng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过可解模型分析欠掺杂铜氧化物超导体中费米弧（Fermi arcs）与d波超导性（d-wave superconductivity）的竞争关系，发现费米弧产生的多体效应（many-body effect）显著抑制超导转变温度Tc，并使能隙-Tc比远超平均场极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 欠掺杂铜氧化物超导体的正常态是神秘的费米弧金属（Fermi-arc metal），需要分析能同时展现费米弧和d波超导性的可解模型，以理解两者竞争机制。

Method: 采用最近提出的可解模型，该模型能清晰展现费米弧的形成机制；通过引入d波配对相互作用（d-wave pairing interaction），获得超导转变温度Tc的渐近精确解。

Result: 模型产生了随空穴掺杂（hole doping）变化的超导穹顶（superconductivity dome），与铜氧化物实验观测定性一致；解析证明费米弧产生的多体效应会额外抑制Tc，超越费米面收缩的简单预期，并使能隙-Tc比远超平均场极限。

Conclusion: 研究为理解高温超导体中费米弧物理与d波超导性的竞争提供了分析基准，揭示了费米弧多体性质对超导特性的关键影响。

Abstract: Because the normal state of underdoped cuprate superconductors is an enigmatic Fermi-arc metal, it is valuable to analyze an exactly solvable model that exhibits both Fermi arcs and $d$-wave superconductivity. Here, we focus on a recently proposed solvable model in which the emergence of Fermi arcs is especially transparent. Upon incorporating a $d$-wave pairing interaction, the model produces an asymptotically exact solution for the superconducting transition temperature $T_c$ that traces out a superconductivity dome as a function of hole doping, in qualitative agreement with experimental observations in cuprates. Crucially, we show analytically that the Fermi arcs generate an additional many-body effect that suppresses $T_c$ beyond the simple reduction expected from a shrinking Fermi surface. The many-body nature of the Fermi arcs further introduces the gap-to-$T_c$ ratio greatly surpassing the mean-field limit. These findings provide an analytic benchmark for understanding how Fermi-arc physics competes with $d$-wave superconductivity in high-$T_c$ superconductors.

</details>


### [194] [Polar, checkerboard charge order in bilayer nickelate La3Ni2O7](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25119)
*Ryo Misawa,Shunsuke Kitou,Jian-Ping Sun,Yingpeng Yu,Chihaya Koyama,Yuiga Nakamura,Taka-hisa Arima,Jin-Guang Cheng,Max Hirschberger*

TL;DR: 该研究通过同步辐射X射线衍射揭示了La₃Ni₂O₇在常压下的电荷序，这种电荷序与高压下的高温超导相竞争，为理解双层镍酸盐中的相竞争和压力诱导超导机制提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 竞争性电荷序和自旋序对于揭示非常规超导性的本质至关重要。先前研究可能忽略了La₃Ni₂O₇中重要的结构对称性破缺特征，需要更精确的实验手段来揭示其真实晶体结构和电荷有序状态。

Method: 利用同步辐射X射线衍射技术对高质量单晶样品进行研究，通过高光子通量和大动态范围探测微弱反射信号，这些信号强度比主要布拉格反射弱近四个数量级。

Result: 观测到被先前衍射研究忽略的微弱反射，证实了滑移镜面对称性破缺，导致极性晶体结构而非广泛使用的中心对称结构模型。极性由镍位点上的棋盘状电荷序结合八面体倾斜诱导，类似于双层锰氧化物。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解双层镍酸盐中的相竞争和压力诱导超导机制提供了结构基础，揭示了电荷序与超导相之间的竞争关系，对非常规超导机理研究具有重要意义。

Abstract: Competing charge and spin orders are central to uncovering the nature of unconventional superconductivity. Here we utilize synchrotron X-ray diffraction on a high-quality single crystal to reveal the charge order of La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ at ambient pressure, which competes with the high-temperature superconducting phase under pressure. Enabled by the high synchrotron photon flux and a large dynamic range, we resolve faint reflections -- nearly four orders of magnitude weaker than the main Bragg reflections -- that were overlooked in prior diffraction studies. This observation evidences a broken glide-mirror symmetry, leading to a polar crystal structure, rather than the widely used centrosymmetric structure model. The polarity is induced by checkerboard charge order on nickel sites in combination with octahedral tilting, reminiscent of bilayer manganese oxides. Our results provide a foundation for understanding phase competition and the mechanism of pressure-induced superconductivity in bilayer nickelates.

### [195] [Vortex-driven superconducting diode effect in asymmetric multilayer heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25147)
*Jiong Li,Ji Jiang,Qing-Hu Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过模拟非对称多层异质结构，揭示了超导二极管效应（SDE）的微观机制源于洛伦兹力与非对称涡旋动力学的相互作用，并发现通过改变层堆叠顺序可以完全抑制该效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导二极管效应（superconducting diode effect, SDE）因其在量子技术和节能器件中的潜在应用价值而受到广泛关注。本研究旨在探索SDE的微观机制，特别是澄清涡旋动力学（vortex dynamics）在其中所起的作用。

Method: 研究采用含时金兹堡-朗道理论（time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory）模拟非对称多层异质结构。通过系统改变由铌、钒和钽构成的三层结构中的层厚度、外磁场和堆叠顺序，以分析其影响。

Result: 模拟结果显示，显著的SDE源于洛伦兹力（Lorentz forces）与非对称涡旋动力学之间的相互作用，且该效应强烈依赖于层堆叠顺序。研究发现，仅通过改变组成层的堆叠顺序即可完全抑制SDE。

Conclusion: 这些发现为理解SDE的微观机制提供了见解，并为在实际超导器件中控制和消除SDE提供了一种可行的方法。

Abstract: The superconducting diode effect (SDE), characterized by nonreciprocal critical currents, has attracted growing attention due to its potential applications in quantum technologies and energy-efficient devices. In this work, we explore the microscopic mechanism of the SDE by simulating asymmetric multilayer heterostructures within time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau theory. We systematically vary the layer thickness, external magnetic field and stacking order in a trilayer structure composed of niobium, vanadium, and tantalum, which share a similar structure to that in the pioneering experimental work, to clarify the role of vortex dynamics. Our simulations reveal a pronounced SDE originating from the interplay of Lorentz forces and asymmetric vortex dynamics, which strongly depend on layer stacking order. Besides, by simply changing the stacking order of the constituent layers, the SDE can be entirely suppressed. These findings offer insights into the microscopic mechanisms of the SDE and provide a feasible approach for controlling and eliminating the SDE in practical superconducting devices.

</details>


### [196] [Thermal stability of pair density wave in a $d$-wave altermagnetic superconductor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25314)

Method: 采用超越平均场理论（beyond mean-field theory）的非微扰蒙特卡洛方法（non-perturbative Monte Carlo approach），研究二维d波交变磁性超导体（two-dimensional $d$-wave altermagnetic superconductor）中的有限动量超导电性（finite-momentum superconductivity）。

Result: 研究结果表明，交变磁性（altermagnetism）能够在无外磁场条件下稳定对密度波（PDW）态，并使其在有限温度下保持鲁棒的相位相干性（robust phase coherence）。

Conclusion: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）是实现热稳定对密度波（PDW）超导电性的有前景途径，研究还识别了明确的热力学和光谱特征（thermodynamic and spectroscopic signatures）。

Abstract: We study finite-momentum superconductivity in a two-dimensional $d$-wave altermagnetic superconductor using a non-perturbative Monte Carlo approach beyond mean-field theory. We show that altermagnetism stabilizes a pair density wave (PDW) state without external magnetic fields and enables its survival at finite temperatures with robust phase coherence. Our results establish altermagnetism as a promising route to realizing thermally stable PDW superconductivity and identify clear thermodynamic and spectroscopic signatures.

### [197] [Many-body Josephson diode effect in superconducting quantum interferometers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25558)
*Zelei Zhang,Jianxiong Zhai,Yi Zhang,Jiawei Yan*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于多体机制的强约瑟夫森二极管效应（JDE），通过由两个平行量子点与超导引线耦合形成的相互作用纳米SQUID实现。该效应具有分支选择性特征，正负临界电流在不同多体分支上优化，显著增强了二极管效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统约瑟夫森二极管效应（JDE）的非互易性源于单个连续演化基态内的偏斜电流-相位关系。本研究旨在探索一种基于多体机制的新型强JDE，通过分支选择性机制实现显著增强的二极管效率。

Method: 研究采用由两个平行量子点与超导引线耦合形成的相互作用纳米SQUID系统。在超导原子极限（superconducting atomic limit）下建立有效模型，并利用非局域（nonlocal）库珀对隧穿通道，该通道将两个电子束缚在不同臂上。同时通过广义原子极限框架验证了有限间隙器件的稳健性。

Result: 研究发现了一种分支选择性（branch selected）JDE机制：正负临界电流在跨越0-π相边界的不同多体分支上优化，产生了显著的二极管效率增强。非局域库珀对隧穿通道重塑了0-π边界，在参数空间中产生了明显的"二极管带"，与仅存在局域库珀对转移时获得的脆弱热点形成鲜明对比。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种基于多体机制的新型强约瑟夫森二极管效应，其分支选择性机制和非局域库珀对隧穿通道是实现高效二极管效应的关键。即使在现实的有限间隙器件中，该结论仍保持稳健，为纳米尺度超导器件设计提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose a many-body mechanism for a strong Josephson diode effect (JDE) in an interacting nanoscale SQUID formed by two parallel quantum dots coupled to superconducting leads. Unlike conventional diode behavior, where nonreciprocity originates from a skewed current-phase relation within a single, continuously evolving ground state, the JDE reported here is \emph{branch selected}: the positive and negative critical currents are optimized on different many-body branches across the $0$-$π$ phase boundary, yielding a substantial enhancement of the diode efficiency. We further show that a \emph{nonlocal} Cooper-pair tunneling channel, which binds the two electrons on different arms, is essential: it reshapes the $0$-$π$ boundary and produces a pronounced ``diode band'' in parameter space, in sharp contrast to the fragile hotspot obtained when only local Cooper-pair transfer is available. While the key physics is captured by an effective model in the superconducting atomic limit, our conclusions remain robust for realistic finite-gap devices, as demonstrated within a generalized atomic-limit framework.

</details>


### [198] [Prediction of new superconducting bilayers heterostructures using quantum confinement and proximity effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.25648)
*Giovanni A. Ummarino,Alessio Zaccone*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论分析表明，量子限域（quantum confinement）与邻近效应（proximity effect）的协同作用可显著增强双层异质结构的超导临界温度，甚至在构成材料本身非超导或弱超导的情况下诱导出超导性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度超导性（nanoscale superconductivity）的核心挑战在于理解并利用量子限域与邻近效应在实验可行的金属异质结构中的协同作用。研究旨在探索这两种效应共存的双层异质结构中的超导行为。

Method: 采用广义的Eliashberg框架，该框架同时包含了量子限域和邻近耦合效应。通过这一理论模型研究双层异质结构中两种效应的相互作用机制。

Result: 理论预测显示，量子限域与邻近效应的相互作用可显著提升超导临界温度（superconducting critical temperature）。特别地，在某些双层结构中，即使构成材料在体相状态下是非超导或弱超导的，也能诱导出超导性。

Conclusion: 量子限域双层结构（quantum-confined bilayers）被认为是工程化金属异质结构中涌现超导性（emergent superconductivity）的有前景途径。研究结果为设计新型超导材料提供了理论指导。

Abstract: A central challenge in nanoscale superconductivity is to understand and exploit the combined action of quantum confinement and proximity effects in experimentally realistic metallic heterostructures. We theoretically investigate superconducting bilayer heterostructures in which these two effects coexist. Using a generalized Eliashberg framework that incorporates both quantum confinement and proximity coupling, we show that their interplay can substantially enhance the superconducting critical temperature. In particular, the theory predicts superconductivity in selected bilayers whose constituent materials are nonsuperconducting or only weakly superconducting in the bulk. These results identify quantum-confined bilayers as a promising route to engineering emergent superconductivity in metallic heterostructures.

</details>
